=========================
A2-08: An Unfamiliar Land
=========================

Description: I am an itinerant merchant, and on my travels have seen much of
             this world.
             I wandered the Empire of Rozarria for a time, and upon coming to
             Jylland found myself uncustomarily surprised. What are these
             "Judges" that affix themselves to the clans in this land?
             They are no doubt different from the keepers of the law that I
             know-yet perhaps there is some connection?
             -Aega, Traveling Merchant
Quest Type: Investigation
Rank: 15
Appears: After completing Quest C3-06 (Grounded!) and Quest B2-05 (A Simple
         Question), and visiting Fluorgis.
Price: 300 Gil
Location: The Aldanna Range

                  Adaptability = 15

              Negotiation +1

=====================
A2-09: Moorabella Cup
=====================

Description: Clan Tourneys are Under Way!
             The next tourney will be the Moorabella Cup.
             Rules are as follows:
              -Maximum participants: 6
              -Bouts to be won: 3
             -Tourney Guild - Moorabella Branch
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes in the entry bout!
                      Defeat all foes in the elimination bout!
                      Defeat all foes in the final bout!
Forbidden: Items
           Items
           Items
Rank: 41
Appears: After completing Quest B2-16 (Pearls in the Deep), Quest A2-05
         (Graszton Cup), and visiting Graszton, during the month of Mistleaf.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Moorabella
Days: 10
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Lanista
Required Talents: Teamwork = 11
                  Adaptability = 11
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 82 Clan Points
              Teamwork +3
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 7760 Gil
        Raging Brooch

Here, you are entered into a tournament against three rival clans. You have 
to fight each clan one after another, so there is no time to rest and switch 
members in between. Additionally, you cannot use items, which shouldn't be an 
issue as long as you have a White Mage or some equivalent handy to cure your 
group. First up is the Bangaa Brotherhood, which consists of a Defender, 
Cannoneer, Gladiator, Bishop, Warrior, and Templar. The second clan is called 
the Nu Mou Nobles (Black Mage, White Mage, Arcanist, Time Mage, Illusionist, 
and Alchemist). The third and final clan to face, the Arbiters of Death, are 
comprised of a Sniper, Illusionist, Berserker, Sage, Dragoon, and Hunter.

The best approach is to take out the most dangerous enemy first, as you would 
expect. In the first battle, that would be the Gladiator and Warrior, as well 
as the Templar (his Break ability can turn your clan members to Stone). For 
the second battle with the mages, they are all a threat in their own right, 
but the White Mage needs to go first. From there, ganging up on each mage one 
at a time to defeat them will work well. You can save the Time Mage for last, 
as he doesn't have attack magicks like the others do. Now for the final 
battle, the Illusionist and Sage are the strongest attackers due to their 
magick, so concentrate on them first. You should attack the others with long-
range attacks, as they can do the same to you.

Before you kill the last enemy in each round, take a moment to heal up 
everyone since the next battle begins immediately after the current one ends. 
If you survive all three battles and come out on top, you win the tournament!


=================
A2-10: Odd Places
=================

Description: There is a well about which strange rumors always spring up
             around this time of year. They say it glows in the depth of
             night, when all lies sleeping, or that monsters not usually seen
             in these parts appear, even that there are sometimes more wells,
             or fewer. Could someone please find out the truth?
             -Typical Camoan Housewife
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Examine the wells!
Forbidden: Items
Rank: 39
Appears: After completing Quest D4-06 (Seeking the Stone) and visiting any
         town, during the month of Silversun.

Location: Camoa
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 28
                  Adaptability = 28
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 78 Clan Points
              Aptitude +2
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 9450 Gil
        Fire Sigil (x3)

In this quest, you are in an area where there are four distinct sections, 
each with its own enemies. There will be a well that you have to examine, and 
upon examination of the well, you will be warped to a new area and the quest 
will be complete. Certain wells only appear after you completed certain story 
quests, and you can only examine one well each time you accept this quest. I 
will list the requirements in order for you to access each well (you will 
have to repeat this quest numerous times to see them all).

    Upper-left (Axebeak): Must complete Quest D4-06 (Seeking the Stone).
    Upper-middle (Fire Drake): Must complete Quest D4-16 (A Request).
    Upper-right (Bomb): Must complete Quest D4-11 (Wanted: Sky Pirate Vaan).
    Bottom-left (Adamantitan): Must complete Quest D4-16 (A Request).

In the Pub at Wood Village, you will meet up with Margot. He will ask if you 
know where Dayvis is since apparently he's the one who stole the sword in 
question. Pick the second option (Galleria Deep) and you will succeed.


==========================
A2-12: The Way of the Meek
==========================

Description: Someone's after me, I'm sure of it. But why? I haven't a clue.
             I'm so very frightened.
             Please, someone - protect me! If it's gil you want, I can pay!
             -Dayvis the Meek
Quest Type: Escort
Victory Circumstance: Protect Dayvis and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Items
Rank: 15
Appears: After completing Quest B2-06 (Wanted: Gilmunto).
Price: 300 Gil
Location: The Bisga Greenlands
Days: 20
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Defender
Required Talents: Negotiation = 8
                  Teamwork = 8
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 30 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 3400 Gil
        Superior Silk Thread (x3)
        Earth Stone (x3)

Out on the cliffs, your goal is to protect Dayvis from a group of bandits 
looking to rob him. The enemies consist of an Archer, White Monk, Warrior, 
Black Mage, White Mage, and Soldier. This can be a particularly annoying 
battle due to the mages, and the White Monk's strong Air Render attack. You 
would do well to have strong attackers in this battle, especially ones that 
can attack from a distance (Black Mages for example). It would also serve you 
well to take out the White Mage as early as possible. Be careful of attacks 
on Dayvis though, since if he dies, you fail the mission!


===================
A2-13: Fluorgis Cup
===================

Description: Clan Tourneys are Under Way!
             The next tourney will be the Fluorgis Cup.
             Rules are as follows:
              -Maximum team size: 1
              -Bouts to be won: 3
             -Tourney Guild - Fluorgis Branch
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes in the entry bout!
                      Defeat all foes in the elimination bout!
                      Defeat all foes in the final bout!
Forbidden: Buffs
           Fire, Ice, Lightning
           Reaction Abilities
Rank: 24
Appears: After completing Quest C3-06 (Grounded!), Quest A2-09 (Moorabella
         Cup), and visiting Graszton, during the month of Emberleaf.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Fluorgis
Days: 10
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Gladiator
Required Talents: Teamwork = 15
                  Adaptability = 15
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 48 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 2730 Gil
        Pin of Order

In the fourth tournament cup you are participating in, you have to fight 
through three one-on-one battles. The first battle is against a Blue Mage, 
the second against a Red Mage, and the final battle against a Master Monk. 
Since you can only dispatch one clan member to fight all three of them, make 
sure it's someone who has strong attacks, a solid set of abilities, and can 
cure themselves if needed.

In the first battle, the Blue Mage has abilities which can inflict various 
status effects on you, such as Poison, Blind, and Silence, and can increase 
his own attack and magickal power. Heading into the second battle, the Red 
Mage you face will be a little more difficult, especially since she has 
Doublecast (cast two magick spells in the same turn) and Doubleshot (attack 
twice). If the person you brought into the battle can steal, you can try and 
take the Ribbon accessory from the Red Mage.

As for the third and final battle, the Master Monk, he has some strong 
abilities including Cross-counter and Withering Strike, plus all of his 
statistics are boosted from his Destroyer passive ability. This is the most 
difficult of the three battles, so keep your health up and beat down this guy 
to win the tournament! You will also receive the Pin of Order as an added 
bonus for winning.


===========================
A2-14: The Way of the Timid
===========================

Description: I've heard there are many robbers about these days, and I'd
             rather not travel alone.

When you arrive here, you will find Dayvis again, but this time he has 
tricked you into appearing so he and his clan can fight you! They consist of 
an Archer, Berserker, Soldier, Warrior, White Monk, and Thief. As usual, you 
will want to kill the White Monk first due to its Air Render and other such 
abilities. The Archer's Wallet Shot can be a drain on your finances as well, 
if you are not careful. The most elusive enemy here is the Berserker because 
of its evasion-boosting abilities; you can save him for last though. Once you 
defeat this clan, you will take back the stolen sword and the quest ends.

A2-15: Pirate Attack
====================

Description: We've received word that one of our merchant ships is being
             pursued by pirates. They're likely after her cargo of gemstones.

Late at night in Graszton, you will find the Veluga Pirates attempting to rob 
the ship at port. Of course, your clan arrives to stop them from boarding the 
ship and stealing it all. You are up against three Vikings, a Moogle Knight, 
Archer, and Black Mage. The law in place prohibits you from attacking the 
Archer and Black Mage, which is fine; Lord Grayrl the Viking is your main 
target. The Vikings can hit you with Thunder magick, so be careful! Make your 
way up the street, blocking the enemies from getting past, taking out anyone 
in your way. When you get to Grayrl, defeat him quickly and the cargo is 
saved!


=======================
A2-16: Wanted: Big Eyes
=======================

Description: -WANTED!-
             Wanted: Big Eyes, for 3 counts of the disruption of business and
             25 counts of inducing shock.
             Big Eyes possess a single large eyeball and generally travel in
             packs.
             -Jylland Defenders of the Peace
Quest Type: Headhunt
Victory Circumstance: Defeat the Big Eyes!

        Wyrm Carapace

Here, you are sent to defeat the Big Eyes, which consist of three Bloody Orbs 
and two Plagues. The smaller Bloody Orbs are nothing to really worry about 
aside from using Silence on your group; it's the Plagues that have the 
devastating attacks. They can Charm and Confuse your party, and even turn 
them into Stone, plus they can do this from a distance. You should hopefully 
have some Gold Needles handy in the event anyone in your party gets turned to 
Stone. You should really bring some magick-users to pummel them from afar, 
concentrating on the more dangerous Plagues first. The quest ends when you 
defeat them all.


===============
A3-01: Goug Cup
===============

Description: Clan Tourneys are Under Way!
             The next tourney will be the Goug Cup.
             Rules are as follows:
              -Maximum team size: 6
              -Bouts to be won: 3
             -Tourney Guild - Goug Branch
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes in the entry bout!
                      Defeat all foes in the elimination bout!
                      Defeat all foes in the final bout!
Forbidden: Grouping
           Grouping
           Grouping
Rank: 26
Appears: After completing Quest C3-16 (Sleepless Nights), Quest A2-13
         (Fluorgis Cup), and visiting any town, during the month of
         Plumfrost.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Goug
Days: 10
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Lanista
Required Talents: Teamwork = 20
                  Adaptability = 20
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 52 Clan Points
              Teamwork +3
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 2630 Gil
        Ewer of Darkness

For this tournament, you once again have to fight three clans in a row 
without any breaks in between, in order to win. The first clan, Wild Kupoon, 
consists of six Chocobo Knights (five of whom are on different colored 
Chocobos, and one without a Chocobo). The second round will pit you against 
Violene, a clan of Viera (Fencer, White Mage, Sniper, Spellblade, Green Mage, 
Elementalist). The final battle in the Goug Cup is against Prima Donna 
(Fencer, Hunter, Spellblade, Raptor). As always, there are no breaks in 
between matches, so be sure to keep your clan's HP up (healing towards the 
end of each battle is ideal).

As for the battles themselves, you will have to take out the greatest threat 
early in the battle so as to make the rest of the fight easier. In the first 
battle against the Chocobo Knights, all of the Chocobos can cure each other, 
plus they each have similar attacks. The greatest threat is the Red Chocobo 
with its Choco Meteor attack, so you may want to take it down first. They are 
all weak against lightning-based attacks, so having a mage with those types 
of spells will put an end to this battle rather quickly.

For the second battle, you will certainly want to put down the White Mage 
quickly, for obvious reasons. The Elementalist has Fire Whip and the 
Spellblade has Confusion Blade, which can Disable and Confuse your clan 
members. That is not good, especially with all the strong attacks they can 
inflict upon you, so you need to defeat those two quickly as well. The Sniper 
is another threat due to her ability to instantly kill one of your clan 
members.

As for the final round in this tournament, you are up against the members of 
Prima Donna. The Spellblade clearly needs to be defeated first, since she can 
inflict Immobilize and Doom status on your allies. The Raptor can also 
Disable her target with one of her abilities, so you need to be careful here 
as well. Other than that, the Prima Donna members don't really have any 
notable attacks, so just take them out one at a time until you defeat them 
and win the tournament! You will also receive the Ewer of Darkness as a bonus 
for completing this quest.


===============================
A3-03: Wanted: The Mirage Bunny
===============================

Description: -WANTED!-
             Wanted: The Mirage Bunny, for 1,268 counts of footpadery and
             4,232 counts of eating and running.
             Small in size, adorable in aspect, and quick to flee the scene
             of the crime.
             -Jylland Defenders of the Peace
Quest Type: Headhunt
Victory Circumstance: Defeat the Mirage Bunny!
Forbidden: Instruments and Books
Rank: 19
Appears: After completing Quest B2-16 (Pearls in the Deep) and reading the
         Notice "Wielders of the Cannon" in the Pub.
Price: 300 Gil
Location: The Galleria Deep
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 11
                  Adaptability = 11
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 38 Clan Points
              Aptitude +1
              Teamwork +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 5710 Gil
        Pagoda Wood (x5)

Here in the caverns, you will indeed find the Mirage Bunny (a Hoppy Bunny), 
as well as other monsters accompanying it (Red Marshmallow, Yellow Jelly, 
Fire Drake, Thunder Drake, Headless). The Mirage Bunny is your target, so you 
don't need to worry about killing the others. The mark itself has an Illude 
ability which can Charm your party, so be careful of that. Also, the 
elemental enemies (Flans and Drakes) can heal each other with their 
respective spells while hurting you if you're too close, so watch out! The 
Headless can be quite powerful attackers; try to take them out from a 
distance. As for your main target, use fire-based attacks to quickly bring it 
down. When it's at critical health, it becomes Invisible, which raises its 
evasion quite a bit. You will want to kill the Mirage Bunny quickly, since 
new enemies WILL appear in the area until you do! How's that for motivation?


===============
A3-05: Loar Cup
===============

Description: Clan Tourneys are Under Way!
             The next tourney will be the Loar Cup.
             Rules are as follows:
              -Maximum team size: 6
              -Bouts to be won: 5
             -Tourney Guild - Jylland Branch
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes in the entry bout!
                      Defeat all foes in the second bout!
                      Defeat all foes in the third bout!
                      Defeat all foes in the elimination bout!
                      Defeat all foes in the final bout!
Forbidden: Using MP
           Actions by Viera
           Items
           < 50 Damage
           Targeting Distant Units
Rank: 34
Appears: After completing Quest D4-06 (Seeking the Stone), Quest A3-01 (Goug
         Cup), and visiting any town, during the month of Skyfrost. You must
         be in Targ Wood, Camoa, Graszton, or Moorabella to accept this
         quest.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Moorabella
Days: 10
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Lanista
Required Talents: Teamwork = 28
                  Adaptability = 28
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 68 Clan Points
              Teamwork +3
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 4290 Gil

For this tournament, you once again have to face several clans in succession 
without any breaks in between matches. The difference from previous 
tournaments is that there are five battles to win instead of three. The first 
battle is against the Camoa Braves (two Thieves, Warrior, Black Mage, White 
Monk). The second battle is against the Veluga Pirates (two Vikings, a Thief, 
and a Juggler). The third matchup is against the 100 Geniuses, consisting of 
a Sage, White Mage, Black Mage, and Illusionist. The Arbiters of Death 
(Sniper, Sage, Berserker, Hunter, Dragoon, Illusionist) will be your 
opponents in the fourth round. The final round puts you against House Bowen 
(Fighter, Assassin, Illusionist, Ravager).

In the first battle, your main target from the start should be the Black Mage 
given his magickal attacks, followed by the White Monk with Air Render and 
Earth Render. For the second round, the Juggler's Smile Toss (casts Quicken) 
can be most annoying, especially since the Vikings are tough and tend to 
steal items and even armor from you! They also have the Thundaga magick, 
which can hit very hard if you aren't careful. In the third battle, you will 
definitely want to defeat the Sage as quickly as possible, due to the fact he 
has both Scate and Gigaflare, which are very powerful abilities to have. The 
Illusionist is the second greatest threat since his attacks can hit your 
entire clan.

As for the fourth round of the tournament, the Illusionist is once again the 
most dangerous of the group due to her abilities. The Sniper has Doubleshot, 
which can make her attacks hurt quite a bit as well. The rest of the enemies 
in this match are strong attackers, but it's nothing you haven't seen before, 
so there isn't anything noteworthy to add. When you have only one enemy 
remaining, be sure to heal up, as you will need it for the last battle.

Speaking of the last battle, you are up against House Bowen. The most 
dangerous of the group are the Illusionist and the Assassin, since they can 
both inflict Stop status on your clan members in addition to causing lots of 
damage. Their Assassin also tends to use Vanish a lot, which means you cannot 
attack until her next action makes her visible again. That said, she will 
probably be the last one in the group you defeat. Once you defeat House 
Bowen, you will claim victory of this tournament, and receive the Ring of the 
Wheel as an added bonus!


=====================

Description: -WANTED!-

             vegetative life.
             -Jylland Defenders of the Peace

        Screamroot

You will meet Florah out here on the hill, who insists on fighting you in 
order to protect the plant enemies in the region. You are up against her (a 
Geomancer), Malboros, a Great Malboro, and a Deadly Nightshade. The Malboros 
need to go first because of their Bad Breath ability which can induce some 
nasty status effects on your party. Florah's Geomancer abilities can also hit 
you from a distance and cause some bad effects, such as Immobilize. Either 
way, you only need to defeat Florah in order to complete this quest. You may 
as well defeat the other enemies since Florah has a very high defense, and 
the enemies can get rather annoying with their abilities after a while.


======================
A3-08: Death March, II
======================

Description: -The Game Is On!-
             Wanted: Participants for the greatest game in Ivalice! This
             time, it's the second Death March. To the victor go the spoils.
             -Rules of the Game-
             *Uphold the law
             -Bronkrise Gamer's Guild
Quest Type: Uphold the Law
Victory Circumstance: Uphold the law and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Not Moving 1 Tile

                            Scholar

                  Adaptability = 15

For the second round of the Death March, you once again have to uphold the 
law in order to gain victory. You are put against a more advanced clan this 
time, consisting of a Soldier, Parivir, Juggler, Fusilier, Elementalist, and 
Trickster. The battle is much tougher this time because you can only move one 
space per turn, and all the enemies can inflict status effects on you from a 
distance. You really need to have some good long-distance attacks ready, 
especially offensive and defensive magicks if you are going to stand a 
chance. Nonetheless, once you start picking off the enemies one at a time, it 
gets much easier. Try to aim for the Parivir first, as his attacks are the 
most devastating.


==================
A3-09: Ordalia Cup
==================

Description: Clan Tourneys are Under Way!
             The next tourney will be the Ordalia Cup.
             Rules are as follows:
              -Maximum team size: 6
              -Bouts to be won: 5
             -Tourney Guild - Rozarria Branch
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes in the entry bout!
                      Defeat all foes in the second bout!
                      Defeat all foes in the third bout!
                      Defeat all foes in the elimination bout!
                      Defeat all foes in the final bout!
Forbidden: Knockback
           Buffs
           Solitude
           Not Moving
           Restoring MP
Rank: 37
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request), Quest A3-05 (Loar Cup),
         and visiting any town, during the month of Bloodfire. You must be in
         Fluorgis or Goug to accept this quest.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Fluorgis
Days: 10
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Lanista
Required Talents: Teamwork = 39
                  Adaptability = 39
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 74 Clan Points
              Teamwork +3
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 4660 Gil

In this tournament, like the Loar Cup, you have five matches to get through 
in order to win. The first match puts you against the Fyrebird clan (Dragoon, 
Black Mage, Ninja, Fighter, Summoner, and a Chocobo Knight atop a Red 
Chocobo). In the second round, you fight the Bedeviled clan (Templar, Master 
Monk, Fighter, Berserker, Ravager, Gladiator). The third round has you 
fighting the Jytras Pirata (Defender, Black Mage, Sniper, Moogle Knight, 
White Mage, Thief). For round four, you are up against Prima Donna once again 
(Fencer, Raptor, Hunter, Spellblade). Finally, the last battle has you 
fighting the Eastwatch (three Parivirs, two Ninjas, and an Assassin). There 
are no breaks between matches, but I recommend healing up towards the end of 
each battle. Also, if you have the accessory which summons Ultima equipped, 
it will make all the difference if you are taking a beating in some of these 
matches.

For the first battle, the most dangerous opponent by far is the Chocobo 
Knight with the Red Chocobo. Its Choco Meteor attack can be quite 
devastating. The Summoner has summons which can cause damage to your entire 
party, as well as the Fire Whip ability which can Disable you, so you'll want 
to go after her early on as well. The second match is mainly physical 
fighting, but the Fighter has Dual Wield which makes him even more of a 
threat. You will take quite a beating in this match, so hopefully you have a 
good person who can heal your group on board (or someone who has the 
accessory to summon Ultima equipped).

In the third battle, you need to defeat the Sniper right away due to their 
ability to cast Doom on one of your clan members instantly with the Death 
Sickle ability. The White and Black Mages need to go next, to prevent healing 
of the others and strong magick attacks from being used against you. The rest 
of the enemies are not too difficult once you get rid of the first three I 
mentioned; the Defender can take a lot of damage, so he may take the longest 
to beat. Moving to the fourth round, you should focus on defeating the 
Spellblade early on due to the status effects she can inflict (Disable, Doom, 
and Immobilize). The Raptor can be annoying later in the battle with her 
multi-target abilities, so you should go after her once the Spellblade is 
down.

Now, for the last battle, you are up against a lot of heavy hitters at once. 
Luckily for you, only one of the Ninjas has Dual Wield, but the others have 
abilities which can inflict a variety of bad status effects upon you (Confuse 
and Slow, among others). The Ninjas will be the most annoying due to their 
high evasion, and the fact that one of them can move a great distance due to 
their Ninja Tabi (which you can steal if you wanted). Defeat everyone here 
and you will be the champion of yet another tournament. You will also receive 
the Tainted Cufflink as an added bonus.


=========================
A3-10: Wanted: Tonberrion
=========================

Description: -WANTED!-
             Wanted: Tonberrion, for possession of a deadly weapon (carving
             knife) and rampant hatred.
             Must be dealt with in four rounds of battle if further losses
             are to be avoided.
             -Jylland Defenders of the Peace
Quest Type: Headhunt
Victory Circumstance: Defeat the tonberrions in 4 rounds!
Forbidden: Copycat
Rank: 23
Appears: After completing Quest C3-06 (Grounded!), reading the Notice "Our
         Hate" at the Pub, and visiting Fluorgis.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Tramdine Fens
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 15
                  Adaptability = 15
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 46 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 3190 Gil
        Low Arcana (x5)

For this headhunt battle, your target is the group of Tonberrions (three 
Tonberries, and a Tonberry King) in the area. There are three of them total, 
and you have four rounds to kill them all. If you are familiar with these 
creatures from other Final Fantasy games, they are the same here. Basically, 
they will stalk a given target until they get close enough, at which point 
they will strike with such force that you will pretty much die instantly. 
They also have a move called Karma, which causes damage based on the amount 
of enemies that particular target has killed up until this point.

All of these moves are VERY dangerous, so you will be sure to keep your 
distance from these enemies. That said, physical attacks that can hit from 
afar (Aurablast especially) are quite welcome. Flintlocks tend to do a lot of 
damage to these enemies, plus they can attack from a distance. Tonberries 
take half damage to all of the elements, which is why I didn't say to use 
magick. Basically, if you don't let them get close enough to you, you'll be 
safe the entire battle. You still need to defeat them all within four rounds 
though.


=======================
A3-11: Death March, III
=======================

Description: -The Game Is On!-
             Wanted: Participants for the greatest game in Ivalice! This
             time, it's the final Death March. To the victor go the spoils.
             -Rules of the Game-
             *Uphold the law
             -Bronkrise Gamer's Guild
Quest Type: Uphold the Law
Victory Circumstance: Uphold the law and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Not Moving 3 Tiles
Rank: 41
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request), Quest A3-08 (Death March,
         II), and visiting any town.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Graszton
Days: 20
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Sage
                            Scholar
Required Talents: Teamwork = 39
                  Adaptability = 39
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 82 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
Reward: 5030 Gil
        Gold Chalice

Here, you get to partake in the third and final Death March battle. Your 
opponents this time consist of an Assassin, Trickster, Time Mage, Ninja, 
Elementalist, and Green Mage. The greatest threat to your clan by far is the 
Assassin with her Last Breath ability (causes auto-KO). Some of the other 
enemies can inflict status effects; the Elementalist's Fire Whip is the one 
you need to be most concerned over, as it can Disable you. Your main concern 
also should be that you move exactly 3 tiles per turn. Keep this in mind, 
since if you don't, you automatically fail the quest. Once you start picking 
off the mages, the battle will get much easier; defeat them all and you will 
be the champion here!


=========================
A3-12: Wanted: Combatants
=========================

Description: We have an unexpected opening in the roster of our forthcoming
             tourney. We do not often invite outsiders, but if the tourney is

        Blood-darkened Bone

For this quest, you are asked to dispatch one of your clan members for the 
upcoming tourney. Since they are looking for someone familiar with combat, 
you would best send a good melee fighter who doesn't rely on magick or 
weapons to fight, specifically a Berserker or a White Monk. After three days, 
the quest will be a success if you sent the correct job!


==================
A3-13: Jylland Cup
==================

Description: Clan Tourneys are Under Way!
             The next tourney will be the Jylland Cup.
             Rules are as follows:
              -Maximum team size: 6
              -Bouts to be won: 7
             -Tourney Guild - Ivalice Headquarters
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes in the entry bout!
                      Defeat all foes in the second bout!
                      Defeat all foes in the third bout!
                      Defeat all foes in the fourth bout!
                      Defeat all foes in the fifth bout!
                      Defeat all foes in the elimination bout!
                      Defeat all foes in the final bout!
Forbidden: < 100 Damage
           Ranged Weapons
           HP <= 20
           Targeting All Units
           Back Attack
           Lightning
           Copycat
Rank: 41
Appears: After completing Quest E5-01 (The Dig), Quest A3-09 (Ordalia Cup),
         and visiting any town, during the month of Coppersun.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Moorabella
Days: 10
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Lanista
Required Talents: Teamwork = 44
                  Adaptability = 44
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 82 Clan Points
              Teamwork +4
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 6720 Gil
        Gift of the Judge-Sal

For this final tournament, you have to fight your way through seven matches 
without any breaks in between, in order to be the champion. The first round 
is against the Arbiters of Death (Sniper, Sage, Illusionist, Berserker, 
Hunter, Dragoon). Your second match is against the Nortyrants (Flintlock, 
Geomancer, Seer, Parivir, Trickster, Green Mage). The third battle pits you 
against the members of Prima Donna (Fencer, Hunter, Raptor, Spellblade). The 
fourth round is against the Eastwatch (three Parivirs, two Ninjas, and an 
Assassin). Round five is against the Delite Delta (White Mage, Assassin, 
Summoner). In the sixth battle, you are up against House Bowen (Fighter, 
Ravager, Assassin, Illusionist). Finally, the last battle is against Hopcroft 
(Ninja, Black Mage, Dragoon, White Mage, Arcanist, Raptor).

For the first battle, you will want to eliminate the Sage quickly due to his 
Gigaflare ability, which can inflict massive damage on your party. The 
Illusionist and Sniper should be your next targets since their attacks are 
strong and in the Illusionist's case, can hit multiple members at once. In 
the second matchup, you should defeat the Seer and Parivir first, since they 
are the strongest attackers you will face in the battle. The Green Mage will 
try to Disable and Immobilize you, so she should be taken out early on as 
well. In the third battle, you need to defeat the Spellblade first so you 
don't get hit by her status effects (Disable, Immobilize, Doom). If you have 
a Thief in your group, you can steal a Ribbon from the Raptor if you want it. 
Make sure you use special abilities to defeat the Raptor, since she cannot be 
hit with regular attacks.

For the fourth battle, you need to cut down those Parivirs quickly as they 
can become overwhelming fast with their attacks. Same thing goes for the 
Ninjas; they are fast and have high evasion, as well as Dual Wield and the 
Ninja Tabi, but you need to defeat them quickly to eliminate the threat. In 
the next battle, you should concentrate on the White Mage first, since you 
don't want your enemies to be healed after you attack. Do NOT use magick 
attacks against them, since they have auto-Reflect due to their equipment. 
The Summoner should be your second target because of her ability to cause 
lots of damage on your group. The Assassin will be the most annoying since 
she can Vanish and has high evasion.

When you are fighting against House Bowen, you should defeat the Illusionist 
first since his abilities can hit multiple people at once for a lot of 
damage, plus he can Slow or Stop your clan members. The Assassin has 
Shadowbind, which can also Stop you, but you should save her until the end 
since her constant use of the Vanish ability will make her difficult to chase 
with other enemies to deal with.

In the last battle with Hopcroft, the Ninja is a big threat with his ability 
to inflict Doom status on your clan members. The Arcanist is another one you 
need to eliminate early due to his Graviga attack (takes 50% of your health), 
as well as the Black Mage with Smile Toss along with high-level magick 
attacks. The White Mage needs to go early as well due to her Doublecast 
ability, but is not an immediate threat as the others you face are. After you 
defeat them, you will become the champions of the Jylland Cup! You will also 
receive the Gift of the Judge-Sal as an added bonus, too.


========================
A3-14: Wanted: Gaitsnipe
========================

Description: -WANTED!-
             Wanted: Gaitsnipe, for poaching offenses, and the assassination
             of notable personages.
             These cold-blooded killers are highly skilled in the use of
             ranged-weaponry.

                  Adaptability = 18

              Aptitude +1
              Teamwork +1

        Malboro Wine (x2)

For this quest, you have to defeat the Gaitsnipe clan. They are all skilled 
with long-range attacks, as advertised (Cannoneer, Sniper, Flintlock, Hunter, 
Archer, Fusilier). Of course they will hit you from afar, so you will need to 
get in close and return fire in the way of close-range attacks and magick. 
It's best to pick off the strongest ones, particularly the Cannoneer, early 
on, so as to avoid anyone dying in your group. When you defeat the entire 
crew, you win.


===========================
A3-15: Something's Dropped!
===========================

Description: One of the mooglewalkers we use for transporting goods has
             overturned! It was full of valuable gemstones, kupo! If someone
             makes off with the load, we're finished for sure! Bankruptcy,
             kupo!!! Retrieve the load as soon as you can! Save our house,
             kupo!
             -Moogle Porters
Quest Type: Item Recovery
Victory Circumstance: Gather all the gemstones!
Forbidden: Reaction Abilities
Rank: 27
Appears: After completing Quest C3-11 (Rumors Abound) and reading the Notice
         "The Kthili Surveyors" in the Pub.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Nazan Mines
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 18
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 54 Clan Points
              Aptitude +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 4820 Gil
        Tanned Beast Hide (x3)

In this cave, you are sent to recover the lost gemstones scattered about (see 
the sparkling spots on the ground). You will have to deal with two Thieves, 
two Yellow Jellies, and a Beastmaster, however. There are seven gemstones to 
recover, and new enemies appear every round, so you should be quick in 
collecting them. The Yellow Jelly enemies have the Acid ability, which can 
Slow you down, plus they can heal themselves with lightning attacks. The 
Beastmaster can also control the Yellow Jellies, which makes him a good 
target to go after early on. The Thieves are not too much of a threat, but I 
doubt you want them stealing all your items and gil either! Remember that you 
don't have to fight these enemies, though the extra loot gained won't hurt. 
The quest ends once you recover all of the gemstones.


=====================

The premise of this quest is simple: you have to find a specific monster 
every month somewhere in Jylland and engage it in battle (it will be a 
special blue "!" event on the area maps). You need to defeat it within the 
specified amount of rounds to successfully collect its tag.


=====================
A4-01: Champions' Cup
=====================

Description: Announcing a Special Champions' Cup Clan Tourney!
             The Champions' Cup pits the winners of this year's clan tourney
             with the winners of last year's tourney. Come and see the best
             of the best in desperate combat!
             -Tourney Guild - Ivalice Headquarters
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes in the Special Bout!
Forbidden: < 20 Damage
Rank: 54
Appears: After completing Quest A3-13 (Jylland Cup), completing the game and
         reloading complete game save data, during the month of Goldsun.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Fluorgis
Days: 10
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Lanista
Required Talents: Teamwork = 54
                  Adaptability = 54
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 99 Clan Points
              Teamwork +5
              Adaptability +3
Reward: 8510 Gil
        Waterwyrd Crystal

In this tournament, you only have to engage in one battle against Clan 
Centurio. They are comprised of a White Monk, Viking, Archer, White Mage, 
Soldier, and Green Mage. As with any battle with a White Mage, they should be 
your first target; even more so in this case since he can use Gigaflare to 
inflict lots of damage on your clan. The Archer can inflict Doom and Charm 
status, so you will want to go after her rather quickly as well. The Green 
Mage can use Doublecast with various status effects, so you will want to be 
careful about that, too. These guys can take quite a beating, but once you 
take out the three I mentioned, the battle will become much quicker. Once you 
defeat them and reaffirm your position as the champions, the quest will end.


=========================
A4-02: Wanted: Icicle Ark
=========================

Description: -WANTED!-
             Wanted: Icicle Ark, for encasing both a manor and its lord in

        Mysidia Alloy (x5)

Here in the desert, you are sent to defeat the Icicle Ark clan. Their clan 
consists of a Gladiator, Parivir, Illusionist, Summoner, Black Mage, and 
Scholar. Of course, the Gladiator and Parivir need to be defeated first since 
they are most powerful with their attacks, but don't forget the mages behind 
them. The Illusionist has some powerful attacks that can hit your entire clan 
from a distance, as can the Black Mage. This is especially true with the 
Summoner, who you want to kill FAST, as her summons can be quite devastating 
on your group. Once you start picking off the magick-users, you will find the 
battle to be a lot easier. Once you defeat their clan, the quest is complete.

Beastmaster and a Rocktitan. House Bowen will also be here to aid you in 
defeating the Kthili Surveyors you are up against. Bowen's group starts on 
the high ledge while you start in the lower area, which means you have to 
face the enemies head-on. Bring in some good attackers and you will be set 
here, as these enemies are horribly outnumbered and House Bowen's members 
have some moves that will destroy the enemies rather quickly!

A4-06: Wanted: Floraxion
========================

        Putrid Liquid (x2)
        Malboro Vine
        Malboro Flower (x2)

For this headhunt battle, you are to defeat a giant Rafflesia known as 
Floraxion, accompanied by two Great Malboros. The Great Malboros have their 
Bad Breath, which can inflict a variety of status effects on your party, and 
the giant Floraxion can use several attacks which inflict all sorts of status 
effects on your party. Also, there are numerous traps hiding on the terrain, 
so if you have a Ranger with Awareness, it will come in handy here. As for 
your mark, it can also shoot out a seed which causes another Malboro to 
appear in the battle. You cannot see Floraxion's HP at first, but once you 
start attacking it, you will be able to see how much it has left. Use lots of 
fire-based attacks and it will go down quickly.

=============================

             moogles-they are to be considered rude and riotous.

        Screamroot (x2)

In this battle, you are faced with the Moogle Rangers, which consists of a 
Black Mage, Moogle Knight, Juggler, Flintlock, and a Chocobo Knight on a 
White Chocobo. This isn't too bad, as long as you make sure to eliminate the 
Black Mage (the greatest threat) quickly. The Juggler can be annoying with 
its Smile Toss, which casts Quicken on its target. The Moogle Knight is 
another one to watch out for, as its physical attacks can be a bit rough 
after a while. The White Chocobo can use Choco Recharge, which refills MP, so 
if you haven't killed their Black Mage yet, this can be quite dangerous for 
you. Overall, this isn't a very hard crowd to beat, and once you do, the 
quest will be complete.


============================
A4-11: Red King of Cinquleur
============================

Description: We of Cinquleur seek battle with the strongest of warriors!
             Defeat me if you can, and you shall be rewarded!
             -Red King Ruuj of Cinquleur
Quest Type: Defeat Mark
Victory Circumstance: Defeat Red King Ruuj!
Forbidden: Fire, Ice, Lightning
Rank: 44
Appears: After completing Quest A1-16 (You Say Tomato) and visiting Camoa.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Baptiste Hill

                  Adaptability = 6
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 88 Clan Points
              Aptitude +2
              Teamwork +2
Reward: 8110 Gil
        Chocobo Skin
        Coeurl Pelt
        Sequencer

Here, you have to fight against the lone Red Mage Ruuj. The only problem 
however is that Ruuj's level is in the mid-40s, and she has Doublecast, which 
means she can cast two spells in a row for double devastation of your clan! 
You can bring your full six-person party to the fight; make sure you have 
strong attackers and magick-users who can hit from a distance so as to avoid 
Ruuj's Counter attack. She also has a Ribbon equipped, so there won't be any 
chance of landing a status ailment on her. If you are around level 25 and 
have some strong jobs (Fighters, Gladiators, Black Mages, and Sages come to 
mind), you should be in excellent shape to win. When you defeat Ruuj, you 
will receive the Sequencer blade as an added gift.

A4-14: Wanted: The Mutadragons
==============================

Description: -WANTED!-

             -Jylland Defenders of the Peace

In this battle, you are facing off against the three Mutadragons. These 
beasts are rather strong and can attack you with various elementals, 
specifically fire, ice, lightning, and holy. They cannot be affected by most 
debuffs, so don't even waste your time with them. Bring your strongest 
attackers, especially those who can attack from a distance since the enemies 
can hit you from afar as well. If you have a Thief, you can use Steal 
Accessory to try and grab the Orb of Minwu and the Empyreal Armband from the 
dragons. These dragons hit hard, so have someone on hand to heal if needed. 
Once you defeat the trio, they will retreat and the battle will end.


=============================
A4-15: Blue King of Cinquleur
=============================

Description: We of Cinquleur seek battle with the strongest of warriors!
             Defeat me if you can, and you shall be rewarded!
             -Blue King Bliu of Cinquleur
Quest Type: Defeat Mark
Victory Circumstance: Defeat Blue King Bliu!
Forbidden: Using MP
Rank: 55
Appears: After completing Quest A4-11 (Red King of Cinquleur).
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Bisga Greenlands
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 7
                  Adaptability = 7
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 99 Clan Points
              Teamwork +3
              Adaptability +3
Reward: 7810 Gil
        Platinum (x2)
        Lamia Scale (x2)
        Divariwood
        Peytral

Here, you face the Blue King Bliu in battle. He is a level 55 Blue Mage with 
some wicked abilities, including Dual Wield, Magick Frenzy, and two powerful 
Blue Magick spells. The law that's in place also puts you at a disadvantage, 
since it rules out your magick-users (unless you don't mind breaking the law 
here). It is highly recommended that you do not attempt this battle until 
your clan is at least in the level 30-35 range.

Anyway, long-range attacks are excellent, particularly Flintlocks and 
Cannoneers, Assassins and Snipers, and even strong close-range attacks from 
Ninjas (with Duel Wield) and Gladiators. If you have a Fusilier, they may be 
quite useful here as well, especially if they have Stopshot (Blue King Bliu 
is not immune to "Stop", so this can help you win without even taking 
damage).

Aside from that approach, be careful when fighting up close, since his 
Counter can hit you twice because of his two weapons. Also, the Magick Frenzy 
is a VERY dangerous move, so have items on hand to heal up whoever gets hit 
by it. When you defeat the Blue King, he will give you a Peytral as an added 
reward.


=========================
A4-16: Wanted: Woodworker
=========================

Description: My roof's about to collapse under the weight of all this snow.
             If I don't shore it up soon, that'll be the end of the whole
             thing! But the job is bigger than I can manage on my own, so I'm
             gonna need a second pair of hands to finish it up. I figure
             she'll take about five days to get squared away.
             -Bique, Retired Woodworker
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Dispatch the right person for the job!
Rank: 16
Appears: After completing Quest C3-01 (Mountain Watch) and visiting
         Moorabella.
Price: 300 Gil
Location: Moorabella
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 13
                  Adaptability = 13
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 32 Clan Points
              Negotiation +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 2520 Gil
        Rose Branch (x4)
        Quality Hide (x3)

For this quest, you have to dispatch one of your clan members to complete the 
task at hand for five days. Since this quest is looking for a woodworker to 
help fix a roof, it would be handy for the person you dispatch to be able to 
use hammers. Green Mages would be perfect for such a task, so dispatch a 
Green Mage (equip them with a hammer, too) and you should be successful.


============================
A5-01: Wanted: Magick Weapon
============================

Description: !!!Urgent Request from the Bureau of Defense!!!
             Wanted: An unmanned Magick Weapon, before it has the opportunity
             to cause further damage.
             The Weapon has four legs and attacks anything that comes within
             range. Mist readings are off the charts, preventing detailed
             study. Anyone successful in stopping it will be duly rewarded.
             -Jylland Defenders of the Peace
             -Bureau of Defense
Quest Type: Headhunt
Victory Circumstance: Defeat the Magick Weapon at all costs!
Forbidden: Items
Rank: 96
Appears: After completing Quest D5-13 (Bringer of Doom), Quest A4-14 (Wanted:
         The Mutadragons), and having Adelle master the Hilo ability
         (Chirijiraden) as a Heritor.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Aldanna Range
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 54
                  Adaptability = 54
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 99 Clan Points
              Aptitude +5
              Teamwork +5
              Adaptability +5
Reward: 24960 Gil
        Fiend's Blood

Here, you are up against probably one of the toughest single enemies in the 
game: the Magick Weapon! It is a large Upsilon monster sitting atop a hill, 
and it is at a very high level (in the 90s). Its Beguile ability can 
Charm/Doom several of your clan members at once, so you must make sure 
everyone has the proper accessories equipped to counter that (Fortune Ring, 
Ribbon, Orb of Minwu). You also want your most powerful attackers here as 
well, seeing that this thing has close to 2000 HP and can take quite a 
beating. After two rounds of battle, the Mist in the area will explode, 
causing lots of damage to your entire clan, so be ready to cure!

The Magick Weapon will use Beguile often, as well as its other attacks which 
also cause a high amount of damage. It would serve you well to be at a high 
level as well (70s at least) before taking on this beast. Having attackers 
with Dual Wield and the Ultima abilities (Ultima Masher/Charge/Sword) will 
help a LOT. Once you defeat this creature, the battle will be over!


==============================
A5-03: Green King of Cinquleur
==============================

Description: We of Cinquleur seek battle with the strongest of warriors!
             Defeat me if you can, and you shall be rewarded!
             -Green King Verre of Cinquleur
Quest Type: Defeat Mark
Victory Circumstance: Defeat Green King Verre!
Forbidden: Restoring HP
Rank: 66
Appears: After completing Quest A4-15 (Blue King of Cinquleur).
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Zedlei Forest
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 8
                  Adaptability = 8
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 99 Clan Points
              Teamwork +3
              Adaptability +3
Reward: 13090 Gil
        Strange Liquid (x2)
        Great Serpent's Fang (x2)
        Save the Queen

For this battle, you meet Green King Verre, who is of course a Green Mage at 
level 66. You should surely not attempt this battle until your party is at 
least around level 40. She has some nasty moves, including Last Breath and 
Nightmare, which can cause Doom and Sleep status, and KO your clan members. 
She can also raise her accuracy with Tranq, which increases the chances of 
such abilities working. You have a lot to deal with here, so send out your 
strongest melee and long-range attackers. Magick is USELESS in this battle 
since Green King Verre is equipped with a Mirror Mail, which causes Reflect. 
Once you manage to defeat her, she will reward you with the Save the Queen 
blade as an added reward for victory.

Description: We've begun development of a new gun, kupo! But developing and

For this quest, as with the other quests where a certain person is requested, 
you have to dispatch one of your clan members to do the job for five days. 
Since it involves using a gun, the obvious pick is sending a Fusilier for 
this quest.


==============================
A5-07: Black King of Cinquleur
==============================

Description: We of Cinquleur seek battle with the strongest of warriors,
             kupo! Defeat me if you can, kupo, and you shall be rewarded!
             -Black King Nware of Cinquleur
Quest Type: Defeat Mark
Victory Circumstance: Defeat Black King Nware!
Forbidden: Debuffs
Rank: 77
Appears: After completing Quest B2-11 (Now That's a Fire!), Quest A5-03
         (Green King of Cinquleur), and completing an auction.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Galleria Deep
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 9
                  Adaptability = 9
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 99 Clan Points
              Teamwork +4
              Adaptability +4
Reward: 9820 Gil
        Wind Sigil (x3)
        Crown Scepter

In this quest, you are up against Black King Nware, who is a level 77 Black 
Mage. His equipment makes him immune to debuffs and can absorb fire, ice, and 
lightning attacks. That being said, try to stray away from magick-users in 
this battle, in favor of melee attackers, especially long-range attackers 
like Fusiliers and Tricksters. It's also a very good idea not to attempt this 
battle until your clan is at least up to level 50. Since his only Black 
Magick spells take up more than 10 MP, you get a free turn before he can 
start attacking you. Use that time wisely to move closer and beat him down 
quickly. Keep in mind that Nware's equipment allows him to heal up from his 
magick attacks, so you will want to have attackers who can deal a lot of 
damage to make up for that. Once you manage to defeat the Black King, he will 
give you a Crown Scepter as a bonus for victory!


========================
A5-08: Wanted: Caretaker
========================

Description: I just received word that my grandmother hurt herself, kupo. She
             needs someone to take care of her, but I won't be able to go for
             another week. Will you go and see that she's all right until I
             arrive, kupo?
             -Karm
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Dispatch the right person for the job!
Rank: 16

         town.

                  Adaptability = 28

              Negotiation +1
              Adaptability +1

        Clear Sap (x3)

For this quest, you must dispatch one of your clan members for seven days. 
Since the job this time is to take care of an elderly woman, a White Mage 
Viera fits the description perfectly. It seems that a White Mage from any 
other race will not cut it, so be sure to send a Viera White Mage and you 
will succeed in this quest.


==============================
A5-11: White King of Cinquleur
==============================

Description: We of Cinquleur seek battle with the strongest of warriors!
             Defeat me if you can, and you shall be rewarded!
             -White King Blanch of Cinquleur
Quest Type: Defeat Mark
Victory Circumstance: Defeat White King Blanch!
Forbidden: Missing
Rank: 88
Appears: After completing Quest B2-16 (Pearls in the Deep), Quest A5-07
         (Black King of Cinquleur), and visiting Graszton.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Rupie Mountains
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 11
                  Adaptability = 11
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 99 Clan Points
              Teamwork +4
              Adaptability +4
Reward: 13720 Gil
        Clock Gear (x8)
        Cheer Staff

Here, you fight the last of the kings of Cinquleur, and as you would expect 
this is the toughest of them all. You should not attempt this until your clan 
is at least up to level 55 or so, seeing as the mark himself is level 88! 
White King Blanch is a White Mage, but he has Sage abilities as his secondary 
set of action commands, which means he has access to abilities like Scathe, 
Gigaflare, and Bio. To top it off, he has the Passive ability Blood Price, 
which means his magick spells use HP instead of MP, causing him to be ready 
to fight from the start! It would help a lot if you have long-range attackers 
in your party for this battle, and even close-range attackers with Dual 
Wield. This guy is going to hit you with everything he's got, so you need to 
do the same, and then some. It is actually helpful that he has Blood Price 
active, since that means his health will go down a bit each time he casts a 
spell. Regardless, you need to hit him with your strongest attacks and 
quickly so he doesn't have a chance to destroy your team with his powerful 
magick. Once you defeat the final king here, he will reward you with a Cheer 
Staff, and the quest will be over.


=====================
A5-14: The Five Kings
=====================

Description: We of Cinquleur seek battle with Clan Gully!
             -Cinquleur
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: < 200 HP
Rank: 99
Appears: After completing Quest A5-11 (White King of Cinquleur), completing
         the game and reloading complete game save data.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Aldanna Range
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 54
                  Adaptability = 54
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 99 Clan Points
              Teamwork +5
Reward: 15440 Gil
        Lightwing Crystal
        Condemner's Choker

In this battle, you have to face all five kings of Cinquleur at the same 
time! They are all at level 99, and if you thought they were tough as 
individual units, it gets many times worse when they are all together. Each 
one has its own abilities that make them individually difficult, too (Red 
Mage has Doublecast, Blue Mage has Magick Frenzy, White Mage has Sage 
abilities like Scathe and Bio, Black Mage has upper-level attack magick, 
Green Mage has abilities that can Doom/Sleep/KO you). Your first target 
should certainly be the White Mage so they cannot regain their health.

You seriously need to bring your absolute strongest attackers into this 
battle with the best equipment and accessories that summon Scions, not to 
mention Ribbons, Fortune Rings, and Ninja Tabis. The best approach is to take 
them each out one at a time; if you have the Ultima abilities (Masher, 
Charge, etc.), they will come in handy, as will the Ranger's Mirror Items, 
and certain summons (High Seraph's Plume for Ultima, Ring of Precepts for 
Zodiark though it may backfire on you). If you are feeling daring, you could 
have a Tinker try and use Red Spring in hopes it will Haste your group. 
Either way, you need to concentrate on one king at a time, since that's the 
only way you will be able to bring them down effectively. Keep your distance 
in between turns and make good use of your abilities to stay in this fight. 
Once you win, you will receive the Condemner's Choker, which allows you to 
summon Zeromus!


=====================
B1-01: A Step Further
=====================

Description: I seek someone to escort me to Targ Wood, providing protection
             as necessary. I am off to work for the Imperial League of
             Physicians in Rozarria, and I would like to visit the places
             dear to my heart one last time before I leave. Thank you.
             -Mack, Scholar at large
Quest Type: Escort
Victory Circumstance: Protect your charge and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Solitude
Rank: 19
Appears: After completing Quest D4-01 (Making Music) and Quest A1-04 (The
         Next Step), and visiting Moorabella.
Price: 300 Gil
Location: Targ Wood
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 22
                  Teamwork = 22
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 38 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
Reward: 4690 Gil
        Prime Tanned Hide (x6)

In this battle, you have to protect Mack, a Scholar, against the opposing 
clan. Your enemies consist of a Seer, Black Mage, Arcanist, Green Mage, Time 
Mage, and Scholar. The most dangerous ones of the mix are the Black Mage with 
Firaga, the Time Mage with Stop and Slow, and the Scholar with attacks that 
can hit everyone on the battlefield. The enemy's attack magicks can be quite 
brutal, and as such you will want to eliminate them from using long-range 
attacks as quickly as you can. Anyone who can use a bow or gun to attack, as 
well as magick, will be quite useful here. The Scholar you were sent to 
protect is helpful, in that he will buff your clan and heal you as needed. 
When you defeat the opposition, the quest will be complete.

B1-03: Sun-ripened Mayhem
=========================

Description: My fields are overrun with cockatrices! I need someone to save
             my tomatoes!
             I can't offer much in the way of a reward, but I'm desperate-
             those tomatoes are special!
             Oh, and cockatrices spook real easy, so don't bring a whole
             bunch of folk, or they'll just run off and hide.
             -Farmer Colt
Quest Type: Escort
Victory Circumstance: Protect the tomatoes and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Targeting All Units
Rank: 7

         during the month of Goldsun.
Price: 200 Gil
Location: Camoa
Days: 20
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Defender
Required Talents: Negotiation = 7
                  Teamwork = 7
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 14 Clan Points
Reward: 910 Gil
        Tomato Stalk (x2)
        Iron Carapace (x3)
        Bitter Sap (x4)

Here, you have to defend three tomato allies from the four Cockatrices at the 
other end of the area. They are rather weak (around Level 5), and you can 
only bring four units into the battle, which is just fine. Simply press 
forward onto the field and attack the enemies before they get a chance to 
defeat any of the tomatoes. If a tomato is killed, you will fail, so be sure 
to protect them! Luckily, they will attack the Cockatrices as well, so this 
shouldn't take too long at all.


===========================
B1-05: Beetle in a Haystack
===========================

Description: I was out walking my pet scarab beetle, Nero, and I lost him! I
             only took my eyes off him for a second, but he managed to
             scamper off somewhere. A friend of mine gave him to me before he
             moved away, and Nero's all I have to remember him by now.
             Please help me get him back! I polish him real good every day,
             so his shell really shines. Just look for something shiny on the
             ground and you should find him in no time!
             -Letty

Reward: 440 Gil
        Ball Moss
        Wind Stone (x3)
        Pointed Horn

For this battle, you will be up against two Wolves and two Axebeaks. There 
will be numerous sparkling spots on the map which you must visit and search 
for a chance to find the scarab beetle. The majority of the spots are on the 
other side of the map, which you can only access by crossing the two bridges. 
Fight your way across and check each sparkling spot until you find the scarab 
beetle, at which point the quest is over.


====================
B1-06: Wayward Drake
====================

Description: I awoke one morning to find my drake, Goud, missing without a
             trace. I haven't the slightest notion where he might have gone.
             Well, that's not entirely true. I've heard rumor that a drake
             was recently sighted in the Aldanna Range. I need someone to
             venture there and discover whether or not it is my dear Goud.
             -Mr. Grann
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Weaken Goud and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Ice
Rank: 15
Appears: After completing Quest B2-06 (Wanted: Gilmunto) and Quest B1-05
         (Beetle in a Haystack).
Price: 300 Gil
Location: The Aldanna Range
Days: 20
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Arcanist
Required Talents: Negotiation = 8
                  Adaptability = 8
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 30 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 1330 Gil
        Pointed Horn (x2)
        Dark Stone (x5)
        Dragon Bone (x2)

Out here on the mountain range, you will encounter Goud, the missing drake 
(it's the green enemy). It is a Fire Drake, and is accompanied by Thunder 
Drakes and a Werewolf. The Thunder Drakes have a habit of healing each other 
with lightning-based attacks when weak, and all of them have strong attack 
power. You only have to get your target to a HP critical state and the quest 
will end (if you have a character with Air Render, this can be quite easy). 
However, it may be useful to defeat the others if not for their extra loot.


===========================
B1-07: The White of Its Eye
===========================

Description: My pet's gone and run away again. How many times does this make?
             I've lost count! Her name's Chari, and I saved her from the
             other bloody orbs that picked on her because she was a different
             color. You'd think she'd be a little more grateful, but she just
             keeps running away. Someone help me find her! She has a
             beautiful white...coat? It should make her easy to tell apart.
             -Fes
Quest Type: Escort
Victory Circumstance: Protect Chari and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Fire, Ice, Lightning
Rank: 21
Appears: After completing Quest B2-16 (Pearls in the Deep) and Quest B1-06
         (Wayward Drake).
Price: 400 Gil
Location: The Rupie Mountains
Days: 20
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Defender
Required Talents: Negotiation = 11
                  Teamwork = 11
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 42 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 4920 Gil
        Crusite Alloy (x3)

Here, you will find three Floating Eye enemies closing in on a white Bloody 
Orb named Chari. Chari is an ally and you must protect her by defeating the 
others. The law bans usage of Fire, Ice, and Lightning (this includes weapons 
infused with those elements!), but luckily it doesn't bar Earth attacks (an 
Elementalist's Boulder Crush would be excellent as the Floating Eyes are weak 
against it). Chari will also attack, quite powerfully I might add, so all you 
have to worry about is healing it if need be. Once you kill the three 
enemies, the quest is complete.


=====================
B1-08: Flown the Coop
=====================

Description: I was taking one of the cockatrices for a walk in the Menagerie
             grounds when it flew into a frenzy and lashed out at me with its
             beak. Before I knew what had happened, it had fluttered over the
             pen fence and run away. This is the second time one of our
             monsters has gotten away from me in recent days, and if Mr.
             Grann finds out, I won't hear the end of it! I need someone to
             recover the cockatrice before anyone notices it's missing. It
             answers to the name of Okta.
             -Keeper Lloyd, Grann's Menagerie
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Weaken Okta and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Bladed Weapons
Rank: 25
Appears: After completing Quest C3-06 (Grounded!) and Quest B2-07 (The White
         of its Eye), and visiting Fluorgis.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Fluorgis
Days: 20
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Arcanist
Required Talents: Negotiation = 15
                  Adaptability = 15
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 50 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 4500 Gil
        Mind Ceffyl (x6)

Out here, you will find the group of Cockatrices, with Okta in the middle of 
it. Since they all look the same, you have to go by the names displayed when 
you highlight them. Anyway, you need to defeat the rest of the enemies and 
only weaken Okta. The Cockatrices themselves are not too difficult, but they 
can cast Haste on themselves, which can be quite annoying. Be careful when 
you make your way to the lower area to fight them, as there are several 
hidden traps along that path. If you have a Sage with Water, you can make 
quick work of these enemies. They really don't attack you that strongly, so 
you should have no issue winning here, as soon as you defeat the others and 
critically weaken Okta.

             -Must have fluffy white fur.
             -Enough to feed two.
             -To be used as an appetizer, one per serving.

The area will be full of Hoppy Bunnies (purple fur) and Dreamhares (white 
fur). The details ask for you to kill two of the Dreamhares, no more and no 
less. Ignore the rest of the enemies here. Once you have killed two 
Dreamhares, move one of your clan members next to the apprentice and talk to 
him to complete the quest.


========================
B1-11: Foodstuffs: Aroma
========================

Description: Foodstuffs needed. You will be required to catch specific
             monsters at a specific location. The details are as follows:
             -Green and uniquely aromatic.
             -Enough to feed two.
             -Boil down considerably, so two per serving.
             Too many is no good. Too few is also no good.
             -Poison Tasters Guild "The Iron Stomach"
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Procure the requested ingredients!
Forbidden: Knockback
Rank: 19
Appears: After completing Quest B2-06 (Wanted: Gilmunto) and Quest B1-10
         (Foodstuffs: Texture).
Price: 300 Gil
Location: Zedlei Forest
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 8
                  Adaptability = 8
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 38 Clan Points
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 2800 Gil
        Crusader Tonic (x2)
        Waltwood (x3)
        Kempas (x2)

This time, the area will be filled with Malboros, Deadly Nightshades and 
Alraunes. As was the case in the previous Foodstuffs quest, you have to 
defeat enemies to gather ingredients for the apprentice standing watch. In 
this case, you need to kill four Malboros (no more, no less), and talk to the 
apprentice after you have done that. While there are other enemies that 
appear, you can kill them for the added loot and to increase the odds of 
another Malboro appearing on the field. All of the enemies this time are very 
annoying with the adverse status effects on your clan. The fact that finding 
and killing the Malboros may take a while causes this quest to be even more 
annoying since you have to deal with way too many Alraunes as well. As soon 
as you kill the right amount, go talk to the apprentice and get out of here!


=============================
B1-12: Foodstuffs: Appearance
=============================

Description: Foodstuffs needed. You will be required to catch specific
             monsters at a specific location. The details are as follows:
             -Must be yellow and lustrous.
             -Enough to feed nine.
             -One is enough for three servings.
             Too many is no good. Too few is also no good.
             -Poison Tasters Guild "The Iron Stomach"
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Procure the requested ingredients!
Forbidden: Fire, Ice, Lightning
Rank: 29
Appears: After completing Quest C3-11 (Rumors Abound) and Quest B1-11
         (Foodstuffs: Aroma).
Price: 400 Gil
Location: The Bisga Greenlands
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 18
                  Adaptability = 18
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 58 Clan Points
              Aptitude +1
Reward: 5920 Gil
        Waterwyrd Crystal

For this quest, you will be up against an assortment of Flans. The ones you 
need are the Yellow Jelly enemies, though. It's obvious that only one is on 
the map when you start the quest, but as you defeat enemies, new ones will 
appear. Keep in mind you only need to kill three Yellow Jellies, but you can 
kill as many of the others as you want (to cycle the respawns a bit more 
quickly). Keep an eye on your party's health, since these monsters cast 
magick in their own elements, healing themselves and hurting you. As soon as 
you kill three Yellow Jellies, move next to the apprentice and talk to him to 
end the quest successfully.


=====================
B1-14: Our Playground
=====================

Description: Some old creeps moved in on our playground! The place with the
             cool old well! Now my old woman's sayin' it's a good opportunity
             for me to study and stuff. Can you believe it!? Someone drive
             those creeps away!
             -Obuta, Camoa Kids Leader
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Ice
Rank: 7

         month of Rosefire.
Price: 200 Gil
Location: Camoa
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 4
                  Adaptability = 4
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 14 Clan Points
Reward: 700 Gil
        Insect Husk (x2)
        Sanative Needle (x6)
        Wind Stone (x9)

Here you will meet up with the Zedlei Consortium, who are your enemies 
(Yellow Jelly, Grenade, Malboro, Berserker, and two Rangers). At this point 
in the game, they are quite weak which means you should have no trouble 
beating them with little effort. The only annoying aspect is the fact that 
the Rangers will plant traps whenever they move around, so be careful not to 
move where one was recently placed!


====================
B1-15: Mushroom Chef
====================

Description: I am a mushroom chef by trade. Know any dish with fungi in it? I
             cook it. So you can imagine why I'd want one of those fabled
             Baptiste mushrooms. Careful, though, there are poisonous
             mushrooms growing in the same place. I'm sure you'll be fine, of
             course. Just try them when you're out there and you'll know the
             difference.
             -Sawah, Mushroom Chef
Quest Type: Item Recovery
Victory Circumstance: Find a Baptiste mushroom!
Forbidden: Back Attack

         Mistleaf.
Price: 300 Gil
Location: Baptiste Hill
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 6
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 22 Clan Points
              Aptitude +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 980 Gil
        Aged Linen Thread (x3)
        Cottonflue (x4)
        Coeurl Pelt (x3)

In this area, there are six mushrooms, each with sparkling spots for you to 
taste in order to find the Baptiste mushroom. There are some enemies here 
though, including a Dreamhare, Lilith, Lamia, and Sprite. You don't have to 
fight them, but you should as you look for the mushroom. The most annoying 
enemies of course are the Lamia and Lilith, due to their ability to Charm 
your clan members. Once you find the best tasting mushroom, the quest ends.


===============
B1-16: Showdown
===============

Description: Clan Gully,
             I beg your assistance! No sooner had we succeeded in tracking
             down Klesta's demesne than Bowen disappeared!
             I fear he has gone to deal with the beast himself. We make haste
             to intercept him before it is too late, but I would ask that you
             secure for us some cloudy sap...it is a vital piece of our
             strategy for dealing with our flighty foe once and for all.
             -Tweigel of House Bowen
Quest Type: Defeat Mark
Victory Circumstance: Defeat Klesta!
Forbidden: Back Attack
Rank: 24
Appears: After completing Quest B2-16 (Pearls in the Deep) and Quest B2-03
         (Throw Down), completing the Side Quest "I Got A Bad Feeling", and
         visiting Graszton.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Targ Wood
Days: 20
Required Items: Cloudy Sap
Required Talents: Teamwork = 11
                  Adaptability = 11
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 48 Clan Points
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 3030 Gil
        Cursed Coin (x5)
        Skull (x2)
        Vampyr Fang (x2)

Klesta has returned yet again, and Bowen has chased it to its new location. 
You are sent to protect Bowen and defeat this beast once and for all, with 
House Bowen arriving just in time to help as well. Just like the previous 
attempts, go forth and attack Klesta with your strongest attackers; it has 
over 900 HP so it can take quite a beating! After you deplete it to half 
health, it will attempt to flee. At that point, you throw the Cloudy Sap at 
it, and the beast will land again. That's your chance to finish it off once 
and for all, so continue with the beatdown. Beware of Klesta's attacks as 
usual; have some items or healing magick ready in the event that you need it. 
Once you finally deplete its HP, it will die for good, making for a 
bittersweet victory for Bowen. You will also receive a Demon Feather as an 
added reward for killing Klesta.
