=================
B2-03: Throw Down
=================

Description: Clan Gully,
             We are in pursuit of an infamous monster that promises to be
             quite a handful... Would you aid us in driving this menace away?
             -Bowen of House Bowen
Quest Type: Defeat Mark
Victory Circumstance: Defeat Klesta!
Forbidden: Harming the Weak
Rank: 14
Appears: After completing Quest A1-16 (You Say Tomato), and reading the
         Notices "Klesta Comes" and "Headhunter Friese" at the Pub.
Price: 300 Gil
Location: Baptiste Hill
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 6
                  Adaptability = 6
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 28 Clan Points
              Negotiation +1
Reward: 2870 Gil
        Zingu Pearl Shell (x3)
        Adamant Alloy (x8)
        Green Liquid (x4)

Here, you meet up with House Bowen for a battle against the giant Crushatrice 
Klesta (the one from your very first battle in the game). House Bowen 
consists of a Fighter, Illusionist, Ravager, and Assassin (Veis). Don't worry 
too much about healing them, since it seems that even if they get to low HP, 
they stay at 1 (at least the Fighter and Illusionist do). As for Klesta's 
attacks, it uses Territorial Marking which can hit multiple units hard from a 
distance, so be careful. Klesta has a lot of HP, and when it gets to a 
critical level, out come the tougher moves such as Devour. Once you deplete 
its HP entirely, it will run away, ending the battle.


======================
B2-04: A Fatal Mistake
======================

Description: A local watch hired us to set traps to help them deal with their
             monster problem. Unfortunately, I set my traps in the wrong
             place.
             If word of my mistake gets out, I'll be in serious trouble.
             That's why I need someone to destroy the traps for me without
             causing a big stir.
             -Esther, New Hire
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Destroy the traps in 3 rounds!
Forbidden: Targeting All Units
Rank: 33
Appears: After completing Quest C3-06 (Grounded!) and Quest B2-08 (It's a
         Trap!), and visiting Fluorgis.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Galleria Deep
Days: 20
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Ranger
Required Talents: Negotiation = 15
                  Adaptability = 15
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 66 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
Reward: 4830 Gil
        Kalos (x4)

In this cavern, there will be eight assorted traps for you to trigger and 
destroy. There are once again enemies who insist on fighting you over it, 
believing your clan put them there in the first place. You have three rounds 
to destroy all the traps, so there's no time to fight the enemies. The yellow 
traps cause Silence, green causes 10 HP of damage, blue causes spikes to take 
1/2 your current HP, and purple causes Charm. Many of the traps can be taken 
out easily, but you need to really push to get to the ones in enemy territory 
quickly. It will get frustrating when the enemies are standing on the traps 
you need to reach, so try and beat them to it (Time Mages and Jugglers come 
in handy here).

===================

Description: While traveling through the Aldanna Range I mistakenly dropped

                  Adaptability = 8

        Zincatite (x5)

In this battle, you face up against three Baknamys and a Luchorpan, which is 
a stronger version of Baknamy. Your main focus is not the enemies, but to 
clear the eight traps set throughout the area. This time, there are two 
different kinds of traps, signified by color (yellow causes Silence, blue 
takes 1/2 your current HP). Anyway, the enemies are actually quite simple, so 
you might as well take them out quickly before going after the traps. To 
destroy the traps, you have to actually trigger them by moving onto the 
specified targets. Once you clear the last trap, your work here is done.


=========================
B2-09: Wanted: Lang Bros.
=========================

Description: -WANTED!-
             Wanted: The Lang Brothers, for the injury of 28 members of the
             Arbiters of Death, a clan to which they formerly belonged.

Out here, you are met by the Lang Brothers, who consist of an Archer, Black 
Mage, Fighter, and Thief. For such a fearsome group, they are actually not 
all that threatening. The only brother who poses a major threat is the 
Fighter with his Air Render ability. He is the also the first one you'll 
likely face up close in battle, so you can quickly dispose of him if you 
brought some strong attackers along. Even the Black Mage only has the low 
level magicks, so they shouldn't be too much for you to worry about. Once you 
defeat all four brothers, the quest ends.

When you come to Graszton, you will be asked to donate some money to the Carm 
Mercantile. You can either donate 100 Gil or 1000 Gil, or nothing at all. It 
may seem like nothing happens when you first take this quest, but if you 
retry it and donate more, you can earn some great rewards, listed below:

     10000 Gil: Elixir
     20000 Gil: Eureka Crystal
     30000 Gil: Grimoire Stone
     40000 Gil: Dark Matter
     50000 Gil: Einherjarium
     60000 Gil: Orichalcum
     70000 Gil: Demon Feather
     80000 Gil: Ribbon

==================
B3-01: Death March
==================

Description: -The Game Is On!-
             Wanted: Participants for the greatest game in Ivalice! This
             time, it's the Death March. To the victor go the spoils.
             -Rules of the Game-
             *Uphold the law
             -Bronkrise Gamer's Guild
Quest Type: Uphold the Law
Victory Circumstance: Uphold the law and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Not Moving
Rank: 23
Appears: After completing Quest E1-02 (Bonga Bugle - Silversun).
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Graszton
Days: 20
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Sage
                            Scholar
Required Talents: Teamwork = 9
                  Adaptability = 9
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 46 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
Reward: 2440 Gil
        Dipraeu Bronze (x3)

On this square battlefield, you will be facing another clan in battle (Black 
Mage, White Mage, Fencer, Thief, Soldier, White Monk). As the objective 
states, you MUST obey the law and defeat your enemies. This should be simple 
enough, since it only requires that you move every turn. If you have attacks 
that hit multiple units, this should go rather quickly. As usual, the White 
Monk is the toughest in the group with his abilities, but you will want to 
eliminate the mages early on as well for obvious reasons. However you want to 
take them on, when you win, the quest is complete.


===========================
B3-03: A Lady's Proposition
===========================

Description: I want to fight against a monster and know the thrill of battle
             for myself. Father tells me to put such thoughts from my mind,
             but I will have none of it. Will you fight alongside me? I wait
             in the Rupie Mountains.
             -Syrenead Sie Hyskaris
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Protect Syrenead and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Harming the Weak
Rank: 25
Appears: After completing Quest B2-16 (Pearls in the Deep) and visiting
         Graszton.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: The Rupie Mountains
Days: 20
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Defender
                            Arcanist
Required Talents: Negotiation = 11
                  Adaptability = 11
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 50 Clan Points
              Negotiation +1
              Teamwork +1
Reward: 4500 Gil
        Zodiac Ore (x8)
        Orichalcum

Here, you will find the Viera Syrenead on the mountain side ready to battle 
the Nagaraja at the peak. Since she is weak, you have to defend Syrenead 
while fighting this beast. The difficulties that arise here are the law, 
which prohibits attacks enemies at a lower level than you are (at this point 
in the game, you are likely stronger than the enemy, so there's possibly no 
avoiding this), and the fact you have to scale the cliffs to reach it. 
Syrenead is not clumsy, and actually stays behind to help your party rather 
than getting attacked by the wyrm. Nonetheless, make your way up the mountain 
and defeat the target to clear the quest.


=====================
B3-04: On the Rampage
=====================

Description: There's a monster on a nearby hill and, well, it's completely
             out of control! They say it lost its children, and being a
             mother I can understand how it must feel, but it's causing
             landslides right and left... I'm sorry, but could someone deal
             with it?
             -Concerned Mother
Quest Type: Defeat Mark
Victory Circumstance: Defeat the Mamatrice!
Forbidden: > 100 Damage
Rank: 22
Appears: After completing Quest C3-16 (Sleepless Nights) and Quest B2-15 (For
         the Cause).
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Moorabella
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 9
                  Adaptability = 9
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 44 Clan Points
              Negotiation +1
Reward: 2700 Gil
        Fiend's Blood (x4)

In this battle, you face a giant Mamatrice sitting atop one of the hills. It 
has plenty of HP and can hit you with its Territorial Marking and Devour 
attacks from afar. Make your way across the snowy field and engage it in 
battle using your strong melee fighters, as well as long-range magick users. 
The Mamatrice cannot move, so you will be able to get into a good position 
for this fight. After you deplete all of its HP, it will simply fly away 
defeated, leaving you with the victory.


===========================
B3-06: A Lady's Persistence
===========================

Description: Father didn't believe I defeated a wyrm in my first battle.
             Perhaps if I capture it and show it to him he will not find it
             so easy a claim to dismiss. Will you assist me? I wait in the
             Rupie Mountains.
             -Syrenead Sie Hyskaris
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Protect Syrenead and weaken the ivory wyrm!
Forbidden: Harming the Weak
Rank: 31
Appears: After completing Quest C3-11 (Rumors Abound) and Quest B3-03 (A
         Lady's Proposition).
Price: 400 Gil
Location: The Rupie Mountains
Days: 20
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Defender
                            Arcanist
Required Talents: Negotiation = 18
                  Adaptability = 18
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 62 Clan Points
              Negotiation +2
              Teamwork +2
Reward: 5740 Gil
        Mind Ceffyl (x2)

This time when you meet with Syrenead, you have to fight another Nagaraja 
wyrm. If you've been leveling up a lot prior to this quest, you may have 
trouble staying within the bounds of a law. It's not that big of a deal 
though. Anyway, you need to protect Syrenead as you scale the mountain and 
fight the mark. Its attacks can hit multiple party members, but at this point 
it's nothing you can't handle. Come with units that can move far and quickly 
(Dragoons are useful for their high Jump statistic), that way you can make it 
up the mountain side in no time flat. As for Syrenead, she does a good job 
protecting herself and your party, so you won't have to worry too much about 
her. When you get to the top, battle the wyrm until it's at a critical state, 
then Syrenead will capture it and the quest is complete.


======================
B3-08: Unfamiliar Folk
======================

Description: I saw some unfamiliar folk in the Ruins of Delgantua. It's just
             a feeling, but I don't think they're from around here. I don't
             think they're even from Jylland!
             They looked like they were planning something. ...Maybe someone
             aught inquire further?
             -Perna, Professor of Archaeology
Quest Type: Investigation
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Actions by Humes
Rank: 24
Appears: After completing Quest C3-01 (Mountain Watch) and visiting
         Moorabella.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: The Ruins of Delgantua
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 9
                  Aptitude = 9
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 48 Clan Points
              Negotiation +1
              Teamwork +1
Reward: 2940 Gil
        Four-leaf Clover (x2)
        Platinum (x3)

When you arrive in the Ruins, you will meet the unfamiliar group of people as 
advertised. They are a rather generic group, consisting of a Black Mage, two 
Archers, a Soldier, Warrior, and an Animist. They may seem generic until you 
get into the actual battle, where pretty much all of their moves can inflict 
some sort of negative status effect on your characters. You will want to get 
rid of the Black Mage first, of course, followed by the Soldier and Warrior. 
The Animist is probably the lowest threat of the group, but the others are 
the most dangerous with their status effects and self-buffs. Also worth 
noting is the fact that non-Hume characters have trouble getting across the 
water to the enemy's side, so aim for having lots of long-distance attacks 
ready for this battle.


==========================
B3-09: A Lady's Insistence
==========================

Description: The wyrm I keep at our home is well-behaved and docile, but a
             group of our neighbors have voiced complaint. Such ignorance...
             To appease them, I've resolved to cut off my poor pet's horn-
             that should make him appear less fearsome. This is easier said
             than done, however, and I shall require help.
             -Syrenead Sie Hyskaris
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Protect Syrenead and weaken the ivory wyrm!

         Lady's Persistence), and visiting any town.

                            Arcanist
Required Talents: Negotiation = 28
                  Adaptability = 28
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 60 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 8510  Gil
        Beastlord Horn (x2)

This is the third time you come to Syrenead's aid. This time, you are on a 
snowy hill and your objective is to weaken yet another Nagaraja. You have to 
make your way up the hill and weaken it to critical health in order to meet 
the requirements of Syrenead. She will buff your group as the battle goes on, 
but should she be attacked, you need to heal her. The wyrm won't really 
attack you until you get onto the hill with it, so be prepared for stronger 
attacks when you get there. The law in place prohibits regular attacking, so 
use a lot of abilities and magick to weaken this beast.


===============

                  Adaptability = 14

        Wyrmtwig (x2)

You once again meet up with the Duelhorn folks here. It is a different group 
this time, consisting of a Hunter, Warrior, Fencer, Thief, White Mage, and 
Time Mage. In such a situation, you will want to kill the White Mage first, 
especially since he has Cura this time. The Time Mage would be next, so you 
don't have to worry about your enemies being sped up. Their Warrior is quite 
strong, so you should have even stronger melee attackers ready to take him 
out. The Thief is probably the most annoying with its Moogle Lance attack, 
plus it absorbs fire attacks. Either way, once you defeat this part of the 
Duelhorn clan, the quest is over.


=======================
B3-13: Wanted: Barmaid!
=======================

Description: To assist with the Great Land Festival in Camoa, we are
             currently on the look out for attractive barmaids. During the

                  Adaptability = 3

        Knot of Rust (x6)
        Ether (x3)
        Phoenix Down (x3)

For this quest, you have to dispatch one of your clan members for 14 days. 
Since they are asking for an attractive barmaid, you would do well to send a 
female clan member, or a Viera (all-female race).


==================
B3-14: Making Port
==================

Description: There's a ship coming in to port soon I got a bad feeling about.
             The chief says the paperwork checks out-no problem. No problem
             with the paperwork? That's suspicious right there! You show me a
             seaman's shipping writ, and I'll show you a document not fit for
             feeding to a goat! Someone look into this, would you?
             -Anonymous, Graszton Port Authority
Quest Type: Investigation
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Harming the Opposite Sex
Rank: 25
Appears: After completing Quest C3-11 (Rumors Abound) and Quest B3-11
         (Duelhorn).
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Graszton
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 13
                  Aptitude = 13
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 50 Clan Points
              Negotiation +1
Reward: 4380 Gil
        Crusite Alloy (x4)

Here by the port, you finally meet the Four Commanders of the Duelhorn clan. 
They consist of a Trickster, Summoner, Arcanist, and Ninja. This battle 
really isn't as hard as you would expect, especially when you find out you 
only have to defeat one of them in order to win. The Trickster is annoying 
because he can attack with cards from a great distance, but the Summoner and 
Arcanist have magick which can hurt you a lot more. Pick a target and pummel 
it until it's defeated, and a Soldier will come and call them away so you can 
have an easy victory!


========================
B3-16: Knowing the Beast
========================

Description: Never become attached. The rules on this are clear. But it is
             not so easy to leave one who has fought so long at your side. A
             dreamhare I had ensorceled lamed its leg and lies wounded in the
             mountains near Camoa. Will you help me rescue the poor creature?
             -Ceva, Beastmaster
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Guard the bridges for 4 rounds!
Forbidden: Reaction Abilities
Rank: 6
Appears: After completing Quest A1-11 (The Yellow Wings) and visiting Camoa.
Price: 200 Gil
Location: Camoa
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 4
                  Adaptability = 4
Ability Points: 30
New Job Availability: Beastmaster
Clan Rewards: 12 Clan Points
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 830 Gil
        Danbukwood (x4)
        Skull (x3)
        Clock Gear (x5)

There is an injured Dreamhare on the battlefield being protected by a 
Beastmaster. It is on the same side of the area where your party formation 
begins. The objective is to push the enemies back so that they don't come 
across the bridges and endanger the Dreamhare. Do this by moving your units 
onto the bridges as quickly as possible, then fight the enemies and continue 
moving forward to the other side. You only have to resist the onslaught of 
enemies for four rounds (designated by timers on the top screen). Once the 
fourth round is complete, the Dreamhare will recover and the quest will be 
over. You will also learn the Beastmaster job as thanks for the help!


==========================

Description: It will be Silversun soon, and in Camoa Silversun means the

In Camoa, you will meet the petitioner, who wants someone who can perform at 
the festival. You will have to dispatch that person for ten days. Your best 
picks here in order to succeed are Jugglers and Tricksters.


==================
B4-02: Strong Lady
==================

Description: That old man dressed up as a lady was fighting, oh, and he was
             strong. Real strong! And the clan that lost got dragged off
             somewheres. I cried a little then, and he gave me a sweet. But I
             thought I should tell someone anyway.
             -Crybaby Kocott
Quest Type: Defeat Mark
Victory Circumstance: Defeat the Night Dancer!
Forbidden: Harming the Weak
Rank: 30
Appears: After completing Quest C3-16 (Sleepless Nights), Quest B2-14 (Making
         Port), and reading the Notices "Duelhorn" and "An Invitation from
         Duelhorn" at the Pub.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Camoa
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 15
                  Adaptability = 15
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 60 Clan Points
              Negotiation +2
              Teamwork +2
Reward: 5320 Gil
        Windgod Crystal
        Mythril (x4)

Here, you once again meet up with the Duelhorn group. There are White Monks, 
a Templar, Gladiator, and a Trickster to deal with here. Your primary target 
is the Trickster called the Night Dancer. Since there are three of them, and 
they are arguably the toughest, you should get rid of the White Monks first. 
Plus, they are blocking the way across to the other side! The Trickster is 
annoying with its long-distance card attacks as well; coincidentally that is 
your mark, so try and go after them quickly. The Gladiator has Bangaa Cry, 
which can cause Confuse status. This can be dangerous for your party, so try 
and keep your clan away from that enemy if possible (or have a weak clan 
member attack them if they do get confused). When you finally get across and 
defeat the Night Dancer, she will flee and the battle will be over.


=======================

Description: I love someone whom I can never have.
             The very thought haunts me each moment I draw breath. It is more

             And so I wish to quit this mortal life.

==========================
B4-04: The Goug Consortium
==========================

Description: Kupo! Some members of our department went to field-test our
             latest prototype, but they haven't returned, kupo! We need
             someone to see if they're all right. If that gun were to fall
             into the wrong hands...well, let's not think of that!
             -Goug Consortium
             -Department of Ranged Mutilation
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!

              Negotiation +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 2890 Gil
        Silver Liquid (x2)

Out here, you have to fight against a clan of Fusiliers. They wield guns, 
which means they can all attack from a distance and inflict all sorts of 
status effects. It will come in handy if you have an Elementalist in your 
party, specifically with the Fire Whip ability to disable your targets. The 
enemies are rather weak physically, so if you gang up on them, they will be 
down in no time. It's also important to have your own long-distance attacks 
as well, particularly to hit the Fusilier on the high ledges in the northeast 
area.


=======================
B4-05: Wanted: Sidekick

Description: By the archmage Lezaford and all those great men and women who

==================
B4-06: Caravan Cry
==================

Description: Bandits! Bandits in the Kthili Sands!
             Help!
             -Griv's Caravan
Quest Type: Escort
Victory Circumstance: Protect Alys the Ensorceled and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Opportunity Commands
Rank: 34
Appears: After completing Quest D4-01 (Making Music) and Quest B4-02 (Strong
         Lady), and visiting Moorabella.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Kthili Sands
Days: 20
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Defender
Required Talents: Negotiation = 18
                  Teamwork = 18
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 68 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 5410 Gil
        Four-leaf Clover (x3)
        Ancient Turtle Shell (x2)

Out here in the desert, you find Alys surrounded by a group of enemies 
(Alchemist, White Mage, Viking, two Thieves). You have to protect the 
Summoner from the enemy clan, while defeating them yourself. Your clan is 
split up at the start of the battle, but that's okay since that means you can 
approach the enemy from all angles. The Thieves will try to Immobilize you, 
as well as stealing, so watch out for them. You will want to go ahead and 
defeat the White Mage so he can't heal anyone else, as well as the Alchemist, 
who can let loose with a strong Flare attack. As for the one you are 
protecting, she can use her Scions to buff the party and help attack the 
enemies, which is a great help. Once you defeat the opposing clan, victory 
will be yours and the quest will be done.

When you get here, you will see an ill Lotice come out to greet you. When she 
asks if she is dead, answer how you wish (I picked no) and the quest will 
end.


====================
B4-08: The Eastwatch
====================

Description: Clan Gully!
             The might of your clan is renowned throughout Jylland. We have
             traveled from a land beyond where the sun rises in hopes of
             testing that might against our own. Will you face us in battle?
             -Zengen, The Eastwatch
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Summoning Scions
Rank: 25
Appears: After completing Quest C3-06 (Grounded!) and visiting Fluorgis.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Moorabella
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 15
                  Adaptability = 15
New Job Availability: Parivir
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 50 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
Reward: 3910 Gil
        Moon Ring (x5)

Here aboard a docked airship, you will meet the Eastwatch, which consists of 
two Ninjas, an Assassin, and three Parivirs. As you would expect, the Parivir 
is quite a powerful attacker, with very strong abilities that can decimate 
your clan in short time. The Ninjas don't have Duel Wield, but their various 
Veils can be a nuisance, so you'll want to put a stop to them quickly. If you 
have an Elementalist, their Fire Whip ability will be useful against the 
Parivirs, especially if the Disable status sticks. Once you defeat this 
group, you will be taught the way of the Parivir!


==========================

==========================

Description: Ngaaa!
             I'm short-handed! Don't have anyone to polish up these maces!

members for 10 days. Since the quest description is looking for someone who 
can hold a mace, your best bet is to dispatch a Green Mace and equip them 
with any mace weapon.


======================
B4-10: Aid the Serpent
======================

Description: We've been after a certain mark for some time now, but have been
             foiled in our efforts to stop it. Who better to aid us than
             everyone's favorite swords-for-hire, Clan Gully?
             Come, fight with us!
             -Clan Serpentina
Quest Type: Defeat Mark
Victory Circumstance: Defeat the mark!
Forbidden: Actions by Viera
Rank: 39
Appears: After completing Quest D4-11 (Wanted: Sky Pirate Vaan), Quest B4-06
         (Caravan Cry), completing the Side Quest "With a Smile", and
         visiting Graszton.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Ruins of Delgantua
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 22
                  Adaptability = 22
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 78 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 5320 Gil
        Adamantite (x2)

Here, you think you're fighting a mark alongside a friendly clan, but it 
turns out you are fighting Duke Snakeheart and his Duelhorn cronies instead. 
They consist of a Beastmaster, two Black Mages, a White Mage, Alchemist, and 
an Arcanist (the mark). You only have to defeat the Arcanist in order to 
clear this quest, though the other mages will surely get in your way. Your 
first target should be the White Mage so he can't cure the others, though 
killing the Black Mage and Beastmaster on the front line will prove helpful 
as well. The Alchemist and Arcanist have the most dangerous spells to unleash 
on you, particularly the Arcanist's Death ability, so you shouldn't waste 
time here fighting the others. Once you take out Snakeheart the Arcanist, the 
quest will be completed.

=========================
B4-12: To Be a Spellblade
=========================

Description: Magick and steel: two paths seemingly at odds. Yet both heed the
             spellblade and her will. One may not undertake the trial to
             become a spellblade alone, and I would have you fight at my
             side.
             -Hana, Red Mage
Quest Type: Escort
Victory Circumstance: Protect Hana and defeat 10 foes!
Forbidden: Actions by Gria
Rank: 28
Appears: After completing Quest C3-11 (Rumors Abound).
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Moorabella
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 18
                  Teamwork = 18
New Job Availability: Spellblade
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 56 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 8190 Gil
        Unpurified Ether (x2)

On this small, restrictive arena, you have to protect the Red Mage Hana from 
the enemies ahead. There are only three to start off, but more will enter as 
the battle progresses. It is an all-Viera lineup you'll be facing, so you'll 
be seeing pretty much every job a Viera can handle in this battle. Take out 
the mages as quickly as you can, especially the White Mage. Hana is quite 
useful with her Doublecast ability, in terms of attacking enemies and curing 
your party and herself. Towards the end of the battle, the Spellblade will 
appear and challenge you to battle. She has strong attacks which can put you 
to Sleep, but defeat her like the others and you will win. You will also 
learn the ways of the Spellblade as a result!


========================

members. In this case, the petitioner is looking for artillery support, which 
means Cannoneers and Flintlocks are the most appropriate choices. Send one of 
those jobs on this quest and you will succeed.


=====================
B4-14: Caravan Cry II
=====================

Description: We're under attack in Sant D'alsa Bluff from some mean-looking
             sorts. Send help, quick!
             -Pie-Thon Caravan
Quest Type: Escort
Victory Circumstance: Protect Duke Snakeheart and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Non-elemental Effects
Rank: 45
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request), Quest B4-10 (Aid the
         Serpent), and reading the Notice "Sender Unknown" at the Pub.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Sant D'alsa Bluff
Days: 20
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Defender
Required Talents: Negotiation = 28
                  Teamwork = 28
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 90 Clan Points
              Aptitude +2
Reward: 6010 Gil
        Snowcat Crystal

Over here, you have to fight another bunch of Duelhorn enemies while 
protecting none other than Duke Snakeheart, the guy you had to defeat in the 
previous quest. You are up against a Ninja, Trickster, Master Monk, and a 
Seer. The Master Monk and Seer are nothing to really be concerned over, but 
the Trickster can cause the Charm status on your clan, and the Ninja can use 
the powerful Magick Frenzy ability. Despite what the quest says, you only 
need to defeat Maquis (the Ninja) in order to complete it. So, concentrate 
all your efforts on him; despite his higher evasion statistics, you should be 
able to take him down quite easily. Once you beat him, Alys will appear and 
everyone will leave, causing you to win by default.


=======================
B4-15: Show of Strength
=======================

Description: Help! My chocobo corral's been taken over by a ruffian calling
             himself the Swordking and his band of cohorts! Problem is,
             they're good. Quite good. They claim they've never been bested!
             I cannot protect my beloved chocobos...
             Someone help me, please!
             -Yew, Chocobo Rancher
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Protect Ghi and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Targeting an Area
Rank: 33
Appears: After completing Quest D4-11 (Wanted: Sky Pirate Vaan) and Quest
         B4-11 (A Chill in the Night), and visiting Graszton.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Targ Wood
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 33
                  Adaptability = 33
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 66 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
Reward: 5670 Gil
        Windgod Crystal (x3)

When you arrive here, you will find the Swordking and his cohorts waiting for 
battle, when a Parivir named Ghi comes to challenge them. Apparently they 
have been undefeated only because they immobilize and disable their targets 
before even attacking. As for how you should go about this, bringing your 
strong attackers is a must. Your enemies consist of a Viking, Templar, and 
Defender. These guys are really nothing to be worried about; you can take the 
Templar and Defender out with little effort. The Viking, however, uses 
Thundara, so you need to be a bit more careful as that can hurt a little bit. 
You also need to keep Ghi's health up; he will break out of the Disable and 
Immobilize effects immediately when his turn comes, and his attacks are quite 
potent as well. Either way, once you defeat this trio, the Swordking will 
turn himself to stone and the battle will end.


===================
B4-16: Lord Grayrl!
===================

Description: You be wanting that rare gem of gems, the noble pearl, eh?
             Perhaps I might part with it for 10 million...no, 30 million-
             wait, 50 million! A good price, no? Bwa ha ha!
             Come to the wharf in Graszton. Bring yer money and nothing
             else...'cept maybe a few wheelbarrows to carry it in! Bwah ha!
             -Lord Grayrl, Gentleman Trader
Quest Type: Defeat Mark
Victory Circumstance: Defeat Lord Grayrl!
Forbidden: Not Moving 3 Tiles
Rank: 28
Appears: After completing Quest D4-01 (Making Music) and reading the Notice
         "Bad Clan Rising" at the Pub.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Graszton
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 22
                  Adaptability = 22
New Job Availability: Viking
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 56 Clan Points
              Negotiation +1
              Teamwork +1
Reward: 5110 Gil
        Wyvern Wing (x2)

In this battle, you get to fight against the Veluga Pirates, headed by Lord 
Grayrl. You are surrounded by them: a Thief, Juggler, and three Vikings. The 
law makes it somewhat difficult, as long as you don't forget to move exactly 
3 tiles by the end of every turn. You should take out the Juggler first, due 
to his ability to Stop your clan members. Your primary target is Lord Grayrl, 
who is on the ship, so you don't really need to worry about the two Vikings 
in the back area (although, they can cast Thundara, which will hurt a bit if 
you are not careful). The Vikings and Thief can steal from you as well, so 
that's something else to watch out for. Lord Grayrl has some pretty neat 
accessories if you have a Thief with Steal: Accessory handy, too. Either way, 
once you defeat Grayrl, the battle ends and you will learn how to use the 
Viking job as an added bonus!


=========================
B5-01: Wanted: Woodcutter
=========================

Description: The Lord of Camoa has decreed that several trees be cut from the
             nearby woods. As his personal carpenter, I will oversee your
             work as you fell the trees. The work should only take two days
             to complete.
             -Coerfantl, Carpenter

                  Adaptability = 22

              Negotiation +1
              Adaptability +1

        Lightwing Crystal (x3)
        Wyrmtwig (x2)

For this quest, you are asked to dispatch one of your clan members for two 
days. In this case, the petitioner is looking for someone to help chop down 
trees (which you would use an axe for). That being said, you should buy an 
axe and equip a job who can wield it (Vikings and Chocobo Knights, 
specifically). If you send either of those jobs properly equipped, you will 
succeed here.


==============
B5-02: Summons
==============

Description: Clan Gully!
             Exactly what is your relationship to Duelhorn? Show us. We wait
             in the Bisga Greenlands.
             -A Mysterious Organization
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!

Rank: 40

         "Duelhorn Suffers Setbacks" at the Pub.

                  Adaptability = 33

              Negotiation +2
              Teamwork +2

For this battle, you are in the mountains, and have to deploy your clan in 
the top and bottom areas. You are up against members of Khamja here, 
including a Tinker, White Mage, Black Mage, Soldier, and Master Monk. The 
Black Mage and Master Monk are on the bottom, so you want your best attackers 
down there, while you send a support group to take out the White Mage and 
Tinker at the top. It helps a lot if your attackers can do so from a 
distance, so as to avoid magickal attacks when possible. The Master Monk and 
Soldier have powerful physical attacks, so be prepared to heal as well. Alys 
of Duelhorn (a Summoner) will be here to aid you as well, and her summons 
will be helpful in the battle. Try to take out the Black Mage and Master Monk 
first, then worry about the less threatening enemies above. Once you defeat 
them all, the quest will be complete.


=============
B5-03: Hunted
=============

Description: A fiend hunts me. Each time I think I've slain it, I turn to
             find it stalking me once more. I fear I am lost. I seek help in
             ending my nightmare once and for all. I never want to look on
             this creature again.
             -Scared Sleepless
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Protect Frimelda and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Ranged Weapons
Rank: 39
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request) and Quest B4-15 (Show of
         Strength), and visiting any town.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Aisenfield
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 39
                  Adaptability = 39
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 78 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 7370 Gil
        Firebird Crystal (x2)
        The Fallen Angel
        High Seraph's Plume

When you arrive here, you will find the zombie Frimelda in the area, as well 
as Luc Sardarc, her old lover. He wants to kill this "monster" but you won't 
let it happen, so he fights you. The battle is only between him, and your 
three main characters (Luso, Cid, Adelle). The Paladin you must fight has 
some strong holy-based attacks, so you really need to protect Frimelda from 
them. He has high evasion and defense, plus Blink Counter which will knock 
you back with a counter-attack if you are next to him. Attack from behind and 
with magick if possible; if you can use the Elementalist's Fire Whip to 
Disable him, it will help a lot. Once you beat him, Luc will leave and 
Frimelda will give you her sword, The Fallen Angel, as well as a High 
Seraph's Plume, as thanks.


=============================
B5-04: Geomancer's Way - Snow
=============================

Description: Geomancers bend nature to their will.
             Our society has established a series of trials for prospective
             geomancers to determine whether they are worthy to share in our
             knowledge.
             The Trial of Rivening Snow is the third trial. You have traveled
             far, but your journey is not yet complete. Come when you are
             prepared.
             -Naturalist Society
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Using >= 20 MP
Rank: 37
Appears: After completing Quest C5-01 (Geomancer's Way - Rain).
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Moorabella
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 33
                  Adaptability = 33
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 74 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
Reward: 4730 Gil
        Stradivari

For this third trial, you are in a snowy area fighting against the three 
Geomancers, as well as an Ice Drake and a powerful Zahak. As you would 
expect, the Geomancers have an Avalanche attack which can hurt your allies 
and even put them to sleep, so watch out for that. The Ice Drake also tends 
to use ice-based attacks to heal itself and hurt you, so use fire-based moves 
to defeat it quickly. As for the Zahak, it is very strong and tends to buff 
itself before joining the battle, so worry about the other enemies first. Be 
careful when you do fight it, since the Zahak's attacks are very powerful. 
After you defeat the entire opposition, the trial ends and there is one left!


========================
B5-05: Wanted: Assistant
========================

Description: I need an assistant to assist me in the laboratory with my
             research, kupo. But not the dangerous kind of assisting with
             explosions and fires, kupo. Oh no. I'll only need you for seven
             days, and you'll only be required to work a mere eight hours
             each day. I'll provide your lunch and afternoon tea, as well as
             colognes and perfumes to help mask the smell, kupo!

              Negotiation +1
              Adaptability +1

        Snowcat Crystal

For this quest, you have to once again dispatch one of your clan members to 
complete a task. The petitioner wants a lab assistant, so sending an 
Alchemist will get the job done successfully.


===========================
B5-06: Three-Point Strategy
===========================

Description: A missive containing Duelhorn's strategic plans for the near
             future has been intercepted.
             -Three-Point Strategy-
             Launch coordinated attacks on Camoa, Graszton, and Moorabella,
             using the confusion thus generated to....... Kh.......
             headquarters.....
             *A word from the pub:
             Poster unknown, some sections illegible.
Quest Type: Defeat Mark
Victory Circumstance: Defeat the Night Dancer! (Camoa)
                      Defeat Alys the Ensorceled! (Moorabella)
                      Defeat Duke Snakeheart! (Graszton)
Forbidden: Harming the Opposite Sex (Camoa)
           Actions by Viera (Moorabella)
           Targeting Self (Graszton)
Rank: 48
Appears: After completing Quest E5-01 (The Dig), Quest B5-02 (Summons), and
         visiting any town.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Camoa
          Moorabella
          Graszton
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 39
                  Adaptability = 39
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 96 Clan Points
              Negotiation +2
              Teamwork +2
Reward: 4920 Gil
        Wyvern Wing

For this quest, there are three battles at three different locations you must 
partake in. Once you emerge victorious on all three of them, the quest will 
be complete.

Over in Camoa, you have to face the Night Dancer (a Trickster), as well as an 
all-Bangaa group (Defender, Master Monk, Dragoon, Cannoneer, and Bishop). 
This is a more physical attack-based group, and you have to fight through 
them to get to your main target, which makes it all the tougher. You need to 
kill the Master Monk quickly due to his Lifebane ability being able to cast 
Doom on one of your clan members. The Night Dancer's card attacks from a 
distance can get quite annoying as well, which is all the more reason why you 
should hurry up and get to defeating them. Once you start picking apart this 
group one by one, it gets much easier, trust me. It would be great if you 
bring lots of long-range attackers and magick-users, particularly someone who 
can heal/use items, since you will surely need it with all the attacking 
taking place. Either way, once you defeat the Trickster, Camoa will be safe 
again.

In Moorabella, you are up against Alys the Ensorceled (Summoner), and her 
part of Duelhorn (Spellblade, Sniper, White Mage, Assassin, Elementalist). 
You have to deal with a bit of long-range attacks, as well as powerful 
magicks from the Elementalist and Alys herself. The Sniper and Assassin can 
hit you from afar, but you don't want them too close for their abilities will 
get much worse! You will want some long-range attackers in your party as 
well, especially ones who can Disable/Stop/Silence the enemies (Fusiliers and 
Elementalists come to mind here). Their Elementalist has Doublecast, which 
makes her twice as difficult, so you will want to put a stop to that early 
on. You would do well to defeat everyone except the White Mage and Alys 
herself before moving across to where she is standing atop the roof. She also 
doesn't attack you with summons until you get too close, which makes 
approaching her easy enough. When you get close, let loose with all your 
attacks and she will quickly be defeated, allowing Moorabella to rest easy 
once again.

For the Graszton battle, you have to defeat Duke Snakeheart and his mages. 
You have to fight not only Snakeheart, who is an Arcanist, but he has a Sage, 
Black Mage, Time Mage, Illusionist, and White Mage defending him. Luckily for 
you, you only have to defeat him to win the battle, so you can avoid the 
Black Mage and Sage from the start. Along the path leading to Snakeheart, 
there are a number of traps, so if you have a Ranger with Awareness, they 
will be useful in this battle. It also happens that all the traps that cause 
Charm are by where the enemies are, so more than likely that will play into 
your favor as well. Their Illusionist is by far the most dangerous, due to 
its ability to attack from a great distance. Don't waste any time fighting 
anyone else; just focus on the Duke so that you can end this battle quickly. 
If you have abilities which cause Disable, Silence, or Stop will be great. 
Once you beat Duke Snakeheart, Graszton will be saved.


======================
B5-07: Memories Forged
======================

Description: To Clan Gully:
             A great master of the sword lies upon death's door. I would have
             you deliver something to them. I await in Nazan Mines.
Quest Type: Delivery
Victory Circumstance: Investigate the shining object!
                      Protect Frimelda and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Back Attack
           Back Attack
Rank: 42
Appears: After completing Quest E5-06 (Through Another's Eyes), Quest B5-03
         (Hunted), and visiting any town.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Nazan Mines
          Kthili Sands
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 47
                  Adaptability = 47
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 84 Clan Points
              Negotiation +2
Reward: 6620 Gil
        High Arcana

For this quest, you must first head to Nazan Mines. Once there, you will 
enter a battle against a couple of Wolves and Floating Eyes. It seems that 
the client is not here, but there is something shining on the ground nearby 
that you should investigate. There is only one spot you need to check out for 
this quest, and luckily the enemies are not too difficult, so you should have 
no problems accomplishing this task. As soon as you get to the shining spot 
and examine it, you will find it is a curative for the zombie Frimelda, and 
decide to go bring it to her.

Your next destination for this quest brings you to Kthili Sands. Over here, 
you will have to do battle with four Ghouls. It so happens that you run into 
Luc Sardarc, who is trying to protect Frimelda this time. Since you're 
fighting the other undead enemies here, you should remember to use a Phoenix 
Down or something similar once you get them down to 0 HP so you completely 
defeat them. These creatures are no major threat, but their Drain Touch can 
take a lot of HP away, and they tend to target Frimelda, so you need to keep 
her health high. It isn't required, but it would be extremely useful for you 
to collect the treasure in the fancy chest on the high ledge, as it contains 
an Orb of Minwu. Once you defeat the enemy Ghouls, the battle will end. Luso 
will use the curative on Frimelda, and as an added twist, she will join your 
clan as thanks!


=============================
B5-08: Geomancer's Way - Mist
=============================

Description: Geomancers bend nature to their will.
             Our society has established a series of trials for prospective
             geomancers to determine whether they are worthy to share in our
             knowledge.
             The Trial of Seething Mist is the fourth and final trial. Pass,
             and our wisdom will be yours.
             -Naturalist Society
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: HP <= 100
Rank: 38
Appears: After completing Quest B5-04 (Geomancer's Way - Snow).
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Aldanna Range
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 33
                  Adaptability = 33
New Job Availability: Geomancer
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 76 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
Reward: 4850 Gil
        Mahbeny (x2)

Here in the final trial, you have an uphill battle ahead of you, literally. 
You have to fight the three Geomancers, as well as a Toughskin and a 
Lamashtu. The Lamashtu is the closest to where you begin, so you will want to 
take it out first, so you can spare yourself the potential Charm/Confuse 
status it can inflict! The Toughskin can wreak the most havoc though, since 
its Resonate move can target your entire party and cause Disable status on 
them. You need to have an Elementalist or someone with an ability to cause 
Disable to try and stop the Toughskin as quickly as possible. As for the 
Geomancers, they have their usual abilities that can take advantage of the 
Mist condition (in this case, they can deplete your MP). Once you manage to 
defeat everyone here, you will finally earn the right to become a Geomancer!


========================
B5-10: The Last Duelhorn
========================

Description: Clan Gully,
             Please, stop Maquis. He's taken it upon himself to do everything
             alone.
             I would go, were it not for my wounds... Please, help.
             -Alys
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat Maquis the Phantasm!
Forbidden: Ranged Weapons
Rank: 52
Appears: After completing Quest E5-06 (Through Another's Eyes), Quest B5-06
         (Three-Point Strategy), and visiting any town.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Bisga Greenlands
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 47
                  Adaptability = 47
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 99 Clan Points
              Aptitude +3
Reward: 5320 Gil
        Stradivari

Here, you will come across Maquis, who insists on leading Duelhorn until the 
very end. He splits into six versions of himself, all Ninjas, and the battle 
will commence. You seriously need to have your best clan members here to do 
battle with these guys. Magick-users and strong attack abilities (Aurablast, 
Sidewinder, Moogle Lance, the Ultima attacks) are highly recommended. You 
also need to make sure you have someone that can heal, since you surely will 
run low on HP at some point. You can also bring Hurdy as a Bard, since his 
songs can buff you up and help quite a bit. As for the enemies, they can all 
use their various Veil attacks to inflict adverse status effects on your 
clan, so be prepared to use Esuna or the Bard's Soul Etude to cure those. 
They are all equipped with the Ninja Tabi accessory, which allows them to 
move very far each turn. The best method of attacking here is to concentrate 
on one enemy at a time. That way, you are quickly defeating them, and leaving 
that much less to worry about when you go to the next enemy. Once you manage 
to defeat them all, you will have finally defeated Duelhorn once and for all!


===========================
B5-11: The Way of the Sword
===========================

Description: To Clan Gully:
             I would fight the blademaster returned from death's threshold.
             One on one. Come to the ruins in the north.
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: < 20 Damage
Rank: 50
Appears: After completing Quest E5-11 (Pirate Problems), Quest B5-07
         (Memories Forged), and visiting any town.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Ruins of Delgantua
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 51
                  Adaptability = 51
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 99 Clan Points
              Teamwork +3
Reward: 7880 Gil
        Putrid Liquid

When you come here, you will meet Ghi, who you saw fight another swordsman in 
a previous quest. Frimelda will be here this time, and Ghi wants to fight 
her, being that she is the blademaster and all. You can only send Frimelda 
into this battle, so make sure she is a strong melee job with a secondary 
action ability being Items (so she can cure herself). It will help a LOT if 
she has a Ribbon equipped, since many of Ghi's attacks can inflict status 
effects that prevent you from having control (such as Confuse and Berserk). 
It will also help if you can get your back against a wall, so that Ghi cannot 
get to back attack you, as that will be quite painful if he does. If your HP 
is at 200 HP or below, use the X-Potion to heal up before continuing. Once 
you manage to best Ghi in battle, the battle will be over.


======================
B5-14: Lethean Draught
======================

Description: I must slay a certain monster for the reagents of a potion I
             require, and seek allies to join me on the hunt.
             -Maquis
Quest Type: Escort

        Aurea Pollen

In this battle, you actually have to help Maquis from Duelhorn battle a group 
of Dreamhares. It seems that Maquis doesn't remember you at all. Anyway, this 
group of enemies are so easy, therefore you shouldn't have any difficulty 
defeating them. The only annoying part is their Illude ability, which can 
Charm their target. You still need to protect Maquis though, and since the 
enemies can pack a punch when they group together, you should have someone 
ready to heal him as well. Once you defeat them all, you will find out what's 
wrong with Maquis, and the quest will end.


===================
B5-15: Devil's Pact
===================

Description: I am afflicted with a terrible disease that eats away at my body
             each day. A kind man named Maquis brings me medicine to slow its
             effects, but he's begun to behave strangely. He's had dealings
             with the Witch of the Fens, and I think there may be a
             connection between her and his behavior. I need someone who
             knows the witch to look into this matter on my behalf.
             -Cyda

        Cockatrice Skin

When you arrive here, you will meet the Witch of the Fens yet again. She will 
ask you to slay the enemies that the potion Maquis wanted was derived from. 
That means you have to defeat the Dreamhares only. There are three of them 
here, but they have Illude and will try to Charm you, so be careful! Once you 
defeat the three Dreamhares, the quest will end successfully after the Witch 
of the Fens explains the situation to you.


======================
B5-16: One Last Memory
======================

Description: Maquis cared for me when I was ill. I owe him a debt of kindness
             that can never be repayed. So when he left with a grim look on
             his face muttering something about a snake, a great fear took
             me. I feel I may never see him again. Someone, please, see that
             he's all right.
             -Cyda
Quest Type: Defeat Mark
Victory Circumstance: Defeat Duke Snakeheart!
Forbidden: Back Attack
Rank: 60
Appears: After completing Quest B5-15 (Devil's Pact).
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Galleria Deep
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 54
                  Adaptability = 54
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 99 Clan Points
              Teamwork +3
              Adaptability +3
Reward: 2940 Gil
        Prime Tanned Hide

In this battle, you must defeat Duke Snakeheart once and for all. You are up 
against him (Arcanist), as well as his crew (Defender, Seer, Parivir, 
Flintlock, and Scholar). Movement in this area may be difficult due to the 
fact there are many traps dividing you and the enemy. A Ranger with Awareness 
will help remedy this situation. The greatest threat besides Snakeheart 
himself is the Parivir with his abilities which can Immobilize or Berserk 
your units. The Defender is also quite powerful with Bangaa Cry, which can 
Confuse its targets. As for Duke Snakeheart, he has the most powerful magicks 
Gigaflare and Scathe, as well as Death (instant KO). You only need to defeat 
the Duke in order to complete this quest, but you should take out the 
Defender and Parivir along the way as they are the greatest danger to you. If 
you can somehow Disable these enemies, you will be in a much better position. 
Once you manage to defeat Duke Snakeheart, the battle will be over and you 
will complete this quest.


=================================
C1-01: It's a Secret to Everybody
=================================

Description: My pet shelling, Titoise, has run away, kupo, and I need someone
             to find him for me! You see, I've been keeping him in secret,
             kupo. If Mr. Grann finds out, this little moogle is going to be
             in big trouble. Kupo!
             If that wasn't bad enough, Mr. Grann's daughter, Fes, can't
             stand shellings. So I'm sure to catch a pom-pom lashing from
             both of them, kupo!
             -Keeper Pirillo, Grann's Menagerie
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Weaken Titoise and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Ice
Rank: 40
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request) and Quest B1-08 (Flown the
         Coop), and visiting any town.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Goug
Days: 20

                  Adaptability = 44
Ability Points: 30

              Teamwork +2
              Adaptability +2

        Aqua Galac

For this battle, you are up against three Great Tortoises, a White Chocobo, 
and a Red Chocobo. One of the Great Tortoises is Titoise, so you have to look 
for the name. You need to defeat the rest of the enemies, but only weaken the 
one you want to critical health. The Great Tortoises have a Headbutt ability 
which can Immobilize your party members. The White Chocobo can cure its 
allies, and the Red Chocobo can use the strong Choco Meteor on your clan, so 
watch out! Once you clear out the rest of the enemies, that's when you should 
concentrate on bringing down Titoise's health. Once it's at a critical state, 
the quest will be complete.


=======================
C1-02: Hellhound Astray
=======================

Description: I was cleaning out Helda's pen-one of our hellhounds-and when I
             finished she was gone! She must have broken free of her chain,
             but I know who they'll blame!
             Helda's one of Mrs. Zamaree's favorites, and you can be sure
             that if she finds her missing, there will be, well, hell to pay.
             I need someone to find Helda and bring her back before she's
             missed!
             -Keeper Leena, Grann's Menagerie
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Weaken Helda and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Bludgeoning Weapons
Rank: 39
Appears: After completing Quest C1-01 (It's a Secret to Everybody).
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Kthili Sands
Days: 20

                  Adaptability = 33
Ability Points: 30

              Teamwork +2
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 7370 Gil
        Gold Chalice

In this area, you must do battle against some Hellhounds and Worgens. One of 
the Hellhounds is Helda, the one you need to find and capture. Lucky for you, 
Helda is a different color than the rest of the Hellhounds, so you can 
distinguish her easily. Defeat the other enemies first, then weaken Helda to 
critical health to win this quest. Be careful of the Worgens, as they can use 
attacks from a distance to Silence or Immobilize your allies. Once you defeat 
everyone else and manage to bring Helda to critical health, you are done.


=======================
C1-03: My Little Carrot
=======================

Description: Oh, it's terrible! Simply terrible!
             My poor little Carrot has gone wild all of a sudden and hied off
             to gods know where! Her eyes... Oh, her eyes were like unto a
             malboro's!
             I hope you can bring her back, but if you can't, perhaps you
             could put her out of her misery?
             -Mrs. Zamaree, A certain menagerie owner's wife
Quest Type: Defeat Mark

         Astray), and visiting any town.

        Scarletite

This battle puts you against some tough monsters, including Brown and Red 
Chocobos, a Tonberry, two Great Malboros, and a Cassie (Carrot). It can be 
difficult especially since you're dealing with Malboros, which can inflict 
some nasty status effects on your clan. The chocobos can cure the other 
enemies and hit you with their attack abilities as well. You only need to 
defeat the Cassie in order to clear this quest, so concentrate on getting 
over there as quickly as you can. The Tonberry can be a threat if it decides 
to stalk one of our clan members, and there are also traps strewn about which 
can cause Charm status. Be careful and take out the enemies in your way, then 
defeat Carrot to finish this quest.


===========================
C1-04: An Earnest Multitude
===========================

Description: I seek the love of my life! My search has led me through city
             streets and far abroad. I have even taken up the pen, and met
             three charming ladies in my correspondence. Ah, but I've made a
             mess of things by scheduling a rendezvous with each of them on

Like the two before it, you need to go to the three locations within six days 
to meet with the ladies. This time, they want a love song, so agree to sing 
and you will clear this quest. It is highly recommended you use the dispatch 
feature for this, unless you accept this quest in Fluorgis and do it manually 
from there.


============================
C1-05: Foodstuffs: Nutrition
============================

Description: Foodstuffs needed. You will be required to catch specific
             monsters at a specific location. The details are as follows:
             -Blue, round, feathered, long of tail.
             -Enough to feed sixteen.
             -One eyeball is enough to make soup for four.
             Too many is no good. Too few is also no good.
             -Poison Tasters Guild "The Iron Stomach"
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Procure the requested ingredients!
Forbidden: Copycat
Rank: 30
Appears: After completing Quest C3-16 (Sleepless Nights) and Quest B1-12
         (Foodstuffs: Appearance).
Price: 400 Gil
Location: The Galleria Deep
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 20
                  Adaptability = 20
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 60 Clan Points
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 3780 Gil
        Demon Feather (x2)
        Adamantite (x2)

For this quest, you are in a cave full of Ahrimans and Floating Eyes. If you 
read the orders carefully, they refer to the Floating Eyes (look at the 
description for a comparison), so you should be going after those enemies. Be 
very careful of the Ahriman enemies though, as they can Confuse your party, 
whereas the Floating Eyes can only Silence you. To best tackle this, you will 
have to send half your group to each side, in the event that Floating Eyes 
spawn on either side. Of course, you can kill the Ahriman as well, since they 
won't count towards your total of Floating Eyes. Once you have killed exactly 
four Floating Eyes, go talk to the apprentice to complete this quest.


==============================
C1-06: Foodstuffs: Bon Appetit
==============================

Description: Foodstuffs needed. You will be required to catch specific
             monsters at a specific location. The details are as follows:
             -Hidden within a treasure chest.
             -Enough to feed ten.
             -One finger per serving.
             Too many is no good. Too few is also no good.
             -Poison Tasters Guild "The Iron Stomach"
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Procure the requested ingredients!
Forbidden: Harming the Weak
Rank: 40
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request), Quest C1-06 (Foodstuffs:
         Nutrition), Quest A2-10 (Odd Places) by examining the upper-middle
         well, and visiting any town.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Goug
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 33
                  Adaptability = 33
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 80 Clan Points
              Negotiation +2
Reward: 8420 Gil
        Mysidia Alloy (x4)

For this quest, you are in a room full of treasure chests as well as a Zahak. 
Your job is to go around and open the treasure chests; some contain treasure, 
and others contain Mimics. Those Mimics are the ones you have to kill to get 
the ingredients requested for the quest. You need ten servings, which means 
you need ten fingers; Mimics have five fingers, so you only need to kill two 
of them. Once you do that, go talk to the apprentice and the quest will be 
complete.

Description: I seek the love of my life! My search has led me through city

time. Pick the first option and you will succeed both times.


==============================
C1-09: House Bowen's Challenge
==============================

Description: Clan Gully,
             You've kept yourselves busy since our last meeting. Care to test
             your sword arm against us in a speed battle? Or have you lost
             your edge?
             -Bowen of House Bowen
Quest Type: Meet Objectives
Victory Circumstance: Speed Battle vs. House Bowen
Forbidden: Targeting Self
Rank: 30
Appears: After completing Quest C3-06 (Grounded!) and Quest B1-16 (Showdown),
         and visiting Fluorgis.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Targ Wood
Days: 20
Required Talents: Adaptability = 15
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 60 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
Reward: 4590 Gil
        Water Sigil (x3)

Here, you meet up with House Bowen again, this time for a speed battle 
against a giant Rafflesia. The beast is in the level 30 range, and its 
abilities all inflict some sort of status effect on you, which makes it all 
the more dangerous. That being said, you will definitely want some long-range 
attackers so you can keep your distance from the enemy's range. The mark has 
over 1000 HP, the exact amount remaining you won't be able to see until it's 
below 999. If you have a Black Mage with upper-level Fire magick (Fira or 
Firaga), they will come very much in handy, as will any other fire-based 
attacks. Of course, the objective of the speed battle is to get the last hit 
on the enemy in order to win, so take that into consideration when planning 
your attacks. When you land the final hit on the Rafflesia, you win the match 
and the quest!


==============================
C1-10: Yellow Wings in Trouble
==============================

Description: We're at the mercy of some pretty bad customers... I don't think
             we're going to make it! Help!
             -The Yellow Wings
Quest Type: Escort
Victory Circumstance: Protect the Yellow Wings and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Harming the Weak
Rank: 55
Appears: After completing Quest E5-11 (Pirate Problems), reading the Notice
         "A Theft from the Manor" at the Pub, and visiting any town.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Ruins of Delgantua
Days: 20
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Defender
Required Talents: Negotiation = 51
                  Teamwork = 51
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 99 Clan Points
              Negotiation +3
              Teamwork +3
Reward: 12780 Gil
        Orichalcum

When you arrive here, you will find the Yellow Wings being confronted by none 
other than House Bowen. You need to defend them and defeat your past allies 
in battle. However, if any of the Yellow Wings dies, the quest will be a 
failure. You're up against a Fighter, Illusionist, Ravager, and Assassin. The 
toughest of the group is the Illusionist, due to his ability to hit multiple 
targets with strong abilities. The Assassin's ability to Stop your allies 
will make it all the more worth eliminating her quickly as well. Either way, 
once you put down all of House Bowen, the battle will be over.

==========================
C1-13: Seeding the Harvest
==========================

Description: *****Help Wanted!*****
             It's seeding time again, and each year we lose crops to raiding
             monsters. We seek hardened adventurers to stand between our
             livelihood and their fiendish claws!
             -T.K. Corral
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Defeat 10 foes!
Forbidden: Knockback
Rank: 21
Appears: After completing Quest A2-03 (The Moon Seal), during the month of
         Coppersun.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Camoa
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 8
                  Adaptability = 8
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 42 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 9240 Gil
        Tiny Mushrooms (x2)

In this area, you are faced with a number of different monsters, with more 
joining the battle with each passing round. You'll see a wide variety here, 
each with its own attacks and many status ailments they can inflict on you. 
You need to be able to hit them hard and fast in order to survive this 
battle. You'll be more likely to succumb due to adverse status effects, so 
watch out! My advice would be to keep your clan together so you can 
concentrate on enemies on one side of the area, and let the rest come to you. 
This is a HARD battle, but quite doable if you have the right jobs and are at 
a high enough level. You really need to have attacks that can hit from a 
distance (Fusiliers and Rangers are a huge plus, as are mages).


=====================
C1-14: A Harvest Hand
=====================

Description: *****Help Wanted!*****
             It's harvest time, and what a year it's been! Our crop is so
             large, we need all the hands we can find to help us bring it in.
             The more you harvest, the greater your reward!
             -T.K. Corral
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Gather as much fruit as you can in 4 rounds!
Forbidden: Harming the Weak
Rank: 25
Appears: After completing Quest B2-11 (Now That's a Fire!) and Quest C1-13
         (Seeding the Harvest), during the month of Ashleaf.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Camoa
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 9
                  Adaptability = 9
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 50 Clan Points
              Negotiation +1
              Teamwork +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 12830 Gil
        Healing Water (x2)
        Insect Husk

Out here in the orchard, you will find several fruit-filled trees along the 
sides of the area. Your job is to go to them and gather some fruit. Of 
course, there are plenty of tough monsters here to get in the way, with more 
pouring in every few turns. You only have to survive four rounds though, so 
concentrate more on getting to each of the six trees before that time is up. 
Try to take out some of the more annoying enemies if they are in your way, 
like the Ahrimans and Liliths. After four rounds, the quest will end and the 
number of trees you gathered fruit from will be tallied.

====================
C2-01: Ruinous Traps
====================

Description: I was sent to remove some old traps, but the local monsters had
             other ideas.
             They're very territorial, and don't welcome "interlopers." I was
             lucky to escape with my life, and I have no intention of going
             back! It should be enough to destroy the traps-will you go in my
             place?
             -Esther, New Hire
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Uphold the law and destroy the traps!
Forbidden: Attack
Rank: 46
Appears: After completing Quest D4-11 (Wanted: Sky Pirate Vaan) and Quest
         B2-04 (A Fatal Mistake), and visiting Graszton.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Ruins of Delgantua
Days: 20
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Ranger
Required Talents: Negotiation = 33
                  Adaptability = 33
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 92 Clan Points
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 9450 Gil
        Windslicer Pinion (x2)

For this quest, you once again have to destroy a bunch of traps which are 
apparently guarded by this group of monsters (Baknamys, Luchorpan, and 
Tonberry King). The law makes it so you can't use basic attacks, but that 
doesn't rule out special abilities! Either way, there are eight traps that 
need to be destroyed by you walking on them, so get to it. Bring out your 
fast-moving clan members so you can get around the room quickly. As for 
dealing with the enemies, you can fight them with alternate means aside from 
regular attacks. The Tonberry King is one you will want to keep your distance 
from, but the others are not that big of a deal. Green traps cause around 10 
HP of damage, purple ones cast Charm, blue causes spikes to take 1/2 your 
current HP, and yellow causes Silence. Once all the traps are disabled, the 
quest is complete.


====================
C2-02: Komodo Search
====================

Description: There was an...incident the other day while I was out making a
             delivery, and the load of potions I was meant to deliver ended
             up scattered along the ground. Will you help me collect them?
             Oh, and...let's keep this between you and me. The fewer people
             that know about this, the better.
             -Trader for a certain potion manufactory
Quest Type: Item Recovery
Victory Circumstance: Gather all the potions!
Forbidden: Restoring HP
Rank: 20
Appears: After completing Quest B2-11 (Now That's a Fire!) and Quest C2-05
         (Komodo Departure), and completing an auction.
Price: 300 Gil
Location: The Galleria Deep
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 9
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 40 Clan Points
              Aptitude +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 3660 Gil
        Silk Thread (x2)

In this area, your job is to pick up the potions that the trader dropped. You 
are up against Ice Drakes, Ice Flans, and a Wendigo. The enemies are big on 
using ice-based attacks to heal themselves and hurt you, so be careful. As 
usual, it's a good idea to kill them before going for the potions. By now you 
should have second-tier Black Magick (Fira), which will come very much in 
handy against these creatures. You still have to protect the trader, so try 
and kill any enemy that goes near him (can't heal, thanks to the law in place 
here). There are seven locations to search for potions, as shown by the 
sparkling spots on the ground. After you check them all, the quest ends.


=====================
C2-03: Komodo Arrival
=====================

Description: Finally! We've arrived in Moorabella! I've done it, Celestine!
             Except...now there's a problem. Can someone come and help me,
             please?
             -Komodo Trader
Quest Type: Investigation
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Targeting All Units
Rank: 25
Appears: After completing Quest C3-01 (Mountain Watch) and Quest C2-02
         (Komodo Search), and visiting Moorabella.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Moorabella
Days: 20
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Defender
                            Arcanist
Required Talents: Negotiation = 13
                  Aptitude = 13
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 50 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
Reward: 3330 Gil
        Holy Stone (x3)
        Yellow Liquid (x3)
        Wyrmtwig

Here in Moorabella, you have to help the Komodo Trader fend off another clan 
that wants to get in his way. The Badd Potions group consists of an Archer, 
Black Mage, Time Mage, Illusionist, and Geomancer. You will probably be able 
to kill off the Black Mage quickly since he's the closest to where your clan 
starts off. Luckily this time around you don't have to worry about protecting 
the trader, which means he is more or less a dummy target for the Geomancer 
(these enemies tend to not move from their initial positions). The Time Mage 
has an annoying ability called Rime Bolt Tome which injures enemy and ally 
alike, same as the Illusionist's Freezeblink. The Geomancer's Avalanche can 
harm you and put you to Sleep, plus it has a large range, so you may want to 
eliminate her quickly as well. The Archer is the lowest threat so you can 
save her for last, since the mages and Geomancer all have strong multi-target 
abilities you need to put a stop to. After you defeat the clan, the Komodo 
Trader will thank you by giving you a Wyrmtwig.

=======================
C2-05: Komodo Departure
=======================

Description: I have to deliver some merchandise, and the road promises to be
             treacherous. Guards needed!
             Pay: 2,200 gil
             The successful applicant will have confidence in their sword
             arm, be passionate about their work, and love to quaff potions.
             -Komodo Potions
Quest Type: Escort
Victory Circumstance: Protect the Komodo Trader and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Targeting an Area
Rank: 16
Appears: After completing Quest B2-01 (Wanted: Ugohr) and visiting Graszton.
Price: 300 Gil
Location: The Bisga Greenlands
Days: 20
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Defender
Required Talents: Negotiation = 7
                  Teamwork = 7
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 32 Clan Points
              Negotiation +1
              Teamwork +1
Reward: 2200 Gil
        Zodiac Ore (x5)
        Cruzle Brass (x3)
        Rabbit Tail

Out along the cliffs, your job is to protect the Komodo Trader from the 
bandits threatening to steal his potions. You are up against two Warriors, an 
Archer, Moogle Knight, and a Fusilier. The most annoying of the bunch by far 
is the Fusilier since he wields a gun which can target pretty much anywhere 
on the map. The Warriors also have some pretty strong attacks, so try and 
take them out quickly, especially since they are closer to where you begin. 
Additionally, there are a couple traps strewn about the area (you won't see 
them), so good luck avoiding them. Use items to heal as you take out these 
bandits one at a time. The Fusilier, annoying as he is, will probably be the 
last one you take out because of where he's located atop the cliff and how 
long it will take your clan to get up there as well. If the Komodo Trader is 
weak, heal him since if he dies, you fail!

             market.

             cassie variant of malboro-a vastly inferior specimen. We must

             Look into the matter with all haste.

Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
