When you arrive in Graszton, you will see that you are fighting a band of 
thieves, four of them to be exact. Fortunately for you, all they can really 
do to you is attack and attempt to steal gil. That means it will be a rather 
simple fight to get through. Simply advance up the street and ambush the 
thieves, and take them out to win this quest.


==============================
C2-10: The Root of the Problem
==============================

Description: The counterfeiters recently remanded to our custody have
             divulged the source of the fake De'vine Ribbons. We'll find no
             lasting solution to the problem until we've stopped it at the
             source. Please follow up on this information and take such
             action as you deem appropriate.
             -Galmia Pepe, Office of Administration
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: > 100 Damage
Rank: 21
Appears: After completing Quest B2-16 (Pearls in the Deep) and Quest C2-09
         (The Genuine Article), and visiting Graszton.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: The Galleria Deep
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 11
                  Adaptability = 11
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 42 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
Reward: 2980 Gil
        Black Thread (x2)
        Battlewyrm Carapace (x5)

Here, you will find the hideout of the counterfeiters, and they are ready for 
you! You are up against a Ninja, White Monk, Viking, Fighter, and two 
Thieves. The White Monk will again be the most difficult enemy here, 
especially since it has Aurablast which can hit multiple targets. The Ninja's 
Fire Veil can be tricky as it can Confuse your allies, which is not good. The 
rest of your opponents are just the typical physically attacking sort, so 
there's nothing to really worry about there. Focus on killing the White Monk 
and Ninja first, then take down the others quickly to defeat the counterfeit 
group!


======================
C2-11: The Whole Truth
======================

Description: We've exhausted our supply of materials needed to make De'vine
             Ribbons, and we need someone to bring in the latest harvest.
             -Galmia Pepe, Office of Procurement
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Buffs and Debuffs
Rank: 22
Appears: After completing Quest C3-01 (Mountain Watch) and Quest C2-10
         (The Root of the Problem), and visiting Moorabella.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Zedlei Forest
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 13
                  Adaptability = 13
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 44 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
Reward: 3430 Gil
        Pearl Moss (x3)
        Prime Pelt

Here in the forest, you have to face six of the Cassie variety of Malboros. 
They all have the ability to Charm your clan members, as well as cause Slow 
and Sleep status. They can even use Regen on themselves and raise defense, so 
these enemies are clearly a bunch you'll want to eliminate fast. However, 
once the Cassies advance, you are in for a VERY bad time with all these 
status effects being constantly spammed your way, coupled with them using 
Love Song to repair any damage you manage to inflict on them. You will need a 
lot of long-distance attackers, plus magick-users who can either inflict a 
lot of damage very quickly, or use Haste on your group. It would also be 
essential to have Ribbons equipped to protect against Charm, but you don't 
get those until later in the game, so maybe you should wait until later to 
conquer this quest (or dispatch a good enough party to take care of it).


==============================
C2-12: Chita on Weapons-Adepts
==============================

Description: Ngaaa!
             I teach the youths one thing, they forget ten others! Teach 'em
             to focus, and then they can't focus on anything else!
             Nothing for it but to keep teaching 'em what I can. If it means
             breaking every bad habit they have one by one, so be it!
             -Chita, Chita's Weaponers
Quest Type: Meet Objectives
Victory Circumstance: Speed Battle vs. Chita's Weaponers
Forbidden: Bludgeoning Weapons
Rank: 39
Appears: After completing Quest C3-16 (Sleepless Nights) and Quest C2-15
         (Chita on Weapons-Novices).
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Rupie Mountains
Days: 20
Required Talents: Adaptability = 20
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 78 Clan Points
              Negotiation +2
              Teamwork +2
Reward: 5900 Gil
        Beastlord Horn (x3)

Here, you are again met by Chita's Weaponers (two Warriors and a Gladiator) 
for another speed battle. This time, the battle is against a Golem at the far 
end of the area. As in any speed battle, you need to land the final blow in 
order to win the bout, so time your movements and attacks accordingly. When 
attacking the Golem, do not use magick as it has Reflect automatically. Be 
careful when attacking up close due to its Blink Counter Reaction ability, 
which will knock you back in a counter attack. Chita's Warriors will try and 
gang up on the mark, so try not to weaken the enemy too much when your turns 
are up, or else they may get the kill. Move your clan up close and wait for 
them to attack, then let loose with all your attacks in a row to win this 
easily.


===============================
C2-15: Chita on Weapons-Novices
===============================

Description: Ngaaa!
             The youths these days can't wield a weapon to save their lives!
             ...Feh! Nothing for it but to teach 'em myself.
             -Chita, Chita's Weaponers

              Negotiation +2
              Teamwork +2

        Damascus (x4)
        Coral Fragments (x3)

In this cave, you are met by Chita's Weaponers (two Warriors and a Gladiator) 
and are challenged to a speed battle against a Deathscythe enemy. The 
creature is an undead, so you can hurt it with healing spells if you so 
wanted. It can heal itself with dark-based attacks, however. Nonetheless, you 
should bring strong attackers and surround the mark so you have the prime 
locations to attack it from. You have to inflict the final blow before 
Chita's group does, so time your attacks accordingly. They won't be able to 
attack it if you surround the enemy, so that works in your favor.

In the mountains, your job is to find a kupoppy flower for Kolulu at one of 
five sparkling spots on the ground. However, you will have to fight through 
Wolves, Werewolves, and a Worgen to get to the peak. These enemies are 
nothing new, so you should have no difficulty making your way to the top and 
defeating them all. Of course, the quest ends once you find the flower by 
searching each location until you uncover the kupoppy.

In the Larva Den, you will meet with Scarface and his clan (Juggler, Lanista, 
Master Monk, Hunter). There is a random mark which appears in this area, and 
the objective is for your clan to deliver the final blow before Scarface's 
clan does. Ignore the regular Baknamy enemies that are also in the area, and 
focus on the main mark. If you can increase your speed with Haste, be it with 
a Time Mage or Tinker, it will help immensely. You can only bring four clan 
members into the battle, so bring your strongest attackers so you can beat 
this mark quickly. It only matters who has the final blow on it, so act 
accordingly so that your clan can kill the beast and win the match.

Description: Saw some suspicious fellows the other day, dragging this little
             monster off somewhere... I wonder if it weren't one o' them
             endangered monsters?
             A Carm Mercantile fella was only telling me about 'em the other
             day. Made a donation right there and then, I did! Anyway, that

For this quest, you are sent to protect the cluckatrices from the Hellhounds 
and the Beastmaster controlling them. The Hellhounds themselves won't really 
bother with the Cluckatrices, but will attack your clan. That leaves it to 
the Beastmaster to control them so they DO attack the endangered animals. 
That said, you need to focus all your attacks on killing the Beastmaster 
quickly. If you can Disable him (Elementalist's Fire Whip comes to mind), you 
will be much better off. When you defeat the Beastmaster, the quest will be 
complete following another scene involving Cid and Ewen.

==========================
C3-08: Cleaning to Ordalia
==========================

Description: Looking for helpers to swab an airship.
             We haven't had the crew to properly clean her for some time now.
             It would be a shame to put her out of service, so we'll have you
             cleaning her mid-flight. Oh, and watch out for the rats.
             -Jylland Airship Inspection Board
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Clean the airship within 4 rounds!
Forbidden: Fire
Rank: 22
Appears: After completing Quest C3-06 (Grounded!) and visiting Fluorgis. You
         must be in Moorabella to accept this quest.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Moorabella
Days: 4
Required Talents: Aptitude = 1
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 44 Clan Points
              Aptitude +1
              Teamwork +1
Reward: 180 Gil
        Fine Wool

Aboard the airship headed for Fluorgis, your job is to clean up all the dirty 
points (sparkling spots on the ground; three on the deck, one on the back 
right wing, and one on each of the front wings). Of course, this would be no 
challenge without the inclusion of six Mimics to slow you down and hinder 
progress. It is imperative that you send only your six clan members with the 
greatest speed and especially range of movement for this quest. You will need 
to push two members to the far end of the ship as quickly as possible, to 
reach those far two swabbing points. It will also help if you have Counter as 
the Reaction abilities for your characters, which will hopefully help to 
eliminate the Mimics without you having to waste a turn attacking. You have 
until the end of the fourth round to complete the task, so if you have your 
characters in position on the far wings, you could keep an eye on the turn 
list on the top screen and have the rest of your party fight off the Mimics 
for some extra loot. Don't waste too much time though, the ship must be clean 
for you to succeed!


========================
C3-09: Stuck in the Muck
========================

Description: Ever since my husband passed away, I've been having this
             recurring dream in which he tells me he wants me to come home.
             My husband met his end in Tramdine Fens, but his wedding ring
             was never found. Perhaps this is why he cannot find his way?
             Someone, please recover it!
             -Widow Maleen
Quest Type: Item Recovery
Victory Circumstance: Find the lost wedding ring!
Forbidden: Ranged Weapons
Rank: 26
Appears: After completing Quest C3-06 (Grounded!) and visiting Fluorgis.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Tramdine Fens
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 15
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 52 Clan Points
              Aptitude +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 4610 Gil
        Mythril (x2)
        Spiral Incisor (x3)

Here in this swampy area, you will have to find the missing wedding ring. To 
get to all of the locations where it may be, you have to fight through a 
Sprite, Great Tortoises, and various Chocobos. You can't use ranged weapons 
here, so magick is key to winning this battle. The Chocobos can cure each 
other, so you may want to finish off an enemy quickly if you don't want to 
prolong the battle. As for the Great Tortoises, they will cast Regen on 
themselves as soon as you attack them, which means you need to hit them hard 
and quickly to defeat them in a timely manner. Regardless of the enemies, as 
soon as you find the ring, the fun here is over.


=======================
C3-10: Poachers Spotted
=======================

Description: They took her away! They took Calea away! I'd been wounded in
             battle, and she went to the woods to pick herbs for a poultice,
             when she saw them-she saw those endangered monster poachers
             doing a deal! That's why they took her!
             Someone, please help her in my place!
             -Leeger, Warrior-in-training
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Go to Calea!
                      Defeat all foes and keep them away from Calea!
Forbidden: Harming the Weak
           Copycat
Rank: 40
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request) and Quest C3-05 (Monster
         Poaching), and visiting any town.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Bisga Greenlands
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 18
                  Adaptability = 18
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 80 Clan Points
              Negotiation +2
Reward: 7880 Gil
        Kuraisle Boxwood (x2)

When you first arrive here, you will find Calea surrounded by four Floating 
Eyes at the far side of the area. The enemies are very easy and their attacks 
are weak, so don't bother wasting time with fighting them. Simply move one of 
your units down to where Calea is, and this part of the quest will be 
complete. Cid and Luso will give Calea some medicine, then chat a bit before 
the thugs from Khamja arrive.

A new battle will commence at this point, with the same clan members you 
picked earlier in the quest. Now you are up against a Master Monk, Assassin, 
Parivir, Seer, Arcanist, and Lanista; overall a tough crowd with plenty of 
strong attacks. You need to be extremely careful here, as the Arcanist and 
Seer can cast Haste and Cura, and the Assassin can use Last Breath, which 
immediately kills its target if successful. The Lanista can also Blind 
multiple members of your party, which makes attacking the more evasive 
opponents like the Parivir even harder to hit. If you have heavy hitting 
melee attackers and magick-users here, you should be in pretty good shape. 
Just don't let them get near Calea; keep the enemies at bay and defeat them 
quickly to clear this quest.

=====================

Description: There's trouble brewing in Targ Wood!
             Came across a young bangaa run afoul of a band of ne'er-do-

Here, your objective is to protect Kyrra the Dragoon from the incoming bangaa 
attack. You will have to face three White Monks and two Warriors here. The 
White Monks are most dangerous since they have the ability Air Render which 
can cause lots of damage, so concentrate on killing them first. The law that 
is imposed in this battle makes it so you can't make quicker work of them, 
but you shouldn't have any problems otherwise. Just work on taking them out 
one at a time; with Kyrra attacking as well, this shouldn't take too long.

=====================

Description: There's talk of a strange group gathering in Targ Wood. They

This battle puts you against four Viera Green Mages who start off in their 
formation in front of your party. Lucky for you only a couple of them 
actually know Green Magick (Blind and Sleep) and they are usually 
ineffective, so all you have to worry about are their weak physical attacks. 
Take them out one at a time with your regular attacks and magick, and you 
should be fine.

C3-15: An Unseen Foe
====================

Description: Illegal monster gambling has been going on in Graszton, right on
             Baron Beltorey's doorstep. It is my belief that this has

             we hear so much about of late. If you know anything, please tell

In Graszton prior to the battle, you witness a conversation between Cid and 
Luso regarding all of the events leading up to this point. Then, people will 
run from the Pub screaming about a fiend bird, which turns out to be the 
Mamatrice and one of her Cluckatrice children. You are here to protect them 
from the people who are trying to attack them (a Black Mage, Viking, and 
Soldier). Take on the Black Mage first, as his spells have the greatest 
potential for damage. You bring a smaller group into this battle, but the 
enemies won't take too long to defeat, though they are quite strong as well 
and will tend to focus their attacks on the monsters. Once you defeat the 
trio, the birds will be saved and the quest will be complete.

=====================
C4-01: Veis, Assassin
=====================

Description: I am Veis, a warrior pilgrim traveling the world and taking such
             wisdom as she will give.
             I have come to Jylland to train for a time with House Bowen, a
             hunter clan of some renown. I request a guide to show me to
             them.
             -Seeker Veis, Assassin
Quest Type: Meet Objectives
Victory Circumstance: Speed Battle vs. House Bowen
Forbidden: Actions by Moogles
Rank: 13
Appears: After completing Quest B2-06 (Wanted: Gilmunto).
Price: 300 Gil
Location: The Rupie Mountains
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 8
                  Adaptability = 8
New Job Availability: Assassin
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 26 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 2280 Gil
        Bomb Shell (x2)
        Giant Feather
        Fire Stone (x5)

For this mission, you have to face a Malboro King enemy at the other side of 
the area. You will meet Veis the Assassin, who wants to join Clan Bowen, but 
they want her to prove her worth first. That means killing the mark before 
Clan Bowen does. You are to assist Veis in doing this. The best approach is 
to move all your units onto the bridge directly in front of where you begin, 
and attack the target from a distance (Air Render is excellent, as is Black 
Magick). The objective is to simply land the final blow on the enemy. If you 
hog the spaces on the bridge, this should be simple as the only person in 
Clan Bowen who can attack from a distance is their Illusionist. Once you beat 
the mark, Veis will teach you the Assassin job so you can use it as well!


======================
C4-02: To Be a Fighter
======================

Description: Who will you find at the front line of any army worth its salt?
             Fighters, and plenty of 'em.
             Prove yourself worthy. Best us in combat, and we'll teach you
             the ways of the sword and fist.
             -Jeorge, Mailed Fist Regular
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Restoring MP
Rank: 14
Appears: After completing Quest B2-11 (Now That's a Fire!) and completing an
         auction.
Price: 300 Gil
Location: Moorabella
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 8
                  Adaptability = 8
New Job Availability: Fighter
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 28 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 1600 Gil
        Tiger Hide (x3)
        Peppergrass
        Ice Stone (x5)

You will be facing a group consisting of three Fighters, a Thief, Soldier, 
and Warrior. For the most part it's a straightforward close-quarters physical 
battle, with the exception of the Warrior's Air Render attack. If you come 
well prepared with your strongest melee attackers and magick users, you 
should be in great shape here. The best advice would be to kill the Fighters 
quickly since their Aurablast ability is strong and can hit multiple members 
of your clan in one shot. Upon completion of the battle, you will gain access 
to the Fighter job!


=========================
C4-05: Popocho's Chocobos
=========================

Description: Kupo! My precious chocobos have all run off! Every last one of
             them! It looks like they've headed for the mountains in the
             Aldanna Range. I need someone to find them before the monsters
             do, kupo!
             -Popocho, Chocobo Knight
Quest Type: Escort
Victory Circumstance: Protect the chocobo and defeat all foes!
                      Protect the chocobos and defeat all foes!
                      Protect Popocho and his chocobos!
Forbidden: > 50 Damage
           Actions by Moogles
           Actions by Humes
Rank: 27
Appears: After completing Quest C3-01 (Mountain Watch) and visiting
         Moorabella.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: The Aldanna Range
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 13
                  Teamwork = 13
New Job Availability: Chocobo Knight
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 54 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 4360 Gil
        Blood-darkened Bone (x4)
        Adamantite (x3)

This quest takes place in the Aldanna Range, putting you into a total of 
three separate battles throughout the area. In each of the battles, there is 
a Yellow Chocobo you must protect from the various enemies. The first battle 
puts you against a Wolf, two Werewolves, and a Zaghnal. Fortunately for you, 
the Chocobo can fight back against the enemies and even cure itself. The only 
tricky part is using weak attacks, especially at the point in the game you 
get this quest. Either way, defeat all the enemies and the first Chocobo will 
be saved.

Now for the second battle, there are two Green Chocobos that need saving from 
the Ice Flans and Wendigos. Since both enemies are ice-based, the Ice Flans 
tend to use Blizzard to heal themselves and hurt you. If you have the 
Elementalist's Fire Whip, it will come in handy here. You will need strong 
attackers to take out the Wendigos since they are quite strong and hit very 
hard. The Green Chocobos can use Choco Barrier, which casts Protect/Shell, as 
well as the standard Choco Cure. Once you defeat the enemies, these two birds 
will be saved.

For the final battle, you have to save two Chocobos (Black and White), as 
well as Popocho this time. You are up against a powerful Zahak, two Ice 
Drakes, and a Ghost. The Ice Drakes can be taken out easily with fire-based 
attacks like in the previous battle with the Ice Flans. The Ghost can be 
taken down with healing magick/items (make sure you use a Phoenix Down or 
Raise to totally destroy it at 0 HP). As for the Zahak, it starts off far 
away and moves slowly, so you should concentrate on the others before 
worrying about it. The Chocobos cast all sorts of buffs, including Regen, 
Protect and Shell, so you should be in excellent shape here. Once you win the 
third and final battle, Popocho will teach you the Chocobo Knight job as 
thanks!


===========================
C4-06: Of Kupos and Cannons
===========================

Description: Strange noises punctuate the night. There's naught but trees and
             the occasional abandoned well for many leagues, yet the din of
             "kupo"s and firearms is quite overwhelming.
             I can scarcely focus, never mind study, and so I find myself
             turning to frivolous fictions.
             Predictably, my schoolwork has begun to suffer and my very
             future is now in peril. Please find the cause of this nuisance
             and put a stop to it!
             -Orposi, Sophomore (again)
Quest Type: Investigation
Victory Circumstance: Survive for 4 rounds!
Forbidden: Debuffs
Rank: 22
Appears: After completing Quest B2-16 (Pearls in the Deep) and reading the
         Notice "Trouble in Jylland" in the Pub.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Camoa
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 11
                  Aptitude = 11
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 44 Clan Points
              Negotiation +1
              Teamwork +1
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 2870 Gil
        Tyrant Hide (x4)
        Alraune Drill (x2)

Out in the middle of the night, you will find a group of Flintlocks having 
their firing practice. Your clan has come to ask them to stop, but they 
refuse, so a battle must ensue. They are all armed with hand cannons, which 
they must Prime before actually launching an attack on you with them. That 
means you get a free round in between attacks to heal up if need be. The 
attacks themselves are rather weak, so you shouldn't be too worried. More 
Flintlocks will emerge from the wells, but the point here is to survive for 
four rounds. You can tell when a Flintlock is primed to attack because of the 
icon above its head. The rounds may feel like they take forever to go through 
because of how many Flintlocks eventually emerge, but it isn't a difficult 
battle. Once the fourth round ends, you have won and the Moogles will teach 
you the way of the Flintlock as an added reward.

Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 38 Clan Points
              Aptitude +2
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 2350 Gil
        Hedychium Pollen (x4)
        Leucojum (x3)

When you arrive in this snowy area, you will find Mayhew and her party 
assembled atop the hill (Raptor, Lanista, Time Mage). There are Ice Drakes, a 
Lamia, and a Bloody Orb below waiting to attack while you search for the 
concertina (the sparkling spots on the ground). The enemies are not terribly 
difficult, especially if you have fire-based attacks for the Ice Drakes. The 
Lamia may pose a challenge if you don't take it out early, with the status 
effects it can inflict. The Devotees that Mayhew brought along are not all 
that useful either, so you'll be doing the fighting and searching pretty much 
on your own. When you find the ornate concertina, the quest is complete. As 
thanks, Mayhew will teach you how to use the Raptor job, which will now be 
availabile.


=============================
C4-08: Loar Airships Grounded
=============================

Description: The skies along the shipping lanes to Loar have been teeming
             with floating eyes. They've even infested the aerodrome. If
             something isn't done, they'll wreck the airships, and could even
             spill out into the town. Stop them before it's too late!
             -Jaq, Airship Pilot
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Opportunity Commands
Rank: 24
Appears: After completing Quest C3-16 (Sleepless Nights). You must be in
         Moorabella to accept this quest.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Moorabella
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 13
                  Adaptability = 13
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 48 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 3750  Gil
        Earthwyrm Crystal (x2)
        Bundle of Needles (x2)

For this battle, you have to fight off the various floating eye enemies on 
the airship. You are up against Bloody Orbs, Floating Eyes, and Ahrimans. The 
Ahriman is the most dangerous due to its ability to Confuse and Charm your 
allies, so you will want to take them out as quickly as possible. Use long-
range attacks and offensive magick to gain the edge on these enemies easily. 
The smaller eyeball enemies don't do much other than attack or use Supersonic 
Wave, which can Silence you. At this point in the game, they are rather weak, 
so you only really need to worry about the Ahriman enemies and their status 
effects. Once you clear up these enemies, the airships will be safe to fly 
once more!

======================
C4-10: Sleight of Hand
======================

Description: Tricksters by name and trade are we-masters of sleight of hand.
             Beat us at our own tricks and the tricks of the trickster trade
             are yours for the trick...er, taking!
             -Glackta, Trickster Extraordinaire
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Receiving Buffs and Debuffs
Rank: 23
Appears: After completing Quest D4-01 (Making Music) and visiting Moorabella.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Nazan Mines
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 15
                  Adaptability = 15
New Job Availability: Trickster
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 46 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 2790 Gil
        Earth Sigil (x5)

For this quest, you must battle five Tricksters in order to learn the way of 
their trade. You should bring a White Mage or someone who can heal, since you 
will be taking a beating from these guys with their long-distance card 
attacks. The law may be difficult to uphold here since the Tricksters can use 
abilities on you which can cause various status effects such as Immobilize 
and Berserk. Other than their card attacks, this group you're fighting is 
quite easy to defeat, so you shouldn't have too much difficulty here. If you 
have a high-jumping clan member (Jump = 4), you can claim the treasure 
containing a Ribbon on the high ledge in the far left side of the room. Once 
you defeat these Tricksters, you will be taught how to use the job as well, 
and the quest will be complete.


===================
C4-11: Kidnapping!?
===================

Description: I can't get word to Prima Donna, and I've tried everything!
             We've got a concert coming up, too... Surely they haven't been
             kidnapped...have they? Oh, gods, they have! Someone look into
             this, please!
             -Manager, Prima Donna
Quest Type: Investigation
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes before they enter the water!
Forbidden: Back Attack
Rank: 30
Appears: After completing Quest C3-16 (Sleepless Nights) and Quest C4-07
         (Instrument of Inspiration).
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Sant D'alsa Bluff
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 20
                  Aptitude = 20
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 60 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 3030 Gil
        Prime Pelt (x3)

In this battle, your objective is clear: defeat all the enemies before they 
make it into the water, and it so happens you are fighting Prima Donna here! 
Anyway, you are up against a Raptor, Fencer, Hunter, and Spellblade, as well 
as two weak Devotees on the right side (Lanista and Time Mage). Send one of 
your party members to defeat the Devotees, and the rest of your group forward 
to the main Prima Donna. Be sure to use your clan members who can move far 
and attack from a distance. If you have the Elementalist, the Boulder Crush 
will come very much in handy to immobilize the flying enemies as they have 
the greatest range of movement. It will be a difficult battle because of the 
guidelines, but it will help if you have your party sit in the water to block 
the enemies from reaching it. A Time Mage with Haste is essential for this 
battle. If you really want to take the easy way out, send out a good dispatch 
party to tackle this quest. Nonetheless, once Prima Donna is defeated, they 
will apologize for accusing you of spying, and the quest will be complete.


================
C4-13: Banbanga!
================

Description: The Tri-Bangaa Temple welcomes novices seeking guidance in the
             martial arts.
             Handed down over many hundred years, the martial arts are
             considered by many the pinnacle of melee combat. Temper body and
             mind as we share with you the secrets of these arts.
             -Monks of the Tri-Bangaa Temple
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Targeting Self
Rank: 29
Appears: After completing Quest C3-06 (Grounded!) and visiting Fluorgis.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Nazan Mines
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 22
                  Adaptability = 22
New Job Availabilty: Master Monk
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 58 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
Reward: 5340 Gil
        Body Ceffyl (x4)

Here, you get to meet the Bangaa Monks, consisting of two White Monks and 
three Master Monks. The Master Monks here are a bit tougher, each of them 
being able to attack twice in the same turn, as well as having the ability to 
attack more strongly if they have low HP. If you have anyone as a Ninja with 
Duel Wield, it will come very much in handy here to quickly take down the 
enemies. Also, anyone with Black Magick or the Elementalist's Fire Whip would 
be useful as well. The key here to avoid taking massive damage is to attack 
from a distance. When you win the battle, you will learn the Master Monk job 
so you too can become one!


=====================
C4-14: The Cat's Meow
=====================

Description: I saw it with me own eyes! A white cat as big as a man if it was
             a foot, it was. Leastwise, I think it were a cat. Prowling about
             the Rupie Mountains plain as day. Well, strutting about in a
             place with monsters like that will get it eaten alive in no time
             flat. Will you go and save it?
             -Maerwynn, Cat Lover
Quest Type: Escort
Victory Circumstance: Protect Roye and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Ranged Weapons
Rank: 27
Appears: After completing Quest C3-16 (Sleepless Nights).
Price: 400 Gil
Location: The Rupie Mountains
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 20
                  Teamwork = 20
New Job Availability: Seer
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 56 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
Reward: 6150 Gil
        Einherjarium (x3)
        Orichalcum (x2)

Out here, you will find Roye on the hill surrounded by various enemies 
(Wendigos, Wolves, and a Zaghnal). Of course, you start the battle as far 
away from his as possible, so that means you have a lot of ground to cover. 
The Seer can fend off the enemies to some extent, but he will very quickly 
find himself cornered, which is not good either. Luckily, he has Magick 
Frenzy which will enable him to fend off enemies quite well when they are 
close together. The Wendigos cannot be hurt with physical attacks if you are 
next to them, so you need to use magick and other abilities to defeat them. 
The rest of the enemies are quite commonplace, even the physically strong 
Zaghnal. You'll want to take that one out as quickly as you can. Once you 
defeat all the enemies here, Roye will be saved and will teach you how to 
become a Seer as thanks!

In this quest, you have to fight some extremely easy enemies for this point 
in the game. They are all at Level 10 and below, so there is no challenge in 
this at all. Simply defeat them quickly and the quest will be over before you 
know it.


=============================
C5-01: Geomancer's Way - Rain
=============================

Description: Geomancers bend nature to their will.
             Our society has established a series of trials for prospective
             geomancers to determine whether they are worthy to share in our
             knowledge.
             The Trial of Venomed Rain is the second trial. When you are
             ready to continue your journey down the path, come.
             -Naturalist Society
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Swimming
Rank: 36
Appears: After completing Quest C5-02 (Geomancer's Way - Sun).
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Tramdine Fens
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 33
                  Adaptability = 33
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 72 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
Reward: 4080 Gil
        Rainbow Thread (x2)

For this second trial, you are up against three Geomancers, as well as a 
Wendigo and Nagaraja. Due to the fact it's raining, the Geomancers will have 
a strong water attack they can use, as well as the usual abilities that can 
inflict status effects on you, most notably Immobilize and Disable. The 
Wendigo and Nagaraja are physically strong as well, so you will want to bring 
a strong melee attacker to beat them down (preferably someone with Duel Wield 
or even Aurablast). Magick users are quite effective here against the Wendigo 
specifically. Just like the first trial, once you defeat them all, your job 
here is done.


============================
C5-02: Geomancer's Way - Sun
============================

Description: Geomancers bend nature to their will.
             Our society has established a series of trials for prospective
             geomancers to determine whether they are worthy to share in our
             knowledge.
             The Trial of the Sun is the first of four trials. When you are
             ready to be tested, come.
             -Naturalist Society
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Reaction Abilities
Rank: 35
Appears: After completing Quest D4-11 (Wanted: Sky Pirate Vaan) and visiting
         Graszton.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Kthili Sands
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 33
                  Adaptability = 33
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 70 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
Reward: 5460 Gil
        Cockatrice Skin (x2)

In this first trial to become a Geomancer, you have to face three Geomancers, 
a Hellhound, and a Nidhogg in battle. The Hellhound is the easiest of the 
bunch, so you should kill it first. The Nidhogg has a lot of HP, plus its 
attacks are quite powerful, even moreso when amplified with Dragon Force, so 
you may want to save it for last. As for the Geomancers, they have a range of 
attack abilities based on what terrain they stand on, so be careful of them 
all. They can cause the Slow status effect and cause a lot of damage. If you 
can get Disable status on any of them, it will be quite helpful to your 
cause. When you defeat the entire group of enemies, you will succeed in the 
first trial here.


=================
C5-03: Starstruck
=================

Description: We've been so busy with our singing we've entirely neglected our
             stage combat. Sparring is well and good, but our adoring public
             wants authenticity-only a proper melee with beasts and blood
             will do! I'm sure we can handle ourselves, but we are out of
             practice, so a bodyguard would be welcome. Will no one come to
             our aid?
             -Prima Donna
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Restoring MP
Rank: 47
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request) and Quest C4-15 (The
         Storage Shed).
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Ruins of Delgantua
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 33
                  Adaptability = 33
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 94 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 8670 Gil
        Waterwyrd Crystal

Here, you will be fighting some enemies alongside Prima Donna. The monsters 
here consist of a Lamia, Great Malboro, Deathscythe, Nidhogg, and Headless. 
Lucky for you, four members of Prima Donna will be here to fight alongside 
you. Some of the enemies here are known for their adverse status effects they 
can inflict on you, so you will want to bring out magick-users and long-range 
attackers to handle them. Try and bring your strongest attackers to this 
battle, that way you can do your part to end this battle as soon as possible, 
with Prima Donna providing some much-needed support.


============================
C5-04: Moorabella Nightwatch
============================

Description: A plague of robberies has fallen upon the land! All occur at
             night and follow a similar pattern, indicating that a single
             group may be responsible. For the swift resolution of this case,
             and the safety of our citizens, we are currently accepting
             applications to join the Moorabella Nightwatch.
             -Jylland Sovereignty Society
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes within four rounds!
Forbidden: Copycat
Rank: 40
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request) and visiting any town.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Moorabella
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 44
                  Teamwork = 44
                  Adaptability = 44
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 80 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
Reward: 6620 Gil
        Aurea Pollen

Here, you have to do battle against three Baknanys and a Luchorpan. The catch 
is that you have to defeat them all in four rounds. The Head Editor of Bonga 
Bugle will be there, as well as the Owner; they won't do much but they can 
still help if an enemy is weak. That can be a bit tricky, especially since a 
couple of them remain out of reach atop a roof, so you will need some long-
range attacks here. Magick-users are quite welcome, as are Tricksters and 
Fusiliers. If you have a melee attacker with Aurablast, that will come very 
much in handy for hitting multiple enemies at once with a strong hit. I find 
that having a Juggler with Smile Toss comes in handy for bringing your best 
attacker's turn around more quickly. When you beat these enemies before the 
end of the fourth round, the quest will be a success.


==============
C5-05: Ravager
==============

Description: To Clan Gully,
             Think you're all that? Prove it! I'm waiting in the Galleria
             Deep!
             -Tigrina, Ravager
Quest Type: Meet Objectives
Victory Circumstance: Speed Battle vs. Tigrina
Forbidden: Targeting Distant Units
Rank: 44
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request) and visiting any town.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Galleria Deep
Days: 20
Required Talents: Adaptability = 44
New Job Availability: Ravager
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 88 Clan Points
              Aptitude +2
              Teamwork +3
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 6720 Gil
        Scarletite

For this quest, you have to partake in a speed battle against Tigrina. She is 
a Ravager and she is by herself, but do not underestimate; her attacks are 
actually quite strong. Your mark is the Flowsand Lord (a Yowie) at the bottom 
of the area, but there are Pit Beasts to deal with along the way. The giant 
mark's attacks have not changed since you faced it earlier in the game, but 
you still need to kill it before Tigrina does. Try and surround the pit where 
the enemy is so she can't get an opening in, but make sure you have someone 
who can heal your party as needed. When you land the final blow on the 
Flowsand Lord first, you win the battle, and Tigrina will teach you how to 
become a Ravager as well!


========================
C5-06: A Lanista's Pride
========================

Description: Something horrible has happened: a great affront to my family I
             cannot let stand! Though it's only a few days before the next
             Prima Donna concert-I've never missed one yet-I find myself
             contemplating selling my tickets and going to face those
             responsible for said affront!
             In short, I have resolved to confront them, and I need someone
             to stand witness.
             -Viva Prima Donna! -Devotee
Quest Type: Escort
Victory Circumstance: Defend the devotee and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Lightning
Rank: 26
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request) and visiting any town.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Fluorgis
Days: 20

                  Teamwork = 39
New Job Availability: Lanista
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 52 Clan Points
              Negotiation +1
              Teamwork +2
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 3050 Gil
        Hero Tonic (x4)

In this battle, you must defend the Lanista (the Devotee) from the Head 
Editor (Ranger) and Owner (Berserker), as well as a Ninja, Assassin, and 
Parivir. The biggest threat is the Assassin, as she can target the Devotee 
from a distance and attack; you'll want to eliminate that quickly. The Ninja 
has Dual Wield, so try and send your best attacker (preferably with Dual 
Wield as well) after him. It will help if you have someone who can heal the 
Devotee if his health runs low. Once you defeat the weak Editor and Owner, as 
well as their bodyguards, the quest is over and you will walk away with the 
ability to become a Lanista!


======================
C5-08: Goug Nightwatch
======================

Description: A plague of robberies has fallen upon the land! All occur at
             night and follow a similar pattern, indicating that a single
             group may be responsible. For the swift resolution of this case,
             and the safety of our citizens, we are currently accepting
             applications to join the Goug Nightwatch.

For this quest, you have to fight three Baknamys and a Luchorpan who are 
threatening the city. You must defeat these four enemies within four rounds, 
although they are not too difficult. The thing is, they are spread out due to 
Goug's layout, so you need to disperse your clan members. Luckily, this is 
made easier by the fact that another group is here to help you defeat them (a 
Parivir, Ninja, and Assassin). Basically, you just need to worry about the 
side you start off on and the other people will handle the rest.

=======================
C5-16: Unplumbed Depths
=======================

Description: Came across a curious notice in the pub about a new tunnel
             discovered in the Neslowe Passage. A little exploration may turn
             up the treasure the passage is rumored to hold.
Quest Type: Defeat Mark
Victory Circumstance: Get the treasure!
Forbidden: Targeting Self
Rank: 49
Appears: After completing Quest D5-13 (Bringer of Doom), having Adelle master
         the Hilo ability (Chirijiraden) as a Heritor, and reading the Notice
         "A New Path!" at the Pub.
Price: N/A
Location: The Neslowe Passage
Days: N/A
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 98 Clan Points
              Aptitude +2
              Teamwork +2
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 11150 Gil
        Stormsoul Crystal

In this area, you will be up against Bloody Orbs, Golems, a Bomb, and a 
Lamashtu. They are guarding the lone treasure chest in the middle of the 
area; however, the problem is you cannot open the chest until you defeat all 
of the enemies! The Golems can use Helmsplitter, which may destroy your 
equipment. The Lamashtu is by far the most dangerous enemy here, since it can 
use Eternal Sleep to cast Sleep/Doom status on everyone in the area, and Kiss 
to Charm your allies. That said, you will want people on your side who can 
attack from a distance or use attack magick. These enemies are not really 
that difficult, but the status effects can really hinder you, so you will 
want to defeat them as soon as you can. Once you beat them all, open the 
chest to complete the quest. Adelle will also master the Adelaide ability, 
which is the final Heritor ability!


=========================
D1-01: An Earnest Delight
=========================

Description: I seek the love of my life! My search has led me through city
             streets and far abroad. I have even taken up the pen, and met
             five charming ladies in my correspondence. Ah, but I've made a
             mess of things by scheduling a rendezvous with each of them on
             the same day! I need someone to meet four of the lucky damsels
             in my stead. Only the dashing need apply-I've a reputation to
             consider!
             -Marnot, Pride of Fluorgis
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Impersonate Marnot!
Forbidden: Harming Seeq
Rank: 25
Appears: After completing Quest E5-01 (The Dig), Quest C1-04 (An Earnest
         Multitude), and visiting any town.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Goug
          Tramdine Fens
          Zedlei Forest
          The Bisga Greenlands
Days: 6
Required Talents: Negotiation = 44
                  Adaptability = 44
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 50 Clan Points
              Negotiation +1
              Teamwork +1
Reward: 2930 Gil
        Prime Pelt

Like the quests before it, you need to go to the four locations within six 
days to meet with the ladies. This time around, you have to enter battle 
against a Viking and a Ranger at the first (Goug) location. Be sure to accept 
this quest in Goug so you can do this in time. For that battle, simply wander 
around for two of rounds and do NOT attack your opponents! You also have to 
impersonate Marnot, so when asked, say his name of course. After the first 
part in Goug, you need to dispatch your clan members to the other three 
locations (you can't possibly finish this in six days without dispatching). 
As long as your dispatched units are right for the job (check to see that 
they are jumping up and down when you select them for dispatch), you'll be 
victorious here yet again.


===================
D1-02: Oh No, Kupo!
===================

Description: I don't know when or how these bombs got in here, but they made
             a real mess of the town, kupo! Our machines got blown to
             smithereens! Kupo-po! I'd pick up the pieces, but I can't see
             for the tears! Could someone collect what's left?
             -Sheni, Machinist
Quest Type: Item Recovery
Victory Circumstance: Gather all the machinery parts!
Forbidden: Harming the Weak
Rank: 39
Appears: After completing Quest D4-11 (Wanted: Sky Pirate Vaan) and visiting
         Graszton.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Goug
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 33
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 78 Clan Points
              Negotiation +2
              Aptitude +2
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 7210 Gil
        Tanned Beast Hide (x2)

In the city of Goug, you are sent to find six machinery parts scattered 
around. However, there are three Bombs, a Grenade, Headless, and Worgen 
waiting to attack you. The law can make things difficult, especially since at 
this point in the game, it's very likely you are stronger than the enemies 
are (you can afford to lose the law bonus if you can't help your levels, I'm 
sure). The Bombs and Grenade can be the most difficult, due to their ability 
to cast Quicken when they have critical health, which will almost always lead 
to them self-destructing, causing massive damage to any nearby allies.

Nonetheless, you don't HAVE to fight, but you probably should since they will 
get in the way of you reaching every sparkling spot in the area. The Headless 
can be a powerful attacker, as can the Worgen (at critical health, the Worgen 
can even call more enemies to the battlefield, so watch out). Also, don't 
forget to collect the rare treasure in the upper-right area (Elixir)! Once 
you collect all of the machinery parts, this quest is done.


===============================

                  Adaptability = 20

Reward: 4970 Gil
        Earth Sigil (x2)

Out here, you are on the Bangaa side fighting against the Nu Mou. You bring 
four of your clansmen to accompany the Bangaa Brotherhood (a Gladiator, 
Bishop, and Cannoneer) in the battle against the Nu Mou Nobles (Time Mage, 
Illusionist, Arcanist, White Mage, Black Mage). Your target should clearly be 
the White Mage, obviously due to its healing abilities. The Black Mage and 
Arcanist are quite dangerous as well, so you will want to deploy other party 
members to take them out. The Time Mage will cast Haste on its allies and 
Slow on you, but it's not that big of a deal since you clearly outnumber 
them. Once the Cannoneer on your team gets to attacking, you will be in great 
shape because of how powerful his shots are. Once you take down this group of 
mages, you will claim victory with the Bangaa.


================================
D1-07: The Rivalry of the Rupies
================================

Description: The Rupie Mountains are ours...but someone apparently forgot to
             tell those interlopers that! Come and see us stomp out this
             latest threat to our territory!
             We'll show them-and the world-that we of the Bangaa Brotherhood
             aren't to be trifled with!
             -Mocedad, Bangaa Brotherhood
Quest Type: Escort
Victory Circumstance: Protect Mocedad and Madreth!
Forbidden: Buffs
Rank: 59
Appears: After completing Quest D4-11 (Wanted: Sky Pirate Vaan), Quest D1-05
         (The Bangaa of the Rupies) three times, Quest D1-10 (The Nu Mou of
         the Rupies) three times, reading the Notice "Rupie Mountain Open?"
         at the Pub, and visiting Graszton.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Rupie Mountains
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 33
                  Teamwork = 33
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 99 Clan Points
              Teamwork +3
              Adaptability +3
Reward: 10030 Gil
        Moon Ring (x2)
        Shining Lute

Out here, you find Mocedad being cornered by House Bowen, and you are here to 
defend him. Once you send your three clan members to the battle, Madreth from 
the Nu Mou clan will appear to aid in the battle as well. You still need to 
protect him, too. Madreth also brought a Time Mage along to further aid the 
cause, which will come in handy. As for House Bowen, you have to deal with 
their usual setup (Fighter, Assassin, Illusionist, Ravager). The Illusionist 
has the most damaging abilities, so you will want to defeat him first. The 
Assassin will probably be your last target due to her constant use of the 
Vanish ability. If any of your guests run low on health, be sure to cure them 
since if they die, you fail the quest. Luckily, Madreth (an Arcanist) can use 
Drain to help heal himself. Once you defeat the enemies, the quest will end 
and you will receive the Shining Lute as a reward for resolving the rivalry!


===================
D1-09: Tree Hugging
===================

Description: Monsters are chewing on the tree where my brother and I used to
             compare heights as children. I fear it will soon die if nothing
             is done. Could someone drive off the monsters for me?
             -Celestine, A Good Sister
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Defeat 10 foes and keep them from the tree!
Forbidden: Restoring MP
Rank: 15
Appears: After completing Quest C2-05 (Komodo Departure).
Price: 300 Gil
Location: Graszton
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 7
                  Adaptability = 7
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 30 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 3280 Gil
        Power Fruit (x2)
        Telaq Flower
        Dirty Wool

This quest puts you in a ring-shaped area with a special tree in the middle. 
A total of 10 enemies will pour into the area (5 or 6 will be onscreen at one 
time), in the form of Antlions and Pit Beasts. The Pit Beasts are the 
stronger ones, so be careful of their Sandstorm ability which can heal them 
and hurt you. You must keep the enemies away from the tree, so split your 
party in half and head in different directions to keep the enemies at bay. 
Once you kill the final enemy, the quest will be complete and the tree is 
safe again.


===============================
D1-10: The Nu Mou of the Rupies
===============================

Description: Our rivalry has gone on for many long years...long enough. I
             want it to end. We must vanquish into shame those musclebound
             Bangaa Brotherhood goons once and for all!
             Seeking warriors with faith in their mental acuity to aid our
             cause in battle. The battlefield will be the Rupie Mountains.
             -Madreth, Nu Mou Nobles
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Items
Rank: 50
Appears: After completing Quest C3-16 (Sleepless Nights), Quest C1-15 (The
         Bangaa Brotherhood), Quest C1-12 (The Nu Mou Nobles), reading the
         Notice "The Rivalry of the Rupies" at the Pub, during the month
         Coppersun.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Rupie Mountains
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 20
                  Adaptability = 20
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 99 Clan Points
              Teamwork +3
              Adaptability +3
Reward: 10640 Gil
        Earth Sigil (x2)

Out here, you are on the Nu Mou side fighting against the Bangaas. You bring 
four of your clansmen to accompany the Nu Mou Nobles (an Arcanist, White 
Mage, and Illusionist) in the battle against the Bangaa Brotherhood (Master 
Monk, Bishop, Cannoneer, Gladiator, White Monk). Your target should clearly 
be the Master Monk and Gladiator, as they are the strongest attackers on the 
opposition. The Cannoneer can attack from a great distance, so you will want 
to eliminate that quickly as well. Luckily, on the Nu Mou side, you have a 
White Mage who will keep your party in good shape, as well as the Arcanist 
and Illusionist to help fight back the Bangaas. Once you defeat the Bangaa 
Brotherhood, you will have completed this quest!


===============
D1-13: Memories
===============

Description: Ayeee! I've lost my precious wayfarer's log, the one I used in
             my youth. It's gone! Gone! How can I go to my grave with this
             hanging over me?
             Would someone care to give me their wayfarer's log? It might
             serve well enough to bring back the memories...
             -Old Man Boiboi
Quest Type: Delivery
Rank: 15
Appears: After completing Quest C2-06 (The Forests of Loar), during the month
         of Mistleaf.
Price: 300 Gil
Location: Targ Wood
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 1
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 30 Clan Points
              Negotiation +1
Reward: 140 Gil

For this quest, Old Man Boiboi will want you to give up your Wayfarer's Log. 
You fill this up by completing certain quests, listed below:

    Quest C2-06 (The Forests of Loar)
    Quest C2-07 (The Lands of Loar)
    Quest C2-08 (The Towns of Loar)
    Quest D2-01 (The Seas of Ordalia)
    Quest D2-02 (The Wonders of Ordalia)
    Quest D2-03 (The Wonders of Loar)
    Quest D2-04 (The Forgotten Places)

Anyway, for each of these quests you complete, you get a log. Depending on 
how many logs you have, you will receive a special reward from the old man. 
Those rewards are as follows:

      1: X-Potion               2: Elixir
      3: Mythril                4: Waterwyrd Crystal
      5: Eureka Crystal         6: Grimoire Stone
      7: Ribbon (first time only; subsequent reward will be Grimoire Stone)


======================
D1-14: 'Tis the Season
======================

Description: Tis the season again...the season for those horrid mimics to
             start spawning.
             Oh, I want to get rid of them this year in the worst way, but it
             will take a while to activate my magickal device that should put
             an end to the infestation. I need someone to hold them off until
             it gets going!
             -Center for Mimic Control Research
             -Assistant to the Chief
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Buy time for four rounds!
Forbidden: HP <= 20
Rank: 29
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request) and visiting any town,
         during the month of Silversun.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Neslowe Passage
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 44
                  Adaptability = 44
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 58 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 6220 Gil

For this quest, you are up against a bunch of Mimics who keep respawning if 
you kill any of them. They really aren't a threat to you, so just bring a 
good party who can attack from a distance and wander the area for four 
rounds, fighting the Mimics to get some extra loot. They tend to drop some 
rare loot items, so it's worth defeating a bunch of them. If you have the 
Faerie Shoes accessory, be sure to equip them on one of your clan members and 
have them collect the rare treasure in the upper-left area, as it contains a 
rare Madu blade. It also works if you have a Gria in your party. Anyway, the 
rounds take a long time to cycle, so you'll have plenty of time to gather 
loot from these creatures. Once the fourth round is over, you are free to go!

==============================
D2-05: Chita on Weapons-Adepts
==============================

Description: Ngaaa!
             It's just no good! I've sung the praises of focus and
             determination high and low, but it just doesn't seem to stick!
             Nothing for it but for me to give a lecture to end all lectures!
             -Chita, Chita's Weaponers
Quest Type: Meet Objectives
Victory Circumstance: Speed Battle vs. Chita's Weaponers
Forbidden: Piercing Weapons
Rank: 49
Appears: After completing Quest D4-11 (Wanted: Sky Pirate Vaan) and Quest
         C2-12 (Chita on Weapons-Adepts), and visiting Graszton.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Ruins of Delgantua
Days: 20
Required Talents: Adaptability = 33
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 98 Clan Points
              Negotiation +2
              Teamwork +2
Reward: 7550 Gil
        Bundle of Needles (x3)

For the third and final time, you are pitted against Chita's group in a speed 
battle! Your mark is a Reaver sitting on the high ledge. You will want to 
avoid magick attackers since the mark has the "Evade Magick" Reaction 
ability, as well as getting too close to it, since it can destroy your armor 
and hit you with a strong Holy Strike attack. Stick with long-range attackers 
like Tricksters, Hunters, Fusiliers, and the like. If you have any units with 
Duel Wield, the extra attack that warrants will be quite useful here. As 
always, you win if you land the final blow on the enemy, so time your attacks 
accordingly. Because Chita's group are melee attackers, it would do you well 
to position your own units around the Reaver so it can't move and they can't 
attack it either. When you win, Chita will give you the Materia Blade as an 
added reward.


===============
D2-06: Bug Hunt
===============

Description: I need someone to catch these really rare antlions for me.
             They're supposed to be different colors from the other antlions.
             I never seen them myself, but they're supposed to live in the
             forest, or grasslands, or something like that. Oh, and I heard
             of one being seen near Moorabella once, too.
             -Eckt, Bug Collector
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes except the blue antlion!
                      Defeat all foes except the green antlion!
                      Defeat all foes except the white antlion!
Forbidden: Ice
           Fire
           Lightning
Rank: 30
Appears: After completing Quest C3-06 (Grounded!) and visiting Fluorgis.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Zedlei Forest
          The Bisga Greenlands
          Moorabella
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 15
                  Adaptability = 15
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 60 Clan Points
              Aptitude +2
Reward: 2650 Gil
        Fire Sigil (x4)
        Wind Sigil (x3)

For this quest, you have to go to three different locations and fight the 
battles there. The only stipulation of each battle is that you can't kill a 
certain color enemy (in this case, Antlions, as the petitioner described). 
The first battle takes place in Zedlei Forest, against two Antlions, a 
Chocobo, a Great Tortoise, and the blue Pit Beast. You need to defeat all the 
other enemies in order to capture the blue Pit Beast. The Chocobo tends to 
cure injured enemies, so you may want to eliminate it first. The Great 
Tortoise is the strongest of the pack, and the Antlions aren't too difficult 
at all. If you have strong attackers and can avoid mistakenly killing the 
blue Pit Beast, you're set here.

The next battle takes place in the Bisga Greenlands. This group consists 
entirely of Antlions this time, but the one you need to capture is the green 
one in the center of the formation. The proximity of the other enemies may 
make this a little more difficult, but once again the Antlions are not that 
difficult. You just need to be a bit more cautious about where you go and how 
you attack. If you have abilities such as Aurablast and Air Render, as well 
as good attack magick, it should be easy to pick off the ones you want. Once 
you defeat the other Antlions, the green Pit Beast is yours for the taking.

Now, for the final battle, you have to go to Moorabella. In addition to the 
white Pit Beast you must save, you need to fight off Werewolves, Lamias, and 
a Sprite. The Werewolves are physically strong, so bring some tough attackers 
to take them out quickly. The Lamias have their abilities which can cause 
adverse status effects, so you would want to defeat them from a distance. The 
Sprite is probably the lowest threat, since it basically goes around casting 
Reflect on the other enemies. It's a different group of monsters to defeat, 
but overall not too difficult. Once you clear them, the white Pit Beast is 
yours and the quest is finally over!

====================
D2-08: Fluffy Flier?
====================

Description: I saw someone fly over a volcano the other day! Flitting through
             the air right over the hot flowing lava, they were! My mom says
             I'm full of it, but I know what I saw. Could someone go check it
             out?
             -Uwattyo, Adventurous Boy
Quest Type: Investigation
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Summoning Scions
Rank: 38
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request) and visiting any town.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Neslowe Passage
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 44
                  Aptitude = 44
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 76 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 5410 Gil
        Emperor Scale

For this battle in this treacherous magma-filled area, you have to fight 
against three Sprites, a Banshee, Brown Chocobo, and a Fire Drake. The 
Sprites and Banshee are the biggest threats since they can all use Meteorite 
which can hit pretty hard. The Banshee can also use an ability which turns 
multiple targets into Stone; be careful of this one! Also, try to end this 
battle quickly since at the end of every round, the ground will shake, and 
after a few rounds everyone will start taking damage from it. Either way, 
once the enemies are gone, the quest is over.


=======================
D2-09: Cake: The Recipe
=======================

Description: I had a fight with my father the other day, and we haven't
             spoken a word since. I wanted to make up with him by baking one
             of my special carrot cakes for his birthday...but a monster took
             all six pages of my recipe! Please, someone, get them back for
             me!
             -Lea, Who is in truth fond of her father
Quest Type: Item Recovery
Victory Circumstance: Gather all the pages of the recipe!
Forbidden: Lightning
Rank: 27
Appears: After completing Quest C3-06 (Grounded!) and visiting Fluorgis.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Fluorgis
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 15
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 54 Clan Points
              Aptitude +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 2590 Gil
        Windslicer Pinion (x4)

Your goal out here is to recover the six pages of the cake recipe, as shown 
by the sparkling points on the ground. There are some enemies you need to get 
through in order to reach them all though (Axebeak, two Cockatrices, Bloody 
Orb, Lamia, and Adamantitan). You should defeat the Lamia first, especially 
since it's the closest to you on your path. If you have a Dragoon, you should 
be able to reach the higher ledge earlier and fight the enemies there. Be 
extremely careful of the Adamantitan though, as it can use Munch which will 
break your armor! The Cockatrices can be annoying with their abilities which 
can cast Haste and Quicken on themselves. They stay on the top level, so 
you'll be facing them last. Once you make it through the enemies and collect 
all of the stolen pages, this quest will be a success.

Out here in the desert, you have to face a Rocktitan, two Pit Beasts, two 
Cockatrices, and an Axebeak. The Cockatrices can be annoying since they can 
cast Haste on themselves and the Axebeak can turn your party members to 
Stone. The Pit Beasts and Rocktitan can dish out some powerful attacks as 
well, so you will want to bring some equally strong attackers to take care of 
that. Also, bring some long-range attackers as well as magick-users to make 
quick work of everything here. Regardless of how you do it, once you defeat 
everything here, the battle is over.

Description: That Killan has done it again! He's thrown my final exam papers

monsters, including Deadly Nightshades, a Sprite, Hoppy Bunny, and Dreamhare.

points on the ground. There are six papers to be gathered in total, and once

with, especially from a distance, so you should have no trouble here.

Description: Natural habitats in the Tramdine Fens are in danger! Cockatrice

For this quest, you have to do battle with five Cockatrices. They are all 
quite simple, though they can give themselves Haste status, which can be 
annoying when you're trying to defeat them quickly. As for their attacks, 
it's nothing really noteworthy to be concerned over. Just move in quickly and 
defeat them all to end this straightforward quest.


============================
D2-16: Cilawa the Gluttonous
============================

Description: I've thought up a new formula I'm eager to put to the test. I'll
             need someone to bring me a fresh rat tail for the mixture.
             -Cilawa the Gluttonous
Quest Type: Delivery
Rank: 5
Appears: After completing Quest B1-09 (Prepared with Love).
Price: 100 Gil
Location: Camoa
Days: 20
Required Items: Rat Tail
Required Talents: Negotiation = 4
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 10 Clan Points
Reward: 560 Gil
        Tanned Hide (x3)
        Ladies' Tresses (x2)
        Cloudy Sap (x3)


======================
D3-01: Gripped by Fear
======================

Description: You have flown aboard an airship? Seen the world from above the
             clouds and felt the cool wind on your face? I too wish to know
             what it is to feel this, but heights terrify me. I seek a
             companion to accompany me aboard an airship and help keep my
             fears at bay.
             -Arna the Superstitious
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Rank: 15
Appears: After completing Quest C3-11 (Rumors Abound).
Price: 300 Gil
Location: Moorabella
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 13
                  Aptitude = 13
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 30 Clan Points
              Negotiation +1
Reward: 1330 Gil
        Spider Silk (x3)

When you get to the Aerodrome, you will meet up with Arna. Ask her if she 
really is scared (the first option), then she will take the flight to 
Fluorgis and the quest will be a success.

=====================
D3-06: Drowsy Draught
=====================

Description: I once had trouble oversleeping and missing my classes, but a
             certain draught I'd rather not recall put an end to that. Oh how
             I miss those mornings spent drowsing in bed! I wish to return to
             my layabout ways, and prim draught is said to be just the thing
             I need. Please bring a succulent fruit and some sweet sap to the
             Witch of the Fens and have her prepare the draught for me!
             -Geldran the Once Drowsy
Quest Type: Delivery
Rank: 20
Appears: After completing Quest C3-16 (Sleepless Nights) and Quest D3-05
         (Rude Awakening).
Price: 300 Gil
Location: Fluorgis
Days: 20
Required Items: Succulent Fruit
                Sweet Sap
Required Talents: Negotiation = 20
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 40 Clan Points
              Negotiation +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 2580 Gil

Even though it is not stated in the quest location part, you still have to 
visit the Witch of the Fens. She is located in the Tramdine Fens area. After 
you get the draught from her, go to Geldran in the Fluorgis area to deliver 
it.


=========================
D3-07: Teach a Man to Run
=========================

Description: The ultimate fisherman needs no rod, line, or hook. All he needs
             is what he was born with. I am in training to become such a
             master, but I seem to have attracted something most unfortunate.
             Somebody help me!
             -Enchan, Perspiring Fisherman
Quest Type: Escort
Victory Circumstance: Protect Enchan and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Copycat
Rank: 37
Appears: After completing Quest E5-01 (The Dig), Quest D3-10 (Teach a Man to
         Fish), and visiting any town.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Tramdine Fens
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 22
                  Teamwork = 22
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 74 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 5150 Gil
        Bundle of Needles
        Potion
        Echo Herbs
        Ribbon

In this battle, you must again help Enchan, who needs assistance battling a 
giant Rafflesia. It can get annoying since the giant plant can shoot out 
seeds, which sprout into Malboros instantaneously to battle you. In addition 
to that, this mark can cause any surrounding units to fall asleep. Keep in 
mind that if you defeat the Malboro it shoots out, another one will be sent 
out right away, so don't waste too much time with that distraction. It helps 
a lot if you have long-range attacks, and especially fire-based abilities to 
quickly deplete its health. It has close to 2000 HP, so the battle may take a 
while; just be prepared to heal Enchan since he can't do anything for himself 
here. Either way, once you defeat the Rafflesia and the Malboro it shot out, 
the quest will be complete. As an added thanks, Enchan will give you a Potion 
and Echo Herbs, as well as the extremely important Ribbon!


=======================
D3-09: Cleaning to Loar
=======================

Description: Looking for helpers to swab an airship.
             We haven't had the crew to properly clean her for some time now.
             It would be a shame to put her out of service, so we'll have you
             cleaning her mid-flight. Oh, and watch out for the rats.
             -Jylland Airship Inspection Board
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Clean the airship within 4 rounds!
Forbidden: Lightning
Rank: 22
Appears: After completing Quest C3-06 (Grounded!) and visiting Fluorgis. You
         must be in Fluorgis to accept this quest.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Fluorgis
Days: 4
Required Talents: Aptitude = 1
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 44 Clan Points
              Aptitude +1
              Teamwork +1
Reward: 180 Gil
        Great Serpent's Fang (x2)

Aboard the airship headed for Moorabella, your job is to clean up all the 
dirty points (sparkling spots on the ground; three on the deck, one on the 
back right wing, and one on each of the front wings). As opposed to the 
Cleaning to Ordalia quest, it seems you are alone on this flight. It is 
imperative that you send only your six clan members with the greatest speed 
and especially range of movement for this quest. You will need to push two 
members to the far end of the ship as quickly as possible, to reach those far 
two swabbing points. You have until the end of the fourth round to complete 
the task, so if you have your characters in position on the far wings, you 
could keep an eye on the turn list on the top screen. Don't waste too much 
time though, the ship must be clean for you to succeed!


==========================
D3-10: Teach a Man to Fish
==========================

Description: The ultimate fisherman needs no rod, line, or hook. All he needs
             is what he was born with. I am in training to become such a
             master, but monsters keep intruding on my fishing hole. Someone
             drive them off!
             -Enchan, Aspiring Fisherman
Quest Type: Escort
Victory Circumstance: Protect Enchan and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Harming Nu Mou
Rank: 28
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request) and Quest B4-03 (I Want to
         Forget), and visiting any town.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Tramdine Fens
Days: 10
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Defender
Required Talents: Negotiation = 18
                  Teamwork = 18
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 56 Clan Points
              Negotiation +1
              Teamwork +1
Reward: 4260 Gil
        Screamroot

Out here in the swamp, you have to defend Enchan (a White Mage) against a 
slew of monsters, including a Wendigo, Hellhound, Adamantitan, Rocktitan, and 
Nagaraja. All of these enemies are strong physical attackers, with many of 
them being able to inflict status effects like Silence and Immobilize. You 
will need someone who can heal in case the monsters gang up on Enchan and you 
need to protect him; if he dies, the quest is a failure. Bring some strong 
attackers and magick-users (the Wendigo is weak against Lightning) to quickly 
bring down these enemies, and the quest will be a success.


==================
D3-11: Love-struck
==================

Description: I was developing a love philtre for my studies, but a classmate
             drank the potion before I could complete it and has come down
             with a terrible fever. I need someone to ask the Witch of the
             Fens to make a potion to cool the fever before my classmate's
             condition grows worse. The ingredients needed are silk bloom and
             malboro wine. Thanks! (And hurry!)
             -Kuleek, Moorabella Magick Akademy

Rank: 23
Appears: After completing Quest D4-01 (Making Music) and Quest D3-06 (Drowsy
         Draught).
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Moorabella
Days: 20
Required Items: Silk Bloom
                Malboro Wine
Required Talents: Negotiation = 22
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 46 Clan Points
              Negotiation +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 2910 Gil

Once again, although it is not explicitly stated in the quest's location, you 
must first visit the Witch of the Fens located in the Tramdine Fens area. She 
will make the potion you need, which you bring to Kuleek in Moorabella to 
complete the quest.


=========================

Description: My unfinished love philtre seems to have taken premature effect,
             and my classmate has become infatuated with me!
             Though I must confess I am somewhat pleased by this, I am left

             I need someone to ask the Witch of the Fens to make an antidote

             Thanks! (And...don't hurry too much.)

the Fens, located at Tramdine Fens first. After she makes the antidote, bring
