=================================
D3-15: Rancher's Request - Yellow
=================================

Description: I'm big on chocobos. So big, I decided to build a chocobo ranch.
             All well and good, right? Wrong! I spent so much on the ranch, I
             didn't have anything left to buy chocobos!
             That's why I need you to go out and catch me a wild one. Yellow
             should do just fine.
             -Yew, Chocobo Rancher
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Deliver a yellow chocobo to Yew!
Rank: 21
Appears: After completing Quest C3-01 (Mountain Watch) and visiting
         Moorabella.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Targ Wood
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 13
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 42 Clan Points
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 180 Gil
        Spiral Vine (x3)
        Kempas (x3)

For this quest, you must bring the Chocobo Rancher a Yellow Chocobo. You are 
required to have a Chocobo Knight in order to carry this out, plus you need 
to already have captured the Chocobo prior to doing this quest. The best 
place to search is in the Targ Wood region. When the Fey Mischief encounter 
appears, enter the battle and defeat all the other enemies except the 
Chocobo. Then, weaken the Chocobo to critical health and move your Chocobo 
Knight next to it. Mount it to capture, then bring it here to complete the 
quest.


================================
D3-16: Rancher's Request - Black
================================

Description: My ranch is up and running, but with only one chocobo, it seems
             even emptier than before! That's why I'm asking you to catch
             another wild chocobo for me! A black chocobo should do nicely.
             -Yew, Chocobo Rancher
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Deliver a black chocobo to Yew!
Rank: 25
Appears: After completing Quest C3-06 (Grounded!) and Quest D3-15 (Rancher's
         Request - Yellow).
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Targ Wood
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 15
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 50 Clan Points
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 1750 Gil
        Kuraisle Boxwood (x2)

For this quest, you must bring the Chocobo Rancher a Black Chocobo. You are 
required to have a Chocobo Knight in order to carry this out, plus you need 
to already have captured the Chocobo prior to doing this quest. The best 
place to search is in the Galleria Deep region during the month of Coppersun. 
When the One-eyed Evil encounter appears, enter the battle and defeat all the 
other enemies except the Chocobo. Then, weaken the Chocobo to critical health 
and move your Chocobo Knight next to it. Mount it to capture, then bring it 
here to complete the quest.

================================
D4-04: Hors D'oeuvre of the Hour
================================

Description: Haven't tried Culinary Crusade's latest gastronomical triumph,
             Amarette Malbonara yet? Now's your chance! Just be careful not
             to burn the ingredients when you harvest them. Heat muddles the
             flavor.
             -Grosso, Culinary Crusade
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Uphold the law and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Fire
Rank: 41
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request) and visiting any town.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Bisga Greenlands
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 39
                  Adaptability = 39
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 82 Clan Points
              Aptitude +2
              Teamwork +2
Reward: 3980 Gil
        Ancient Turtle Shell (x2)

Here, you have to defeat three Malboros and a Malboro King. As you know, when 
dealing with Malboros, you need to keep your distance to avoid their long-
range attacks which can inflict various status effects on your clan. The only 
catch is that you cannot use fire-based attacks as requested by the quest 
petitioner himself. If you use ranged attacks of your own to pick off these 
enemies one by one, it will definitely help make this battle easier and allow 
you to win. After you defeat all four of these enemies, the quest is over.

===========================
D4-07: I've Been Had, Kupo!
===========================

Description: Kupo!!! I've been had, kupo, had!!!
             "Super special hammer," my pom-pom! This is just an ungainly
             lump of iron! That alchemist pulled a fast one on me!
             Someone get that ne'er-do-well and take back my 20,000 gil,
             kupo! His name's Nezzel!
             -Craftsmoogles' League Foreman
Quest Type: Defeat Mark
Victory Circumstance: Defeat Nezzel the Alchemist!
Forbidden: Height >= 10
Rank: 32
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request) and visiting any town. As
         an additional note, you must complete this Quest and Quest E5-16
         (The Ritual) in order to access the Quests to unlock Al-Cid and
         other Quests that require game completion as a prerequisite to
         unlock.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Bisga Greenlands
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 28
                  Adaptability = 28
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 64 Clan Points
              Negotiation +2
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 1960 Gil
        Kalos (x3)

Here, you have to do battle with Nezzel and his group in the mountains. They 
consist of a Green Mage, Thief, Black Mage, White Monk, Time Mage, and of 
course an Alchemist. The biggest threat by far is the Alchemist, since his 
Flare attack can be quite painful. The Black Mage also has higher-level 
magicks which you need to be concerned over as well, but he is far away so 
you have time before you have to worry about it. You only have to beat Nezzel 
in order to complete the quest; the rest of your kills can be for extra loot 
and such. After the battle, you will meet another Alchemist who will give you 
a card which makes it so no enemy can dispel your Judge!


========================
D4-08: Beneath the Sands
========================

Description: Need someone to head over to Kithili Sands and look for my
             treasure. Buried it out there a chocobo's age ago, and now I
             can't remember where it's at. Went looking for it myself, but
             didn't have any luck. Maybe you'll do better.
             -Ricard, Former treasure hunter
Quest Type: Item Recovery
Victory Circumstance: Find the buried treasure!
Forbidden: Summoning Scions
Rank: 40
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request) and visiting any town.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Kthili Sands
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 39
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 80 Clan Points
              Aptitude +2
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 6270 Gil
        Wyvern Wing

In this area, there are six sparkling spots on the ground where the 
petitioner's treasure may be buried. You need to check each spot to find out 
where the buried treasure is hidden, but of course you have to deal with some 
monsters along the way (Thunder Drake, two Pit Beasts, Yellow Jelly, and a 
Brown Chocobo). There are some hazards in the form of hidden traps, which 
cause Charm status, so you may want a Ranger with Awareness to help with 
that. The Thunder Drake and Yellow Jelly can use lightning-based attacks to 
heal themselves and hurt you, and the Brown Chocobo can cause Regen status on 
itself and its allies, so try and take it out quickly. You don't have to kill 
the enemies, but it's useful for extra loot as well as clearing the way to 
the potential treasure locations. Once you find the treasure, your job here 
is done.


======================
D4-09: Airship S.O.S.!
======================

Description: No one's noticed yet, but an airship sitting in the dock has
             been hijacked. I don't want to contact the watch and cause a
             commotion, so I'm posting for help here.
             -Neah, Accidental Witness
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Being Robbed
Rank: 19
Appears: After completing Quest D4-01 (Making Music) and visiting Moorabella.
Price: 300 Gil
Location: Moorabella
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 13
                  Adaptability = 13
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 38 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 2960 Gil
        Gurnat (x2)
        Strange Liquid (x4)

Here, you get to go against the hijackers of the airship face to face. The 
law may be tricky to uphold, seeing as your enemies are Soldiers and Thieves! 
It's not too big of a deal if you break the law, but if you want to uphold 
it, stick to long-range attackers and magick-users. The enemies here are 
quite easy and at a low level for this point in the game, so you should have 
quite an easy time taking them out and saving the hostages.

====================
D4-12: A Small Favor
====================

Description: I require an ether. Bring me one, won't you?
             -Master Metallurgist
Quest Type: Delivery
Rank: 30
Appears: After completing Quest E5-16 (The Ritual), Quest B4-03 (I Want to
         Forget), and Side Quest "Gifted".
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Tramdine Fens
Days: 20
Required Items: Ether
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 60 Clan Points
              Negotiation +2
Reward: 7880 Gil
        Wyvern Wing

When you come to the location at Tramdine Fens, you will find a note instead 
of the petitioner. It will ask you to visit another location to meet up with 
him (this location changes each time you accept the quest). Head to the 
location that fits the description and you will meet who you are looking for. 
Deliver the Ether and the quest will be complete. The list below consists of 
those locations along with their descriptions. Once you complete this quest 
five times, that is it.

    Goug = The city to the south
    Nazan Mines = Where the sun begins its march across the sky
    The Ruins of Delgantua = Land where the sun sets
    Zedlei Forest = Northern reaches of the Strait of Lumes
    Zellea, the Forbidden Land = Island at the end of the world


================================
D4-14: Ordalia Airships Grounded
================================

Description: A pack of bombs from Sant D'alsa Bluff is posing a threat to the
             aerodrome. If they detonate near even one of the airships moored
             there, the entire fleet could go up in flames. Destroy them all
             before it's too late!
             -Ash, Airship Pilot
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Targeting Distant Units
Rank: 25
Appears: After completing Quest D4-06 (Seeking the Stone) and Quest A2-10
         (Odd Places). You must be in Fluorgis to accept this quest.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Fluorgis
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 15
                  Adaptability = 15
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 50 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
Reward: 4610 Gil
        Strange Liquid (x2)

In this battle, you have to face three Bombs, two Red Marshmallows and a 
Grenade aboard an airship. This can be a little bit difficult, especially 
since the enemies can inflict Oil status, plus they all have fire-based 
attacks which heal themselves and hurt you. You will do well to have a mage 
with water-based attacks, but be cautious when you get any of them to 
critical health. The bomb enemies tend to self-destruct when they have low 
health, causing massive fire damage to anyone nearby. Once you manage to 
destroy all of these creatures, the quest will be complete.

==========================
D5-01: Graszton Nightwatch
==========================

Description: A plague of robberies has fallen upon the land! All occur at
             night and follow a similar pattern, indicating that a single
             group may be responsible. For the swift resolution of this case,
             and the safety of our citizens, we are currently accepting
             applications to join the Graszton Nightwatch.
             -Jylland Sovereignty Society
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes within four rounds!
Forbidden: Targeting Distant Units
Rank: 40
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request) and visiting any town.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Graszton
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 44
                  Teamwork = 44
                  Adaptability = 44
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 80 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
Reward: 6620 Gil
        Stormsoul Crystal

In this quest, you have to defeat three Baknamys and a Luchorpan to defend 
Graszton. This time, you will be helped by Chita's Weaponers (two Warriors 
and a Gladiator). You have to defeat these enemies within four rounds, but 
that won't be an issue at all given the help you're getting from the other 
clan. Nonetheless, bring some good attackers that can move quickly and you'll 
be pretty much set here. Just defeat the enemies within four rounds and the 
quest will be complete!


===========================
D5-02: The Camoa Nightwatch
===========================

Description: A plague of robberies has fallen upon the land! All occur at
             night and follow a similar pattern, indicating that a single
             group may be responsible. For the swift resolution of this case,
             and the safety of our citizens, we are currently accepting
             applications to join the Camoa Nightwatch.
             -Jylland Sovereignty Society
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes within four rounds!
Forbidden: Targeting Self
Rank: 38
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request) and visiting any town.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Camoa
Days: 20
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 76 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
Reward: 6620 Gil
        Stradivari

For this battle to defend Camoa, you have to defeat three Baknamys and a 
Luchorpan. Helping you out in this battle are the Camoa Braves (two White 
Monks and a Warrior). Of course, you have to defeat all of the enemies within 
four rounds, but with the added help, this is easily doable. Deploy the units 
who have the highest Move statistics, since you will need to get across the 
area to quickly reach the far off monsters. Either way, they are quite simple 
to fight and don't pose any real threat, so beat them within four rounds to 
clear this quest.


================
D5-03: Stowaways
================

Description: There are murmurings among our passengers that there are ghosts
             aboard the airships.
             Though understandably concerned, we are yet mindful that rumor
             is not fact. We need someone trustworthy to investigate, and, in
             the event that there is a ghostly infestation, remedy the
             problem with all haste.
             -Jylland Airship Inspection Board
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Solitude
Rank: 23
Appears: After completing Quest D4-01 (Making Music) and reading the Notice
         "Spirits in the Sky" at the Pub.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Fluorgis
Days: 20
Recommended Job (Dispatch): White Monk
Required Talents: Teamwork = 15
                  Adaptability = 15
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 46 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
Reward: 2610 Gil
        Wyrm Carapace (x4)

You will be fighting this battle in midflight aboard the airship. The enemies 
consist of Ahrimans, Ghosts, a Bloody Orb, and a Deathscythe. The most 
dangerous of them are the Ahrimans, due to the status effects they can 
inflict on you, most notably Charm, Confuse, and Slow. Other than that, it's 
a typical battle against undead enemies, who will mainly use the magick Dark 
to attack, or try to drain your health with another ability. As always, keep 
in mind that once you deplete the undead enemy's health to 0 HP, you must use 
Raise or a similar ability/item to fully destroy it; that way it doesn't come 
back to life in a couple turns. Once you manage to defeat the enemies aboard 
the airship, the quest will be complete and you will now be in Moorabella.


========================
D5-05: Wanted: Devotees!
========================

Description: Wanted: The criminals known as the Devotees!
             -Duo responsible for several acts of theft.
             -Thought to be involved in arms deals.
             -Thought to be followers of a certain band of musicians.
             -Jylland Sovereignty Society
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat the Devotees!
Forbidden: Ranged Weapons
Rank: 25
Appears: After completing Quest A2-06 (The Stone With No Name), Quest C5-04
         (Moorabella Nightwatch), Quest C5-08 (Goug Nightwatch), Quest D5-01
         (Graszton Nightwatch), Quest D5-02 (The Camoa Nightwatch), and Quest
         D5-06 (Fluorgis Nightwatch).
Price: 400 Gil
Location: The Ruins of Delgantua
Days: 20
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 50 Clan Points
              Negotiation +1
              Teamwork +1
Reward: 5130 Gil
        Aurea Pollen

In this battle, you have to defeat not only the Devotee and Devotee Jr. 
(Lanista and Time Mage), but you have to beat two Baknamys and a Luchorpan as 
well. Before the battle, you confront them with proof they were behind the 
robberies. For each of the five papers you read, pick the answer with "Prima 
Donna" in it to correctly proceed. As for the battle, the monsters are the 
most difficult of all, yet they are simple to beat since they don't really 
have abilities worth noting. The Devotees themselves are very low-level, so 
you can easily dispatch them once you get to where they're hiding. When you 
defeat everyone here, the quest will be complete.


==========================
D5-06: Fluorgis Nightwatch
==========================

Description: A plague of robberies has fallen upon the land! All occur at
             night and follow a similar pattern, indicating that a single
             group may be responsible. For the swift resolution of this case,
             and the safety of our citizens, we are currently accepting
             applications to join the Fluorgis Nightwatch.
             -Jylland Sovereignty Society
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes within four rounds!
Forbidden: Swimming
Rank: 43
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request) and visiting any town.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Fluorgis
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 44
                  Teamwork = 44
                  Adaptability = 44
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 86 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
Reward: 6620 Gil
        High Arcana

Here, you have to do battle against three Baknanys and a Luchorpan. The catch 
is that you have to defeat them all in four rounds. Joining you in this 
battle is House Bowen, which will certainly make killing the enemies in four 
rounds or less that much easier. You should deploy clan members with high 
Jump statistics, since it will make navigating Fluorgis a lot easier. With 
Bowen's help, you will definitely have this cleared in the time allowed; the 
enemies don't hurt you too much, and you heavily outnumber them as well.


=======================
D5-08: A Lost Companion
=======================

Description: Got a strange letter today at the pub from someone named Gade.
             Whoever Gade is, it sounds like a friend of his named Shoofa is
             lost on a "snowy plain." I'm pretty sure the letter came to us
             by accident, but now it's got me curious.
Quest Type: Defeat Mark
Victory Circumstance: Defeat Gade!
Forbidden: Debuffs
Rank: 25
Appears: After completing Side Quest "Gifted" and reading the Notice "A Lost
         Friend" at the Pub.
Price: N/A
Location: The Rupie Mountains
Days: N/A
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 50 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 3940 Gil
        Tiptaptwo

Here, you will have to battle Gade, who happens to be a Wraith, accompanied 
by Ghosts and Zombies. You only have to defeat Gade in order to win this 
battle. Keep in mind that all of your enemies are undead, so you need to 
destroy their tombstones at 0 HP by using a Phoenix Down or something 
similar. As far as their attacks are concerned, they all have the typical 
abilities that can inflict status effects, such as Sleep, Silence, and 
Poison. Either way, the enemies here are nothing to be too concerned over, so 
concentrate on defeating Gade quickly. Once you get him down to 0 HP, the 
battle will end. Adelle will then receive the memento from the Moogle, which 
happens to be the Tiptaptwo, allowing Adelle to learn the Viola ability as a 
Heritor!


============
D5-12: Help!
============

Description: We got a letter today from a man named Wermut, some old guy who
             hurt himself out in the swamp. He wants us to bring him a
             potion, so let's make sure we've got at least one to spare
             before heading out there.
Quest Type: Delivery
Rank: 42
Appears: After completing Quest D5-08 (A Lost Companion), having Adelle
         master the Viola ability (Tiptaptwo), and reading the Notice "Send
         Help!" at the Pub.
Price: N/A
Location: Zedlei Forest
Days: N/A
Required Items: Potion
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 84 Clan Points
              Negotiation +3
Reward: 160 Gil
        Whale Whisker

Here, Adelle will meet with the old man Wermut. He is injured with a twisted 
ankle, so Adelle gives him the Potion to help. As thanks, Wermut will give 
her the Whale Whisker. After Adelle leaves, you will witness a conversation 
between Wermut and someone named Ljda before the quest is complete.


======================
D5-13: Bringer of Doom
======================

Description: Came across a worrying notice in the pub about a creature
             threatening the town of Goug.
             Hard to know whether this prophet Hilo can be trusted, but it
             may be a good idea to take a look, just to be on the safe side.
Quest Type: Defeat Mark
Victory Circumstance: Defeat the Smoldering Incubus!
Forbidden: Reaction Abilities
Rank: 45
Appears: After completing Quest D5-14 (The Shrine of the Paling Gods), having
         Adelle master the Elpe ability (Hyakushiki-masamune) as a Heritor,
         and reading the Notice "Calamity Cometh" at the Pub.
Price: N/A
Location: Goug
Days: N/A
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 90 Clan Points
              Teamwork +3
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 10240 Gil
        Gold Chalice
        Chirijiraden

When you arrive here, you will meet the Prophet Hilo face to face. He will 
give Adelle the Chirijiraden sword, which will come in handy when battling 
the Smoldering Incubus at the top of the area. When you select your clan 
members for the battle, make sure to equip Adelle with her new weapon. 
Anyway, you will want all your long-range attackers in this battle, since you 
can't get directly next to the enemy for a closer hit. As for its attacks, 
you must bring people with Ribbons and Orbs of Minwu equipped, since the 
Incubus can inflict Charm/Doom status on multiple people at once. If you 
equipped Adelle with her new weapon like I said you should, use the Hilo 
ability to attack from afar. It will be a long battle, especially since the 
mark's attacks are extremely powerful, but if you have someone healing and 
able to revive fallen allies, you should be able to recover nicely. Once you 
defeat the giant beast, the quest will be complete.


====================================
D5-14: The Shrine of the Paling Gods
====================================

Description: Came across a worrying notice in the pub about something strange
             happening at the shrines of the Paling Gods in Tramdine Fens. It
             sounds like there has been a growing number of monster sightings
             in the area. Might be worth looking into.
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Rekindle the power of the stones!
Forbidden: Harming the Weak
Rank: 38
Appears: After completing Quest D5-15 (The Beast of Aisenfield), having
         Adelle master the Nesiaam ability (Nagrarok) as a Heritor, and
         reading the Notice "The Shrine of the Paling Gods" at the Pub.
Price: N/A
Location: Tramdine Fens
Days: N/A
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 76 Clan Points
              Aptitude +3
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 8650 Gil
        Hyakushiki-masamune

Over here, you will find a number of monsters, including Malboros, a Great 
Malboro, a Green Chocobo, and a Black Chocobo. There are also three strange 
pillars in the area, and your goal is to go to each and empower them. As for 
the enemies, the Malboros are the most dangerous due to their abilities which 
can inflict status effects on you. You should send in clan members with 
accessories like the Ninja Tabi, so that you can quickly get across the area 
and power up the pillars. Once you do that, the quest wil end. You will also 
receive the next weapon for Adelle, the Hyakushiki-masamune.


==============================
D5-15: The Beast of Aisenfield
==============================

Description: Read a tale about a man who possessed a terrible power. Those he
             knew turned against him, and over time he became a beast. If the
             story's true, maybe he still stalks Aisenfield?
Quest Type: Defeat Mark
Victory Circumstance: Defeat Nesiaam!
Forbidden: < 20 Damage
Rank: 36
Appears: After completing Quest D5-16 (Woman of the Wood), having Adelle
         master the Ljda ability (Ayvuir Blue) as a Heritor, and reading the
         Notice "The Beast of Aisenfield" at the Pub.
Price: N/A
Location: Aisenfield
Days: N/A
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 72 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 6300 Gil
        Nagrarok

In this area, Adelle will be confronted by Nesiaam, who is now in the form of 
a Zahak. He is accompanied by two Fire Drakes, a Headless, Axebeak, and a 
Rocktitan. You only have to defeat Nesiaam though. The Zahak itself is strong 
physically, and its attacks all have elemental effects. The Axebeak can use 
Quicken on other enemies (Wake-Up Call), and the Fire Drakes can use 
Mesmerize to Charm you. Also, the Rocktitan can use Headbutt if it gets close 
enough, which may Immobilize its target. Each enemy has its negative aspects, 
but the Fire Drakes are the greatest threats, so on your way to the Zahak, 
you should probably kill them first. Once you defeat Nesiaam, you will 
receive the Nagrarok, and the quest will end!


========================
D5-16: Woman of the Wood
========================

Description: Came across a worrying notice in the pub about a woman
             surrounded by monsters in the woods. If she's still there, and
             still alive, she may well need help.
Quest Type: Defeat Mark
Victory Circumstance: Defeat Ljda!
Forbidden: Knockback
Rank: 31
Appears: After completing Quest D5-12 (Help!), having Adelle master the
         Wermut ability (Whale Whisker) as a Heritor, and reading the Notice
         "Screaming Beauty" at the Pub.
Price: N/A
Location: Moorabella
Days: N/A
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 62 Clan Points
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 5430 Gil
        Ayvuir Blue

In this area, Luso and Adelle will spot a Viera apparently under attack by 
some monsters. It is actually Ljda, who summons more monsters to attack you. 
Your objective here is to defeat Ljda only, but the others may get in the 
way, so you will probably have to defeat them as well (Fire Drake, Ice Drake, 
Thunder Drake, Banshee, and White Chocobo). These enemies have their usual 
attacks, but the Banshee is the most dangerous with a Holy attack that can 
hit everyone that's a certain level, as well as Meteorite. Ljda herself is an 
Elementalist who can use abilities that may inflict status effects upon you, 
most specifically Disable (Fire Whip). If you can move quickly and attack 
her, you should be able to win early on, ending this battle early.


============================
E1-01: Bonga Bugle - Goldsun
============================

Description: Greetings! Bonga Bugle Head Editor here!
             This month's special: the Field of Hidden Treasures! A place
             where treasures are said to spring into being beneath the
             ground...all by themselves!
             Reporting assistants wanted.
             -Head Editor, Bonga Bugle
Quest Type: Meet Objectives
Victory Circumstance: Find three treasures!
Forbidden: Attack
Rank: 22
Appears: After completing Quest B2-11 (Now That's a Fire!) and reading the
         Notice "The Bonga Bugle" in the Pub, during the month of Goldsun.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Baptiste Hill
Days: 3
Required Talents: Adaptability = 9
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 44 Clan Points
              Aptitude +2
Reward: 1750 Gil
        Recall Grass

When you arrive here, you will find the Head Editor who wants to send you on 
a treasure hunt. He will give you a Treasure Detector, which will help you 
find the hidden treasure. To use it, simply move around the field and when 
you are at a treasure site, the option to check the detector will appear. 
When you check it, it will say whether there is a small or large treasure to 
be dug up. Larger ones are generally worth more, so it's best to go for those 
instead (you have the option to not dig up something if you detect it). After 
you dig up three treasures, the quest is over.

E1-02: Bonga Bugle - Silversun
==============================

Description: Greetings! Bonga Bugle Head Editor here!
             This month, we're taking a look at haunted spots, starting with
             that most forbidding of places, Shadeholme!
             ...Um, someone go with me, please!
             Note: the actual location of our report will be top secret!
             -Head Editor, Bonga Bugle
Quest Type: Escort
Victory Circumstance: Defend the Head Editor and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Copycat
Rank: 18

         "The Bonga Bugle" in the Pub, during the month of Silversun.

Location: Graszton

                  Teamwork = 7

              Teamwork +1

When you arrive at this location, you will see that there are plenty of 
Ghosts and Deathscythes around. You will be tasked with protecting the Head 
Editor from these creatures while you defeat them all. If you have someone 
who can use Black Magick, you will be in rather good shape here. Also, 
remember that you can use recovery items and Cure spells to cause damage to 
them as well. It is also important to remind you that when you defeat them, 
in order to remove the tombstone (so they don't come back to battle some 
more), you need to use a Phoenix Down or an equivalent ability/spell to 
totally destroy it. Once you banish all of the undead, the quest is complete.


============================
E1-03: Bonga Bugle - Ashleaf
============================

Description: Greetings! Bonga Bugle Head Editor here!
             This month, I'll be reporting on Galmia Pepe, fashion mavens
             known for their novel designs and commitment to quality.
             We'll be conducting some stealth interviews to get to the bottom
             of their unparalleled popularity!
             Reporting assistants wanted.
             -Head Editor, Bonga Bugle
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Help the Bonga Bugle get its scoop!
Forbidden: Ranged Weapons
Rank: 22
Appears: After completing Quest B2-16 (Pearls in the Deep) and reading the
         Notice "The Bonga Bugle" in the Pub, during the month of Ashleaf.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Camoa
Days: 8
Required Talents: Negotiation = 11
                  Adaptability = 11
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 44 Clan Points
              Negotiation +2
              Teamwork +1
Reward: 3890 Gil
        Zinconium (x2)
        Cloudy Sap (x2)

For this edition of the Bonga Bugle, you are there to help the Head Editor 
get an interview. However, the Jylland Free Press is there as well trying to 
beat the Bonga Bugle to it. The opposing party consists of a Ninja, Time 
Mage, Geomancer, and Green Mage. You don't have to actually defeat them 
though; the goal is to get to the Galmia P.R. person first. You may want to 
defeat the Time Mage so it can't use Haste and Quicken on its party members. 
Move your fastest party members to the upper area as quickly as you can so 
you can reach the Illusionist first. Be sure to take the treasure by the Head 
Editor, as it contains Brigand's Gloves! You simply have to move to the space 
directly in front of the P.R. person to win this quest.

E1-04: Bonga Bugle - Mistleaf
=============================

Description: Greetings! Bonga Bugle Head Editor here!
             This month's special feature: Unlimited Power! What power? Power
             in battle! What battles? Clan battles! We'll be measuring clan
             power, comparing the clans, and posting our results! Looking for
             clans to participate in this event!
             -Head Editor, Bonga Bugle
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!

Days: 8

                  Adaptability = 33

        Onion

For this quest, you are asked to do battle with a variety of monsters, 
including a Hoppy Bunny, Nidhogg, Malboro, Deathscythe, and Werewolf. The 
Nidhogg and Werewolf are the physical attackers, so send a couple of melee 
attackers to take care of them quickly. The rest of the enemies though have 
abilities which can inflict some rough status effects, so try to take care of 
them from a distance so you stay safe. Once you defeat all of the monsters, 
the Head Editor will thank you and give you a weapon as an added reward (if 
you finish it more quickly, you may get a different weapon as a reward; I 
received the Brilliant Theorbo personally, but you can also get the Nirvana).


==============================
E1-05: Bonga Bugle - Coppersun
==============================

Description: Greetings from the Bonga Bugle!
             This month we're taking a very long, very close look at Prima
             Donna! Is there anyone who doesn't know the incredibly popular
             and talented ladies of this singing group? There won't be after
             this month's issue of the Bonga Bugle! Assistants wanted.
             -Head Editor, Bonga Bugle
             *Selection by interview. P.D. fanatics preferred.
Quest Type: Meet Objectives
Victory Circumstance: Protect the Head Editor and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Harming Seeq
Rank: 30
Appears: After completing Quest C3-16 (Sleepless Nights) and reading the
         Notice "The Bonga Bugle" in the Pub, during the month of Coppersun.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Moorabella
Days: 4
Ability Points: 10 (interview)
                30 (battle)
Clan Rewards: 60 Clan Points
              Negotiation +2
Reward: 2 Gil (interview only)
        4590 Gil
        Holy Stone (x4)
        Damascus (x2)
        Faerie Wing (x2)

When you come here, you will be interviewed by the Head Editor about the 
Prima Donna group. Pick the last option and you will be hired to continue on 
to Fluorgis for the reporting part of the quest. When you arrive over there, 
you will be put into a battle against the kidnappers you fought in another 
quest, and are looking to kidnap Prima Donna! Now that the enemies realize 
how important the Head Editor is, they're going to aim for him, so you must 
protect him; if he dies, the quest is a failure.

As for the enemies, you are up against an Archer, Thief, Hunter, and Blue 
Mage. Additionally, the Prima Donna group are on your side fighting the 
enemy, so you have the added support from them too. The Hunter and Archer are 
most dangerous since they can attack faraway targets. The other two enemies 
can be taken out rather easily, especially since you have such a great force 
of allies here. Once you defeat the would-be kidnappers, the Head Editor will 
have his scoop and this quest will come to an end.

==============================

Description: Greetings from the Bonga Bugle!

             crime syndicates!

When you meet up with the Head Editor, you will be subject to an interview. 
Pick the third option (the howling like a wolf one) and you will be hired to 
go to the specified location and start "reporting". When you get to that 
location, you will be put into a battle against a random rival clan. The 
battles aren't too difficult, so prepare for these like any other; you need 
to protect the Head Editor though, so a healer will be quite useful here. The 
rewards you get for defeating the rival clan are the same regardless of who 
you actually fight.

E1-09: Bonga Bugle - Rosefire

Description: Greetings! Bonga Bugle Head Editor here!
             This month's special: The Master Potter. I'll be photographing
             a pot on loan from master potsmith Master LePot the 3rd!

Here in the forest, you have a task from the Bonga Bugle to accomplish. There 
are five pots, and you must arrange them on five stumps in the middle of the 
area. However, there are enemies in the area, and more keep coming after 
every few turns. Therefore, it's really not worth killing them, and you 
should just worry about placing the urns on the stumps. If an enemy is in 
your way, then attack it; otherwise just focus on the stumps. Once you place

against a random group of monsters (Chocobos in The Rupie Mountains; Bombs in 
Fluorgis; Worgens, Rocktitan, and Tonberry in Nazan Mines). Set up a strong 
party to counter what's waiting for you at your destination. Once you defeat 
all the enemies, while defending the Head Editor and Owner of course (they 
tend to try and attack the enemies as well, be ready to heal FAST), you will 
successfully complete the quest.

E1-13: Bonga Bugle - Bloodfire

Description: Greetings! Bonga Bugle Head Editor here!

     0: Knot of Rust

E1-14: Bonga Bugle - Greenfire
==============================

Description: Greetings from the Bonga Bugle!
             This month we'll be looking at rare and unusual laws! All laws
             are equal, but it turns out that some laws -are- more equal than
             others! I'll need assistants, of course.
             -Head Editor, Bonga Bugle
             *Selection by interview. The secret password is "simply lovely"!
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Uphold the law and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Being Robbed
Rank: 29
Appears: After completing Quest C3-11 (Rumors Abound) and reading the Notice
         "The Bonga Bugle" in the Pub, during the month of Greenfire.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Moorabella
Days: 4
Ability Points: 10 (interview)
                30 (battle)
Clan Rewards: 56 Clan Points
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 2 Gil (interview only)
        3030 Gil
        Onion
        Agathis
        Dipraeu Bronze

When you arrive, you will be subject to an interview by the Head Editor. Tell 
him the password "simply lovely" and you will be hired to go reporting in 
Fluorgis. When you head to Fluorgis, you'll have to enter battle against 
three Thieves, a Soldier, and a Viking. You must uphold the law, which is to 
not get robbed, so you need to keep these enemies at bay. Use a Ranger who 
can lay traps (Sten Needle in particular), as well as a Fusilier or Trickster 
to attack from a distance. If you have an Elementalist with Fire Whip, they 
will be VERY useful here in trying to Disable the enemies. Nonetheless, when 
you defeat everyone here while upholding the law, you will clear the quest.


=============================
E1-15: Bonga Bugle - Skyfrost
=============================

Description: Greetings from the Bonga Bugle!
             This month we'll be taking a look at special places, traveling
             far and wide across Jylland to find the best and the most
             beautiful! And I'll need assistants!
             -Head Editor, Bonga Bugle
             *Selection by interview. Cool and collected applicants
              preferred.
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Protect the Head Editor and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Buffs
Rank: 31
Appears: After completing Quest C3-06 (Grounded!) and reading the Notice "The
         Bonga Bugle" in the Pub, during the month of Skyfrost.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Moorabella
Days: 4
Ability Points: 10 (interview)
                30 (battle)
Clan Rewards: 64 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 2 Gil (interview only)
        4940 Gil
        Hedychium
        Black Thread

When you come to the location, you will be interviewed by the Head Editor. He 
will start to tell a joke, and then you have the option to respond. Pick the 
last option, "*smirk*", and you will get hired. He will then tell you to go 
to the Ruins of Delgantua to start reporting, so head there and you will 
enter a battle.

You will be fighting against five Viera (Elementalist, White Mage, Assassin, 
Green Mage, Sniper). If you are well-prepared, you should be able to kill the 
Assassin first since she is closest to where your party starts. The White 
Mage and Elementalist need to go quickly as well due to their ability to heal 
and damage you. The Sniper has an ability which casts Regen as soon as she 
gets damaged, which means it may be a slightly longer fight with her, but you 
can easily win it. You need to protect the Head Editor from damage as well, 
so if his health runs low, heal him!


===============================
E1-16: Bonga Bugle - Blackfrost
===============================

Description: Happy New Year from the Bonga Bugle!
             We're doing a special on New Year's resolutions, and what better
             place to conduct a survey than where all the people are: in
             Moorabella!
             Calling all those willing to assist this noblest of causes.
             -Head Editor, Bonga Bugle
Quest Type: Meet Objectives
Victory Circumstance: Survey New Year's resolutions!
Forbidden: Attack
Rank: 19
Appears: After completing Quest C3-01 (Mountain Watch) and reading the Notice
         "The Bonga Bugle" in the Pub, during the month of Blackfrost.
Price: 300 Gil
Location: Moorabella
Days: 8
Required Talents: Negotiation = 13
                  Adaptability = 13
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 38 Clan Points
              Negotiation +1
              Teamwork +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 8750 Gil
        Adamant Alloy (x3)
        Hedychium

For this edition of the Bonga Bugle, your job is to survey the townsfolk 
about their New Year's resolutions. You will have to deploy your clan members 
around Moorabella and talk to everyone outside, and even go up to doors and 
knock on them to talk to the people who are inside. You need to find out what 
the most popular resolution is (it is random, so you can't just guess it). 
When you're confident in your answer (there are 13 possible people you can 
ask, in case you want to deduce it that way), talk to the Head Editor and 
give him your answer. If you are correct, you will complete the quest.


=====================
E2-05: Survey No. 258
=====================

Description: Wanted: Researchers to assist with geological survey of the
             Galleria Deep.
             Please survey the area assigned and report your findings.
             -Jylland Geological Survey Committee
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Survey points of geological interest!
Forbidden: Bludgeoning Weapons
Rank: 24
Appears: After completing Quest C3-01 (Mountain Watch) and visiting
         Moorabella.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: The Galleria Deep
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 13
                  Adaptability = 13
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 48 Clan Points
              Aptitude +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 5000 Gil
        Leestone (x7)
        Quality Pelt

In this quest, your job is to survey six locations as designated by sparkling 
spots on the ground. There are some enemies here though, such as Zombies, 
Ahrimans, and a Black Chocobo. You should take care of the Ahriman enemies 
first, as they can Confuse your clan members. As for dealing with the 
Zombies, remember that they are undead, so in order to completely destroy 
them you must use Raise or some equivalent ability/item after you get them 
down to 0 HP. The Black Chocobo's Choco Flame is rather strong as well, so 
you may want to dispatch it quickly too. Once you survey all of the points, 
the quest ends.


=====================
E2-06: Survey No. 259
=====================

Description: Wanted: Researchers to assist with geological survey of Nazan
             Mines.
             Please survey the area assigned and report your findings.
             Transportation fees will be provided.
             -Jylland Geological Survey Committee
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Survey points of geological interest!
Forbidden: Summoning Scions
Rank: 33
Appears: After completing Quest D4-01 (Making Music) and Quest E2-05 (Survey
         No. 258), and visiting Moorabella.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Nazan Mines
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 22
                  Adaptability = 22
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 66 Clan Points
              Aptitude +2
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 5250 Gil
        Darklord Crystal (x5)
        Demon Feather (x3)

Here in the mines, you are sent to take a survey of the area, as designated 
by the six sparkling spots on the ground. You are also faced with Zombies, 
Bloody Orbs, a Ghoul, and a Plague here, though. It's not required that you 
fight them, but it will be in your best interest to take out at least the 
Plague due to its Roulette ability which can KO a random friend or foe 
currently in the battle, as well as its abilities which cause Slow or Disable 
status. Despite that, the rest of the enemies you face here are rather simple 
to get around and beat should you want to fight. Either way, it may be easier 
for you to just defeat everything here as you make your way to the survey 
spots. Once you complete your task, the quest is over.


=====================
E2-07: Survey No. 260
=====================

Description: Wanted: Researchers to assist with geological survey of the
             Neslowe Passage.
             Please survey the area assigned and report your findings.
             Transportation fees and hazard pay (x2) will be provided.
             -Jylland Geological Survey Committee
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Survey points of geological interest!
Forbidden: Opportunity Commands
Rank: 42
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request), Quest E2-06 (Survey No.
         259), Quest A2-10 (Odd Places) by examining the bottom-left well,
         and visiting any town.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Neslowe Passage
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 44
                  Adaptability = 44
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 84 Clan Points
              Aptitude +2

Reward: 10250 Gil
        Firebird Crystal

For this quest, you are sent to survey six geological points of interest, as 
designated by the sparkling spots on the ground. However, you are not alone 
and have to deal with a group of enemies (Master Monk, Cannoneer, Parivir, 
Trickster, Ninja, Seer). You don't have to defeat these guys, but you 
probably should since they can be rather tough and prove to be a nuisance if 
you left them alone. You will want to defeat the Master Monk early on due to 
his Lifebane ability (causes Doom), as well as the Seer with Magick Frenzy. 
Once you manage to investigate all six of the locations, your job here will 
be complete.


=====================
E2-08: Survey No. 261
=====================

Description: Wanted: Researchers to assist with geological survey of Zellea,
             the Forbidden Land.
             Please survey the area assigned and report your findings.
             Transportation fees and hazard pay (x3) will be provided.
             -Jylland Geological Survey Committee
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Survey points of geological interest!
Forbidden: Targeting Distant Units
Rank: 56
Appears: After completing Quest E2-07 (Survey No. 260), and completing the
         game and reloading complete game save data.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Zellea, the Forbidden Land
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 54
                  Adaptability = 54
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 99 Clan Points
              Aptitude +3
              Teamwork +3
              Adaptability +3
Reward: 15250 Gil
        Scarletite

Here, you have to once again survey the area by checking out six sparkling 
spots on the ground. What stands in your way this time are some of the game's 
strongest and most annoying enemies, including Tonberry Kings, Plagues, 
Malboro Kings, Behemoths, and Reavers. There is no point to really killing 
the enemies here, since if you defeat one, another random one will appear in 
its place. There is something unique about this area though; there are a few 
points which will turn purple; if you go to those locations and charge them 
up, you can use a mage cannon which will inflict a strong magickal attack on 
all of the enemies. Either way, once you investigate the six survey spots, 
your job here will be done.


=======================
E2-09: The Finest Blade
=======================

Description: You know the shelled beasts that walk this land with their long-
             forgotten foes' swords lodged in their backs? One such beast is
             the toughskin, and it is rare, for few blades can so much as
             scratch its reddish hide, said to be the hardest of all its ilk.
             And yet there are rumors that one has been spotted, and with
             sword! I would very much like to see such a sword. Bring it to
             me!
             -Metallurgist Steeling
Quest Type: Defeat Mark
Victory Circumstance: Defeat the blade biter!
Forbidden: Bludgeoning Weapons
Rank: 42
Appears: After completing Quest E5-01 (The Dig), Quest A2-10 (Odd Places), by
         examining the bottom-left well, and visiting any town.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: The Neslowe Passage
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 44
                  Adaptability = 44
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 84 Clan Points
              Teamwork +2
Reward: 7740 Gil
        Prime Tanned Hide

For this quest, you have to defeat the red Toughskin in the back area. 
However, in your way stands a Hoppy Bunny, two Rocktitans, and two Pit 
Beasts. You only have to defeat the Toughskin though, luckily. The Hoppy 
Bunny should be your first target due to its ability to cast Haste on the 
other enemies. The Rocktitans have Headbutt, which can Immobilize you, and 
the Pit Beasts use Sandstorm, which can hit multiple party members for a bit 
of damage. The Toughskin has Resonate, which is most devastating since it can 
Disable any of your units with bladed weapons. That will make it rough on you 
if you brought a lot of those type of melee attackers to the battle. Bring a 
magick-user to help you out here so you don't get disabled. It's not 
required, but it will help a lot if you defeat the other enemies en route to 
the Toughskin. Once you defeat your mark, the quest will be complete.

E2-11: Gimme That!
==================

Description: Nyeh heh heh heh!
             Know what I want? A darklord crystal!
             It's valuable, oh, it's valuable...but I'll pay the price! The
             drop off will go down in the Zedlei Forest. Nyeh heh heh! I'll
             be waiting!
             -Zedlei Consortium
Quest Type: Delivery
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Non-elemental Effects
Rank: 28

Location: Zedlei Forest
Days: 20

Required Talents: Negotiation = 20
Ability Points: 30

When you arrive at this location, the petitioner will take the crystal and 
try to pay you only 50 gil for it. Say that's not enough and you will enter 
battle. There will be a whole crowd of enemies here to face (Ice Flan, Yellow 
Jelly, Red Marshmallow, two Rangers, and a Berserker). To top it off, there 
are the usual traps laid about the area, so hopefully you're lucky enough not 
to trip them. The Flan enemies have their usual elemental magick attacks to 
hurt you and heal them. As for the Rangers and Berserker you face, they can 
lay traps and such, so you would want to eliminate them as well. Once you 
defeat everyone here, the battle ends and you win. The Berserker who tried to 
rip you off prior to the battle will pay out the actual reward, too.

E2-13: Plea for Help
====================

Description: We were digging a shaft in the Nazan Mines when it collapsed,
             trapping me and my friends in the darkness. Up until a few days
             ago I could hear my friends' voices, but now I hear only the
             cries of spirits. I'm placing this note in a bottle and casting
             it in one of the underground rivers that runs through the mine
             in the slim hope it will be found in time.
             -Rasgow, Nazan Miner
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Targeting an Area
Rank: 25
Appears: After completing Quest C3-11 (Rumors Abound).
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Nazan Mines
Days: 20
Recommended Job (Dispatch): White Monk
Required Talents: Teamwork = 18
                  Adaptability = 18
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 50 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
Reward: 4260 Gil
        Suspect Mushroom (x2)
        Cod Scale (x2)

Here, you are faced by five Ghosts and a Wraith in the middle. There are a 
few treasures you can collect in this area as well. Your main target is the 
group of ghosts, however. Their status effects can be quite a nuisance, so 
you may want to keep your distance and attack strongly when possible. As 
always when dealing with the undead, you need to use a Raise or Phoenix Down 
to totally defeat them at 0 HP. That said, it is necessary for you to have 
some allies with the Items command available. It also doesn't help that all 
these enemies can heal themselves with their abilities, so you will want to 
kill them all quickly if you can help it. Once you defeat them all, by 
quickly making them all into tombstones or actually exorcising them, the 
quest will be over.


===========================
E2-14: A Treasured Heirloom
===========================

Description: My most treasured family heirloom-a gil snapped shell-has broken
             clean in two! That shell has been handed down for generations as
             a charm to bring good fortune to our family business. That it's
             broken is an affront to my ancestors, and I fear it may bring
             ill luck on my trade.
             I seek someone to catch a gil snapper and replace the broken
             shell! Money's no object-I don't need gil, I need a gil snapper!
             -Maat, Dealer of Antiquities
Quest Type: Defeat Mark
Victory Circumstance: Defeat the gil snapper!
Forbidden: Fire, Ice, Lightning
Rank: 28
Appears: After completing Quest C3-16 (Sleepless Nights).
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Sant D'alsa Bluff
Days: 20
Required Talents: Teamwork = 20
                  Adaptability = 20
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 56 Clan Points
              Teamwork +1
Reward: 5170 Gil
        Spiral Vine (x3)

In this battle, you are to defeat an Adamantitan (gil snapper) in order to 
collect its shell. It is accompanied by two Banshees and Great Tortoises. The 
Banshees are most dangerous since they can use a Meteorite to cause lots of 
damage to one of your clan members. At this point in the game, you should be 
strong enough to quickly take out these enemies and head up the hill to where 
the Adamantitan is. It is a strong enemy, and its Rain of Stone attack will 
heal it and hurt multiple members of your party, so watch out. Once you 
defeat the mark, the quest is over.


======================
E2-15: Picnic Pleasure
======================

Description: Greetings! Bonga Bugle Head Editor here!
             This month, we're taking a look at haunted spots, starting with
             that most forbidding of places, Shadeholme!
             ...Um, someone go with me, please!
             Note: the actual location of our report will be top secret!
             -Head Editor, Bonga Bugle
Quest Type: Escort
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Fire, Ice, Lightning
Rank: 26
Appears: After completing Quest C3-11 (Rumors Abound).
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Nazan Mines
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 7
                  Teamwork = 7
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 52 Clan Points
              Aptitude +1
              Teamwork +1
Reward: 4800 Gil
        Storm Sigil (x3)

For this battle, you have to face a number of different monsters, including 
each color of Flan, two Headlesses, and a Grenade. What makes this fight a 
bit tough is the fact that many of the enemies rely on magick attacks not 
only to hurt you, but to heal themselves as well. Since the three main 
elements are banned from the battle, you should take advantage of long-range 
attacks from other jobs such as Fusiliers and Snipers, even certain abilities 
from Fighters are quite helpful. Your primary focus should be to kill the 
three colored Flans, as they can be the most dangerous in the mix, especially 
with the ability to cast Stop on your party members! Defeat everyone here and 
you will win, as usual.

====================

Description: I'm designing the fastest airship ever built, and I need to find
             a light, but strong metal to use for the gears, kupo. I believe

For this battle, you need to go against three Headless, two Deathscythes, and 
a Lamashtu. This can be a very difficult and dangerous battle, especially 
since the undead creatures and the Lamashtu have abilities which can cast 
Stop and Doom on your clan members. The Lamashtu has an ability called 
Eternal Sleep which has a chance of putting friend or foe to Sleep or Doom 
status. You will need to disable this monster as quickly as possible. Don't 
forget to fully destroy the undead enemies once you get them to 0 HP. After 
you clear the area of enemies, you will receive the well-earned victory.

E3-06: Meeting the Quota
========================

Description: I've always been weak-ill suited for physical labor. As my luck
             would have it, I was chosen to join an expedition to dig for
             licra ore. I really don't think I'm up to the task, and so I
             seek a group of hunters to go in my place.
             -Cain the Frail
Quest Type: Item Recovery
Victory Circumstance: Gather the licra ore!
Forbidden: Targeting an Area
Rank: 30
Appears: After completing Quest C3-11 (Rumors Abound).

Location: Nazan Mines

Clan Rewards: 60 Clan Points
              Aptitude +2
              Teamwork +2

In this quest, you have to face a bunch of Ghosts and Zombies, as well as a 
Ghoul, as you search for the licra ore. There are six locations where the ore 
is to be gathered from, as designated by the sparkling spots on the ground. 
The undead enemies can be annoying, especially with their abilities to drain 
your health and such. As you probably are aware by now, in order to fully 
defeat them at 0 HP, you must use Raise or something similar. You don't get 
any loot for defeating them, but their attacks and related status effects can 
be annoying, so you may want to try and defeat anything in your way. There 
are a few treasures you can pick up in this area, as well. Regardless, once 
you have recovered all of the ore, you are free to go.


=======================
E3-07: Wish Upon A Star
=======================

Description: This past night I saw another falling star in the direction of
             Sant D'alsa Bluff. There had been another the night before last,
             and the night before that, too! I can't rest with the sky
             falling down around me. All I want is a good night's sleep!

For this battle, your primary target is Entz the Alchemist. He is being 
surrounded by Zombies, Great Tortoises, and a Ghoul. The Great Tortoises are 
strong attackers, and the undead enemies can be a pain with their ability to 
Poison you and drain your health. The Alchemist is your main target, and he 
has the ability to rain meteors on your clan, causing lots of damage in the 
process. Ignore the undead and beat down on Entz when you get to him with 
your strong attacks, and he will be down in no time.

================

             of her victory? Someone save my beauty for me!
             -Bunbassa

Here, you are up against the kidnappers of the girl, consisting of a Blue 
Mage, Seer, Ninja, and Archer. The Seer is the weakest in the mix, so there's 
not much to worry about here. The Ninja can Confuse or Silence your allies, 
but luckily does not have Duel Wield, so you have that much less to worry

E3-12: Eternal Rivalry
======================

Description: My master suddenly left the dojo the other day, leaving behind a
             note that said he was off to fight his sworn enemy! I am worried
             for my master. Could someone go and see if he is all right?
             -Anis, Grant's Pupil
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: See the battle to its end!
Forbidden: Restoring HP
Rank: 99
Appears: After completing Quest A2-10 (Odd Places) by examining the upper-
         left well.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Sant D'alsa Bluff
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 22
                  Adaptability = 22
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 99 Clan Points
              Teamwork +5
              Adaptability +5
Reward: 6850 Gil
        Moon Ring (x5)

When you first arrive here, you may be expecting some crazy high-level fight. 
This is actually not the case; you are merely observing a battle between 
Grant, a Master Monk, and his enemy, a Paladin. All you can do is watch them 
do battle on the upper area of the map, while you simply move around. Do not 
interfere with their battle, though; you are only here to watch! Don't worry 
about the ground shaking and everyone taking damage from it, the battle won't 
last long enough for you to die from it. Once the battle ends, the quest is 
over.


================================
E3-13: Rancher's Request - Green
================================

Description: I'd like to have a green chocobo at my ranch to raise along with
             the others, but they're so fast, all of my own attempts to catch
             one have failed. Seek fleet-footed hunters to find and catch a
             green chocobo for me!
             -Yew, Chocobo Rancher

         (Rancher's Request - Black).

Location: Targ Wood
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 18
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 58 Clan Points
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 1750 Gil
        Gold Chalice (x3)

For this quest, you must bring the Chocobo Rancher a Green Chocobo. You are 
required to have a Chocobo Knight in order to carry this out, plus you need 
to already have captured the Chocobo prior to doing this quest. The best 
place to search is in Zedlei Forest around the month of Greenfire until the 
"Open Wide" encounter appears. Then, enter the battle and defeat all the 
other enemies except the Chocobo. Then, weaken the Chocobo to critical health 
and move your Chocobo Knight next to it. Mount it to capture, then bring it 
here to complete the quest.

defeat all the other enemies except the Chocobo. Then, weaken the Chocobo to 
critical health and move your Chocobo Knight next to it. Mount it to capture, 
then bring it here to complete the quest.

=======================
E4-01: Devilish Delight
=======================

Description: Never tasted the delicious tears of devils brought to a simmer
             by the scalding heat of fire and brimstone? Then you've never
             tasted Imp Stew, a sinfully tasty dish!
             It must be eaten while piping hot, or it loses its punch, so
             don't dawdle once you've ladled a bowl or three!
             -Grosso, Culinary Crusade
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes in 4 rounds!
Forbidden: Being Robbed
Rank: 42
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request), Quest D4-04 (Hors D'oeuvre
         of the Hour), Quest A2-10 (Odd Places) by examining the upper-middle
         well, and visiting any town.

Location: Goug
Days: 20
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Ninja
                            Assassin
Required Talents: Negotiation = 44
                  Adaptability = 44
Ability Points: 30

              Teamwork +2
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 6410 Gil
        Prime Tanned Hide
        Fiend's Blood

In this battle, you are up against a Master Monk, Berserker, Beastmaster, 
Thief, and two Fire Drakes. The catch is that you have to defeat everyone 
within four rounds. Generally speaking, the enemies are easy, with the only 
ones you'll have any difficult with being the Master Monk and possibly the 
Berserker with his high evasion. The Fire Drakes can heal each other with 
fire-based abilities, so you should try and kill them quickly before they can 
recover their lost health. Once you defeat all of the enemies within four 
rounds, the quest will be complete. You will receive some Fiend's Blood as an 
added reward for completing this quest, too.


===================
E4-02: Shelling Out
===================

Description: Fisherman's Tortoria is an old Graszton favorite of lightly
             seasoned turtle meat. Simple, and simply delicious! The trick to
             preparing this dish comes not in the kitchen but on the
             battlefield. Bring down the turtles with bladed weapons, and the
             entire dish tastes of metal, so best to avoid using them
             entirely. Are you up to the task?
             -Grosso, Culinary Crusade
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Uphold the law and defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Bladed Weapons
Rank: 50
Appears: After completing Quest E3-12 (Eternal Rivalry) and Quest E4-01
         (Devilish Delight).
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Graszton
Days: 20
Recommended Job (Dispatch): White Monk
                            Master Monk
Required Talents: Negotiation = 44
                  Adaptability = 44
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 99 Clan Points
              Aptitude +3
              Teamwork +3
Reward: 9230 Gil
        Emperor Scale
        Pink Tail

In this battle, you are up against two Great Tortoises, as well as a Lamia, 
two Rocktitans, and an Adamantitan. The Lamia has a powerful Twister attack; 
it has low accuracy, but if it hits, it can be brutal. The other enemies all 
have their Headbutt attacks, which can cause Immobilize status on your clan 
members. If you have a mage, their magick attacks will be useful, 
particularly Aero and other air-based attacks. Luckily, these enemies are 
somewhat slow, but they do have a lot of HP, so you need to be able to 
inflict a lot of damage in order to bring them down. If anyone is equipped 
with a bladed weapon, try to use other abilities that don't use them, or else 
you will fail the quest. Once you defeat all of the enemies without using 
blades, the quest will be a success; you will also receive a Pink Tail as an 
extra reward.


========================
E4-03: Flantastic Finish
========================

Description: Zedlei Flan, a specialty from the forest of the same name, is a
             delicate desert that melts in one's mouth, before melting one's
             heart. Only the freshest ingredients will do for this treat!
             -Grosso, Culinary Crusade
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Weaken the red flan and defeat all other foes!
Forbidden: Opportunity Commands
Rank: 50
Appears: After completing Quest E5-06 (Through Another's Eyes), Quest E4-02
         (Shelling Out), and visiting any town.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Zedlei Forest
Days: 20
Recommended Job (Dispatch): Arcanist
Required Talents: Negotiation = 47
                  Adaptability = 47
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 99 Clan Points
              Teamwork +3
              Adaptability +3
Reward: 7810 Gil
        Fiend's Blood
        Sweet Sap

In this battle for collecting ingredients, you not only go up against the Red 
Marshmallow, but also the Deadly Nightshade, Hoppy Bunny, Lilith, Werewolf, 
and a White Chocobo (good opportunity for a Chocobo Knight). The Hoppy Bunny 
is the most annoying since it can cast Haste on the other enemies. The Lilith 
can also Doom/Charm your clan members with its Kiss, and the Werewolf can 
Immobilize you with its Assault attack. It would be important to eliminate 
the Hoppy Bunny as quickly as you can, followed by the Lilith, so that their 
status effects can't hinder the match any further. Make sure you defeat all 
the other enemies first before going for the Red Marshmallow. All you have to 
do is weaken it to critical health and the quest will be completed. You also 
receive some Sweet Sap as an added reward here.


============================
E4-04: The Art of Gastronomy
============================

Description: A connoisseur of fine cuisine is always in search of the next
             great meal. I am happy to tell you that meal is here, my
             friends! If you think you have what it takes to appreciate the
             finest of gastronomical delights, meet me in Aisenfield!
             -Grosso, Culinary Crusade
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Actions by Humes
Rank: 47
Appears: After completing Quest E5-11 (Pirate Problems), Quest E4-03
         (Flantastic Finish), and visiting any town.
Price: 500 Gil
Location: Aisenfield
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 51
                  Adaptability = 51
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 94 Clan Points
              Adaptability +2
Reward: 10700 Gil
        Spider Silk
        Tanned Beast Hide

When you arrive here, you will get to meet Grosso face to face, who tells you 
to wait for the meal to arrive. It turns out that the meal does arrive, and 
knocks him off into the distance. That leaves your clan to do battle with 
four Behemoths and a Reaver. They are all very strong physical attackers who 
can lower your defense and raise their own attack power, so bring your own 
strong attackers and magick-users into the battle to counter that. The 
Behemoths are weak against ice-based attacks, so if you have a mage, they 
will fit in very well here. You really need someone who can cure your allies 
as well, since they will take quite a beating from the Behemoths. Concentrate 
on taking out one enemy at a time; it will make things much easier. Once you 
defeat them all, you will receive a Tanned Beast Hide as an added reward, and 
the quest will finally be complete.


==========================
E4-05: The Honorable Thing
==========================

Description: Ah, the sweet lips of my love. My one pleasure in this life. But
             the vile Balfonne has stolen a kiss from my darling Preme, and
             with it, her love. I could not let such a slight go unanswered!
             I immediately challenged Balfonne to a duel to settle this point
             of honor, but sadly, urgent matters prevent me from dealing with

             -Hseaunon, Preme's True Love

        Putrid Liquid (x2)

Here, you will find yourself battling another clan hired to go to the duel 
for Balfonne, go figure. Your opposition consists of a Parivir, Defender, 
Hunter, Cannoneer, and White Mage. Of course, the Parivir is most dangerous 
due to his abilities to inflict Slow and Immobilize on your party. The White 
Mage is another enemy that needs to go quickly so she doesn't heal them 
constantly. The rest of the enemies here are not particularly noteworth as 
they attack from a distance, and can be dispatched quite easily from close 
range. Once you defeat them all, the battle will be over.

======================
E4-07: Training Wanted
======================

Description: Those parivir we hired to watch over our town were nothing but
             trouble, kupo. But we learned our lesson. If we want something
             done right, we have to do it ourselves!
             We've formed a town watch to protect the city, but what we have
             in determination we lack in experience. We need someone to help
             us harden up, kupo!
             -Zupp, Commander of the Goug Watch
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!

        Mysidia Alloy

In this battle, you are fighting the new Goug Watch in a training battle of 
sorts, but they can still be tough! You have to fight against a Tinker, 
Thief, Black Mage, Fusilier, Moogle Knight, and an Animist. You need to take 
this battle seriously like always since they aren't going to take it easy on 
you even if they are just learning. You will want to take care of the Tinker 
on the right side quickly, since he can cause status effects on everyone in 
the area. The rest of these guys don't have any special abilities to be too 
worried about. Defeat them, and the quest for their training will be over.


====================
E4-08: Wall of Flame
====================

Description: Bombs have been streamling out of the crater on Firewyrm Mount.
             We're in the process of forming a brigade of mages to deal with
             the threat, but we need more time. Hold back the bombs for us
             until we've finished our preparations!
             -Jank, Goug Firehouse
Quest Type: Satisfy Petitioner
Victory Circumstance: Endure the enemy's attack for 3 rounds!
Forbidden: Ice
Rank: 29
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request), Quest A2-10 (Odd Places)
         by examining the upper-middle well, and visiting any town.
Price: 400 Gil
Location: Goug
Days: 20
Required Talents: Negotiation = 44
                  Adaptability = 44
Ability Points: 30
Clan Rewards: 58 Clan Points
              Aptitude +1
              Teamwork +1
              Adaptability +1
Reward: 4270 Gil
        Gold Chalice

For this quest, you will find yourself dealing with a lot of Bombs. You don't 
necessarily have to defeat them all, but you must survive their attacks for 
three whole rounds of combat. They tend to heal themselves with fire-based 
attacks, all while attacking you with the same abilities. Be careful if you 
get a Bomb to critical health, as it will self-destruct, causing lots of 
damage. There is basically an endless supply of Bombs, where if you defeat 
one, another will appear instantly. If you have someone who can cure your 
party, you will be in great shape here. Once the third round ends, you are 
free to go.

============================
E4-10: Watching the Watchers
============================

Description: We hired a group of parivir to protect our precious city from
             outside attacks, but those very parivir have started wreaking
             havoc -inside- the city, kupo! We need a group of hunters to
             come and take care of the troublemakers.
             -Zupp, Goug Youth Alliance
Quest Type: Battle
Victory Circumstance: Defeat all foes!
Forbidden: Piercing Weapons
Rank: 38
Appears: After completing Quest D4-16 (A Request) and visiting any town.
